        triggers = ["council", "debate", "evaluate"]
        negations = ["don't", "dont", "do not", "never", "without", "skip", "stop"]
        
        if not any(kw in text_lower for kw in triggers):
            return False
            
        for neg in negations:
            if neg in text_lower:
                for kw in triggers:
                    if kw in text_lower and text_lower.find(neg) < text_lower.find(kw):
                        return False
        return True

    def process_text_input(self):
        """Extracts the manual string from the entry box and boots the computing pipeline."""
        query = self.entry_field.get().strip()
        if not query:
            return
            
        self.entry_field.delete(0, tk.END) # Clear command slot
        
        if query.lower() in ["exit", "quit"]:
            self.set_status("🚪 DETACHING CLIENT NODE... GOODBYE", "#ff3333")
            self.append_log(f"\n📝 Command captured: \"{query}\"\n", "sys")
            threading.Thread(target=lambda: [speak_text("Systems shutting down. Goodbye, Aryan."), self.root.quit()], daemon=True).start()
            return

        # Hand transaction execution over to the background processing engine thread
        threading.Thread(target=self.execute_pipeline, args=(query, "Typed Input"), daemon=True).start()

    def trigger_voice_thread(self):
        """Fires off an independent worker thread to poll mic data without freezing the window UI."""
        threading.Thread(target=self.execute_voice_capture, daemon=True).start()

    def execute_voice_capture(self):
        """Controls audio capturing state mechanics cleanly."""
        self.set_status("🎙️ LISTENING TO AMBIENT MIC WAVEFORM...", "#ffcc00")
        self.append_log("\n🎙️ [Microphone Channel Open: Speak now]\n", "sys")
        
        spoken_text = listen_to_user()
        if not spoken_text:
            self.set_status("⚡ SYSTEM STATUS: READY", "#00ffcc")
            self.append_log("⚠️ [No vocal input data recognized. Loop aborted.]\n", "err")
            return
            
        self.execute_pipeline(spoken_text, "Vocal Stream")

    def execute_pipeline(self, command, source_type):
        """Main computational pipeline. Routes data streams and manages model generation."""
        self.append_log(f"\n👤 USER ({source_type}): \"{command}\"\n", "user")
        
        # ROUTE MATRIX PATHWAY A: COUNCIL EXECUTION
        if self.should_trigger_council(command):
            self.set_status("👥 COUNCIL ASSEMBLED: AGENTS GENERATING DATA...", "#ffcc00")
            self.append_log("⏳ Calling Council Boardroom Nodes (Contrarian -> Synergist -> Chairman)...\n", "sys")
            
            debate_packet = run_council_debate(command)
            
            # Print complete strategic packet layout to screen
            self.append_log(f"\n🎭 [THE CONTRARIAN OUTLOOK]:\n{debate_packet['contrarian']}\n", "ace")
            speak_text("Analyzing the risk layout from the contrarian.")
            speak_text(debate_packet['contrarian'])
            
            self.append_log(f"\n🚀 [THE SYNERGIST SOLUTION]:\n{debate_packet['synergist']}\n", "ace")
            speak_text("Reviewing the strategy modification from the synergist.")
            speak_text(debate_packet['synergist'])
            
            self.append_log(f"\n🏛️ [CHAIRMAN SUMMARY & EVALUATION]:\n{debate_packet['chairman']}\n", "sys")
            speak_text("The chairman's final evaluation and takeaways.")
            speak_text(debate_packet['chairman'])

        # ROUTE MATRIX PATHWAY B: STANDARD CHAT ROTATION
        else:
            text_lower = command.lower()
            if "think deeply" in text_lower or "smart mode" in text_lower or "analyze" in text_lower:
                active_model = SMART_MODEL
                self.set_status(f"🧠 RUNNING HEAVY LOGIC LAYER ({active_model})...", "#ffcc00")
                self.append_log(f"🧠 Routing to High-Capacity Logic Engine ({active_model})...\n", "sys")
            else:
                active_model = FAST_MODEL
                self.set_status(f"⚡ RUNNING OPTIMAL SPEED LAYER ({active_model})...", "#00ffcc")
                self.append_log(f"⚡ Routing to Low-Latency Speed Engine ({active_model})...\n", "sys")

            try:
                response = ollama.chat(
                    model=active_model,
                    messages=[
                        {"role": "system", "content": "You are Ace, an elite, highly intelligent desktop GUI AI assistant customized for Aryan."},
                        {"role": "user", "content": command}
                    ]
                )
                reply = response['message']['content']
                self.append_log(f"🤖 ACE: {reply}\n", "ace")
                speak_text(reply)
            except Exception as e:
                self.append_log(f"❌ Core link drop exception: {e}\n", "err")

        self.set_status("⚡ SYSTEM STATUS: READY", "#00ffcc")

# --------------------------------------------------
# APPLICATION RUNNER GATEWAY
# --------------------------------------------------
if __name__ == "__main__":
    app_root = tk.Tk()
    app_instance = AceGUIApp(app_root)
    app_root.mainloop()


----------------------------------------------------------------------------


import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import scrolledtext
import threading
import sys
import os
import time
import ollama

# Import your locked, functional modules
from audio_provider import speak_text, listen_to_user
from council import run_council_debate

# 🤖 THE HYBRID ENGINE DECK
FAST_MODEL = "llama3.2:1b"
SMART_MODEL = "qwen2.5-coder:latest"

class AceGUIApp:
    def __init__(self, root):
        self.root = root
        self.root.title("ACE: Autonomous Console Engine")
        self.root.geometry("700x550")
        self.root.configure(bg="#121212") # Futuristic Dark Theme Base

        # --------------------------------------------------
        # 🎨 CYBERPUNK HUD INTERFACE LAYOUT
        # --------------------------------------------------
        # Top Status Indicator Bar
        self.status_label = tk.Label(root, text="⚡ SYSTEM STATUS: ONLINE [HYBRID PROTOCOL ACTIVE]", 
                                     font=("Consolas", 10, "bold"), bg="#1a1a1a", fg="#00ffcc", anchor="w", pady=5)
        self.status_label.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=10, pady=(10, 5))

        # Core Console Readout Display Log
        self.log_display = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(root, wrap=tk.WORD, font=("Consolas", 11), 
                                                     bg="#1e1e1e", fg="#ffffff", insertbackground="#00ffcc")
        self.log_display.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, padx=10, pady=5)
        
        # Configure unique colored tagging text streams (Fixed the strict aliases here!)
        self.log_display.tag_config("sys", foreground="#00ffcc")   # Neon Teal System Alert
        self.log_display.tag_config("user", foreground="#ffcc00")  # Amber User Output
        self.log_display.tag_config("ace", foreground="#ffffff")   # Clean White Response
        self.log_display.tag_config("err", foreground="#ff3333")   # Crimson Pipeline Failure

        # Bottom Input Dock Framework
        self.input_frame = tk.Frame(root, bg="#121212")
        self.input_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=10, pady=10)

        # Manual Entry Field
        self.entry_field = tk.Entry(self.input_frame, font=("Consolas", 12), bg="#1e1e1e", fg="#ffffff", 
                                    insertbackground="#00ffcc", borderwidth=1, relief=tk.SOLID)
        self.entry_field.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.X, expand=True, ipady=4)
        self.entry_field.bind("<Return>", lambda event: self.process_text_input())

        # Operation Action Buttons
        self.send_btn = tk.Button(self.input_frame, text="SEND", font=("Consolas", 10, "bold"), 
                                  bg="#00ffcc", fg="#121212", activebackground="#00cc99", 
                                  command=self.process_text_input, width=8, relief=tk.FLAT)
        self.send_btn.pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)

        self.mic_btn = tk.Button(self.input_frame, text="🎙️ MIC", font=("Consolas", 10, "bold"), 
                                 bg="#ffcc00", fg="#121212", activebackground="#cc9900", 
                                 command=self.trigger_voice_thread, width=8, relief=tk.FLAT)
        self.mic_btn.pack(side=tk.LEFT)

        # Print initial boot diagnostics to the log display window
        self.append_log("🚀 Ace Protocol Initialized. Standby for input connection...\n", "sys")
        
        # Run standard startup greeting voice inside a safe non-blocking background thread
        threading.Thread(target=lambda: speak_text("System active, Aryan. Standing by."), daemon=True).start()

    # --------------------------------------------------
    # 🧠 CORE ENGINE INTELLIGENCE MATRIX
    # --------------------------------------------------
    def append_log(self, text, tag):
        """Appends formatted messages to the GUI display log safely."""
        self.log_display.insert(tk.END, text, tag)
        self.log_display.see(tk.END) # Auto-scroll down to the latest text token

    def set_status(self, text, color="#00ffcc"):
        """Dynamically switches the text color and readout message of the top HUD bar."""
        self.status_label.config(text=text, fg=color)

    def should_trigger_council(self, text):
        """Checks for council trigger keywords while respecting intent negation modifiers."""
        text_lower = text.lower()
        triggers = ["council", "debate", "evaluate"]
        negations = ["don't", "dont", "do not", "never", "without", "skip", "stop"]
        
        if not any(kw in text_lower for kw in triggers):
            return False
            
        for neg in negations:
            if neg in text_lower:
                for kw in triggers:
                    if kw in text_lower and text_lower.find(neg) < text_lower.find(kw):
                        return False
        return True

    def process_text_input(self):
        """Extracts the manual string from the entry box and boots the computing pipeline."""
        query = self.entry_field.get().strip()
        if not query:
            return
            
        self.entry_field.delete(0, tk.END) # Clear command slot
        
        if query.lower() in ["exit", "quit"]:
            self.set_status("🚪 DETACHING CLIENT NODE... GOODBYE", "#ff3333")
            self.append_log(f"\n📝 Command captured: \"{query}\"\n", "sys")
            threading.Thread(target=lambda: [speak_text("Systems shutting down. Goodbye, Aryan."), self.root.quit()], daemon=True).start()
            return

        # Hand transaction execution over to the background processing engine thread
        threading.Thread(target=self.execute_pipeline, args=(query, "Typed Input"), daemon=True).start()

    def trigger_voice_thread(self):
        """Fires off an independent worker thread to poll mic data without freezing the window UI."""
        threading.Thread(target=self.execute_voice_capture, daemon=True).start()

    def execute_voice_capture(self):
        """Controls audio capturing state mechanics cleanly."""
        self.set_status("🎙️ LISTENING TO AMBIENT MIC WAVEFORM...", "#ffcc00")
        self.append_log("\n🎙️ [Microphone Channel Open: Speak now]\n", "sys")
        
        spoken_text = listen_to_user()
        if not spoken_text:
            self.set_status("⚡ SYSTEM STATUS: READY", "#00ffcc")
            self.append_log("⚠️ [No vocal input data recognized. Loop aborted.]\n", "err")
            return
            
        self.execute_pipeline(spoken_text, "Vocal Stream")

    def execute_pipeline(self, command, source_type):
        """Main computational pipeline. Routes data streams and manages model generation."""
        self.append_log(f"\n👤 USER ({source_type}): \"{command}\"\n", "user")
        
        # ROUTE MATRIX PATHWAY A: COUNCIL EXECUTION
        if self.should_trigger_council(command):
            self.set_status("👥 COUNCIL ASSEMBLED: AGENTS GENERATING DATA...", "#ffcc00")
            self.append_log("⏳ Calling Council Boardroom Nodes (Contrarian -> Synergist -> Chairman)...\n", "sys")
            
            debate_packet = run_council_debate(command)
            
            # Print complete strategic packet layout to screen
            self.append_log(f"\n🎭 [THE CONTRARIAN OUTLOOK]:\n{debate_packet['contrarian']}\n", "ace")
            speak_text("Analyzing the risk layout from the contrarian.")
            speak_text(debate_packet['contrarian'])
            
            self.append_log(f"\n🚀 [THE SYNERGIST SOLUTION]:\n{debate_packet['synergist']}\n", "ace")
            speak_text("Reviewing the strategy modification from the synergist.")
            speak_text(debate_packet['synergist'])
            
            self.append_log(f"\n🏛️ [CHAIRMAN SUMMARY & EVALUATION]:\n{debate_packet['chairman']}\n", "sys")
            speak_text("The chairman's final evaluation and takeaways.")
            speak_text(debate_packet['chairman'])

        # ROUTE MATRIX PATHWAY B: STANDARD CHAT ROTATION
        else:
            text_lower = command.lower()
            if "think deeply" in text_lower or "smart mode" in text_lower or "analyze" in text_lower:
                active_model = SMART_MODEL
                self.set_status(f"🧠 RUNNING HEAVY LOGIC LAYER ({active_model})...", "#ffcc00")
                self.append_log(f"🧠 Routing to High-Capacity Logic Engine ({active_model})...\n", "sys")
            else:
                active_model = FAST_MODEL
                self.set_status(f"⚡ RUNNING OPTIMAL SPEED LAYER ({active_model})...", "#00ffcc")
                self.append_log(f"⚡ Routing to Low-Latency Speed Engine ({active_model})...\n", "sys")

            try:
                response = ollama.chat(
                    model=active_model,
                    messages=[
                        {"role": "system", "content": "You are Ace, an elite, highly intelligent desktop GUI AI assistant customized for Aryan."},
                        {"role": "user", "content": command}
                    ]
                )
                reply = response['message']['content']
                self.append_log(f"🤖 ACE: {reply}\n", "ace")
                speak_text(reply)
            except Exception as e:
                self.append_log(f"❌ Core link drop exception: {e}\n", "err")

        self.set_status("⚡ SYSTEM STATUS: READY", "#00ffcc")

    app_root.mainloop()

        self.entry_field.bind("<Return>", lambda event: self.process_text_input())

        # Operation Action Buttons
        self.send_btn = tk.Button(self.input_frame, text="SEND", font=("Consolas", 10, "bold"), 
                                  bg="#00ffcc", fg="#121212", activebackground="#00cc99", 
                                  command=self.process_text_input, width=8, relief=tk.FLAT)
        self.send_btn.pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)

        self.mic_btn = tk.Button(self.input_frame, text="🎙️ MIC", font=("Consolas", 10, "bold"), 
                                 bg="#ffcc00", fg="#121212", activebackground="#cc9900", 
                                 command=self.trigger_voice_thread, width=8, relief=tk.FLAT)
        self.mic_btn.pack(side=tk.LEFT)

        # Print initial boot diagnostics to the log display window
        self.append_log("🚀 Ace Protocol Initialized. Standby for input connection...\n", "sys")
        
        # Run standard startup greeting voice inside a safe non-blocking background thread
        threading.Thread(target=lambda: speak_text("System active, Aryan. Standing by."), daemon=True).start()

    # --------------------------------------------------
    # 🧠 CORE ENGINE INTELLIGENCE MATRIX
    # --------------------------------------------------
    def append_log(self, text, tag):
        """Appends formatted messages to the GUI display log safely."""
        self.log_display.insert(tk.END, text, tag)
        self.log_display.see(tk.END) # Auto-scroll down to the latest text token

    def set_status(self, text, color="#00ffcc"):
        """Dynamically switches the text color and readout message of the top HUD bar."""
        self.status_label.config(text=text, fg=color)

    def should_trigger_council(self, text):
        """Checks for council trigger keywords while respecting intent negation modifiers."""
        text_lower = text.lower()
        triggers = ["council", "debate", "evaluate"]
        negations = ["don't", "dont", "do not", "never", "without", "skip", "stop"]
        
        if not any(kw in text_lower for kw in triggers):
            return False
            
        for neg in negations:
            if neg in text_lower:
                for kw in triggers:
                    if kw in text_lower and text_lower.find(neg) < text_lower.find(kw):
                        return False
        return True

    def process_text_input(self):
        """Extracts the manual string from the entry box and boots the computing pipeline."""
        query = self.entry_field.get().strip()
        if not query:
            return
            
        self.entry_field.delete(0, tk.END) # Clear command slot
        
        if query.lower() in ["exit", "quit"]:
            self.set_status("🚪 DETACHING CLIENT NODE... GOODBYE", "#ff3333")
            self.append_log(f"\n📝 Command captured: \"{query}\"\n", "sys")
            threading.Thread(target=lambda: [speak_text("Systems shutting down. Goodbye, Aryan."), self.root.quit()], daemon=True).start()
            return

        # Hand transaction execution over to the background processing engine thread
        threading.Thread(target=self.execute_pipeline, args=(query, "Typed Input"), daemon=True).start()

    def trigger_voice_thread(self):
        """Fires off an independent worker thread to poll mic data without freezing the window UI."""
        threading.Thread(target=self.execute_voice_capture, daemon=True).start()

    def execute_voice_capture(self):
        """Controls audio capturing state mechanics cleanly."""
        self.set_status("🎙️ LISTENING TO AMBIENT MIC WAVEFORM...", "#ffcc00")
        self.append_log("\n🎙️ [Microphone Channel Open: Speak now]\n", "sys")
        
        spoken_text = listen_to_user()
        if not spoken_text:
            self.set_status("⚡ SYSTEM STATUS: READY", "#00ffcc")
            self.append_log("⚠️ [No vocal input data recognized. Loop aborted.]\n", "err")
            return
            
        self.execute_pipeline(spoken_text, "Vocal Stream")

    def execute_pipeline(self, command, source_type):
        """Main computational pipeline. Routes data streams and manages model generation."""
        # Print personalized output label
        self.append_log(f"\n👤 ARYAN ({source_type}): \"{command}\"\n", "aryan")
        
        # ROUTE MATRIX PATHWAY A: COUNCIL EXECUTION
        if self.should_trigger_council(command):
            self.set_status("👥 COUNCIL ASSEMBLED: AGENTS GENERATING DATA...", "#ffcc00")
            self.append_log("⏳ Calling Council Boardroom Nodes (Contrarian -> Synergist -> Chairman)...\n", "sys")
            
            debate_packet = run_council_debate(command)
            
            # Print complete strategic packet layout to screen
            self.append_log(f"\n🎭 [THE CONTRARIAN OUTLOOK]:\n{debate_packet['contrarian']}\n", "ace")
            speak_text("Analyzing the risk layout from the contrarian.")
            speak_text(debate_packet['contrarian'])
            
            self.append_log(f"\n🚀 [THE SYNERGIST SOLUTION]:\n{debate_packet['synergist']}\n", "ace")
            speak_text("Reviewing the strategy modification from the synergist.")
            speak_text(debate_packet['synergist'])
            
            self.append_log(f"\n🏛️ [CHAIRMAN SUMMARY & EVALUATION]:\n{debate_packet['chairman']}\n", "sys")
            speak_text("The chairman's final evaluation and takeaways.")
            speak_text(debate_packet['chairman'])

        # ROUTE MATRIX PATHWAY B: STANDARD CHAT ROTATION
        else:
            text_lower = command.lower()
            if "think deeply" in text_lower or "smart mode" in text_lower or "analyze" in text_lower:
                active_model = SMART_MODEL
                self.set_status(f"🧠 RUNNING HEAVY LOGIC LAYER ({active_model})...", "#ffcc00")
                self.append_log(f"🧠 Routing to High-Capacity Logic Engine ({active_model})...\n", "sys")
            else:
                active_model = FAST_MODEL
                self.set_status(f"⚡ RUNNING OPTIMAL SPEED LAYER ({active_model})...", "#00ffcc")
                self.append_log(f"⚡ Routing to Low-Latency Speed Engine ({active_model})...\n", "sys")

            try:
                response = ollama.chat(
                    model=active_model,
                    messages=[
                        {"role": "system", "content": "You are Ace, an elite, highly intelligent desktop GUI AI assistant customized for Aryan."},
                        {"role": "user", "content": command}
                    ]
                )
                reply = response['message']['content']
                self.append_log(f"🤖 ACE: {reply}\n", "ace")
                speak_text(reply)
            except Exception as e:
                self.append_log(f"❌ Core link drop exception: {e}\n", "err")

        self.set_status("⚡ SYSTEM STATUS: READY", "#00ffcc")

# --------------------------------------------------
# APPLICATION RUNNER GATEWAY
# --------------------------------------------------
if __name__ == "__main__":
    app_root = tk.Tk()
    app_instance = AceGUIApp(app_root)
    app_root.mainloop()


---------------------------------------------------------------------------


import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import scrolledtext
import threading
import sys
import os
import time
import ollama

# Import your locked, functional modules
from audio_provider import speak_text, listen_to_user
from council import run_council_debate

# 🤖 THE HYBRID ENGINE DECK
FAST_MODEL = "llama3.2:1b"
SMART_MODEL = "qwen2.5-coder:latest"

class AceGUIApp:
    def __init__(self, root):
        self.root = root
        self.root.title("ACE: Autonomous Console Engine // [ARYAN.H.O.PROTOCOL.O]")
        self.root.geometry("700x550")
        self.root.configure(bg="#121212") # Futuristic Dark Theme Base

        # --------------------------------------------------
        # 🎨 Sophisticated HUD INTERFACE LAYOUT
        # --------------------------------------------------
        # Top Status Indicator Bar (PERSONALIZED)
        self.status_label = tk.Label(root, text="⚡ SYSTEM STATUS: ONLINE [ARYAN.H.O.HYBRID.DECK]", 
                                     font=("Consolas", 10, "bold"), bg="#1a1a1a", fg="#00ffcc", anchor="w", pady=5)
        self.status_label.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=10, pady=(10, 5))

        # Core Console Readout Display Log
        self.log_display = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(root, wrap=tk.WORD, font=("Consolas", 11), 
                                                     bg="#1e1e1e", fg="#ffffff", insertbackground="#00ffcc")
        self.log_display.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, padx=10, pady=5)
        
        # Configure unique colored tagging text streams
        self.log_display.tag_config("sys", foreground="#00ffcc")   # Neon Teal System Alert
        self.log_display.tag_config("aryan", foreground="#ffcc00") # Amber Aryan Output (PERSONALIZED)
        self.log_display.tag_config("ace", foreground="#ffffff")   # Clean White Response
        self.log_display.tag_config("err", foreground="#ff3333")   # Crimson Pipeline Failure

        # Bottom Input Dock Framework
        self.input_frame = tk.Frame(root, bg="#121212")
        self.input_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=10, pady=10)

        # Manual Entry Field
        self.entry_field = tk.Entry(self.input_frame, font=("Consolas", 12), bg="#1e1e1e", fg="#ffffff", 
                                    insertbackground="#00ffcc", borderwidth=1, relief=tk.SOLID)
        self.entry_field.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.X, expand=True, ipady=4)
        self.entry_field.bind("<Return>", lambda event: self.process_text_input())

        # Operation Action Buttons
        self.send_btn = tk.Button(self.input_frame, text="SEND", font=("Consolas", 10, "bold"), 
                                  bg="#00ffcc", fg="#121212", activebackground="#00cc99", 
                                  command=self.process_text_input, width=8, relief=tk.FLAT)
        self.send_btn.pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)

        self.mic_btn = tk.Button(self.input_frame, text="🎙️ MIC", font=("Consolas", 10, "bold"), 
                                 bg="#ffcc00", fg="#121212", activebackground="#cc9900", 
                                 command=self.trigger_voice_thread, width=8, relief=tk.FLAT)
        self.mic_btn.pack(side=tk.LEFT)

        # Print initial boot diagnostics to the log display window
        self.append_log("🚀 Ace Protocol Initialized. Standby for input connection...\n", "sys")
        
        # Run standard startup greeting voice inside a safe non-blocking background thread
        threading.Thread(target=lambda: speak_text("System active, Aryan. Standing by."), daemon=True).start()

    # --------------------------------------------------
    # 🧠 CORE ENGINE INTELLIGENCE MATRIX
    # --------------------------------------------------
    def append_log(self, text, tag):
        """Appends formatted messages to the GUI display log safely."""
        self.log_display.insert(tk.END, text, tag)
        self.log_display.see(tk.END) # Auto-scroll down to the latest text token

    def set_status(self, text, color="#00ffcc"):

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import scrolledtext
import threading
import sys
import os
import time
import ollama

# Import your locked, functional modules
from audio_provider import speak_text, listen_to_user
from council import run_council_debate

# 🤖 THE HYBRID ENGINE DECK
FAST_MODEL = "llama3.2:1b"
SMART_MODEL = "qwen2.5-coder:latest"

class AceGUIApp:
    def __init__(self, root):
        self.root = root
        self.root.title("ACE: Autonomous Console Engine // [ARYAN.H.O.PROTOCOL.O]")
        self.root.geometry("700x550")
        self.root.configure(bg="#121212") # Futuristic Dark Theme Base

        # 🧠 ACTIVE SHORT-TERM MEMORY BUFFER
        # Stores conversation turns to prevent amnesia
        self.chat_history = []

        # --------------------------------------------------
        # 🎨 Sophisticated HUD INTERFACE LAYOUT
        # --------------------------------------------------
        # Top Status Indicator Bar
        self.status_label = tk.Label(root, text="⚡ SYSTEM STATUS: ONLINE [ARYAN.H.O.HYBRID.DECK]", 
                                     font=("Consolas", 10, "bold"), bg="#1a1a1a", fg="#00ffcc", anchor="w", pady=5)
        self.status_label.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=10, pady=(10, 5))

        # Core Console Readout Display Log
        self.log_display = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(root, wrap=tk.WORD, font=("Consolas", 11), 
                                                     bg="#1e1e1e", fg="#ffffff", insertbackground="#00ffcc")
        self.log_display.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, padx=10, pady=5)
        
        # Configure unique colored tagging text streams
        self.log_display.tag_config("sys", foreground="#00ffcc")   # Neon Teal System Alert
        self.log_display.tag_config("aryan", foreground="#ffcc00") # Amber Aryan Output
        self.log_display.tag_config("ace", foreground="#ffffff")   # Clean White Response
        self.log_display.tag_config("err", foreground="#ff3333")   # Crimson Pipeline Failure

        # Bottom Input Dock Framework
        self.input_frame = tk.Frame(root, bg="#121212")
        self.input_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=10, pady=10)

        # Manual Entry Field
        self.entry_field = tk.Entry(self.input_frame, font=("Consolas", 12), bg="#1e1e1e", fg="#ffffff", 
                                    insertbackground="#00ffcc", borderwidth=1, relief=tk.SOLID)
        self.entry_field.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.X, expand=True, ipady=4)
        self.entry_field.bind("<Return>", lambda event: self.process_text_input())

        # Operation Action Buttons
        self.send_btn = tk.Button(self.input_frame, text="SEND", font=("Consolas", 10, "bold"), 
                                  bg="#00ffcc", fg="#121212", activebackground="#00cc99", 
                                  command=self.process_text_input, width=8, relief=tk.FLAT)
        self.send_btn.pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)

        self.mic_btn = tk.Button(self.input_frame, text="🎙️ MIC", font=("Consolas", 10, "bold"), 
                                 bg="#ffcc00", fg="#121212", activebackground="#cc9900", 
                                 command=self.trigger_voice_thread, width=8, relief=tk.FLAT)
        self.mic_btn.pack(side=tk.LEFT)

        # Print initial boot diagnostics to the log display window
        self.append_log("🚀 Ace Protocol Initialized. Standby for input connection...\n", "sys")
        
        # Run standard startup greeting voice inside a safe non-blocking background thread
        threading.Thread(target=lambda: speak_text("System active, Aryan. Standing by."), daemon=True).start()

    # --------------------------------------------------
    # 🧠 CORE ENGINE INTELLIGENCE MATRIX
    # --------------------------------------------------
    def append_log(self, text, tag):
        """Appends formatted messages to the GUI display log safely."""
        self.log_display.insert(tk.END, text, tag)
        self.log_display.see(tk.END)

    def set_status(self, text, color="#00ffcc"):
        """Dynamically switches the text color and readout message of the top HUD bar."""
        self.status_label.config(text=text, fg=color)

    def should_trigger_council(self, text):
        """Checks for council trigger keywords while respecting intent negation modifiers."""
        text_lower = text.lower()
        triggers = ["council", "debate", "evaluate"]
        negations = ["don't", "dont", "do not", "never", "without", "skip", "stop"]
        
        if not any(kw in text_lower for kw in triggers):
            return False
            
        for neg in negations:
            if neg in text_lower:
                for kw in triggers:
                    if kw in text_lower and text_lower.find(neg) < text_lower.find(kw):
                        return False
        return True

    def process_text_input(self):
        """Extracts the manual string from the entry box and boots the computing pipeline."""
        query = self.entry_field.get().strip()
        if not query:
            return
            
        self.entry_field.delete(0, tk.END)
        
        if query.lower() in ["exit", "quit"]:
            self.set_status("🚪 DETACHING CLIENT NODE... GOODBYE", "#ff3333")
            self.append_log(f"\n📝 Command captured: \"{query}\"\n", "sys")
            threading.Thread(target=lambda: [speak_text("Systems shutting down. Goodbye, Aryan."), self.root.quit()], daemon=True).start()
            return

        threading.Thread(target=self.execute_pipeline, args=(query, "Typed Input"), daemon=True).start()

    def trigger_voice_thread(self):
        """Fires off an independent worker thread to poll mic data without freezing the window UI."""
        threading.Thread(target=self.execute_voice_capture, daemon=True).start()

    def execute_voice_capture(self):
        """Controls audio capturing state mechanics cleanly."""
        self.set_status("🎙️ LISTENING TO AMBIENT MIC WAVEFORM...", "#ffcc00")
        self.append_log("\n🎙️ [Microphone Channel Open: Speak now]\n", "sys")
        
        spoken_text = listen_to_user()
        if not spoken_text:
            self.set_status("⚡ SYSTEM STATUS: READY", "#00ffcc")
            self.append_log("⚠️ [No vocal input data recognized. Loop aborted.]\n", "err")
            return
            
        self.execute_pipeline(spoken_text, "Vocal Stream")

    def execute_pipeline(self, command, source_type):
        """Main computational pipeline. Routes data streams and manages model generation."""
        self.append_log(f"\n👤 ARYAN ({source_type}): \"{command}\"\n", "aryan")
        
        # ROUTE MATRIX PATHWAY A: COUNCIL EXECUTION
        if self.should_trigger_council(command):
            self.set_status("👥 COUNCIL ASSEMBLED: AGENTS GENERATING DATA...", "#ffcc00")
            self.append_log("⏳ Calling Council Boardroom Nodes (Contrarian -> Synergist -> Chairman)...\n", "sys")
            
            debate_packet = run_council_debate(command)
            
            self.append_log(f"\n🎭 [THE CONTRARIAN OUTLOOK]:\n{debate_packet['contrarian']}\n", "ace")
            speak_text("Analyzing the risk layout from the contrarian.")
            speak_text(debate_packet['contrarian'])
            
            self.append_log(f"\n🚀 [THE SYNERGIST SOLUTION]:\n{debate_packet['synergist']}\n", "ace")
            speak_text("Reviewing the strategy modification from the synergist.")
            speak_text(debate_packet['synergist'])
            
            self.append_log(f"\n🏛️ [CHAIRMAN SUMMARY & EVALUATION]:\n{debate_packet['chairman']}\n", "sys")
            speak_text("The chairman's final evaluation and takeaways.")
            speak_text(debate_packet['chairman'])

        # ROUTE MATRIX PATHWAY B: STANDARD CHAT ROTATION (WITH MEMORY SYSTEM)
        else:
            text_lower = command.lower()
            if "think deeply" in text_lower or "smart mode" in text_lower or "analyze" in text_lower:
                active_model = SMART_MODEL
                self.set_status(f"🧠 RUNNING HEAVY LOGIC LAYER ({active_model})...", "#ffcc00")
                self.append_log(f"🧠 Routing to High-Capacity Logic Engine ({active_model})...\n", "sys")
            else:
                active_model = FAST_MODEL
                self.set_status(f"⚡ RUNNING OPTIMAL SPEED LAYER ({active_model})...", "#00ffcc")
                self.append_log(f"⚡ Routing to Low-Latency Speed Engine ({active_model})...\n", "sys")

            # 🛠️ CONSTRUCT MEMORY PAYLOAD PACKET
            # System instructions always sit at index 0
            messages_payload = [
                {"role": "system", "content": "You are Ace, an elite, highly intelligent desktop GUI AI assistant customized for Aryan."}
            ]
            # Inject the accumulated history logs straight into the middle
            messages_payload.extend(self.chat_history)
            # Finish by gluing the newest question onto the tail end
            messages_payload.append({"role": "user", "content": command})

            try:
                response = ollama.chat(
                    model=active_model,
                    messages=messages_payload
                )
                reply = response['message']['content']
                self.append_log(f"🤖 ACE: {reply}\n", "ace")
                
                # 📝 WRITE CURRENT TURN INTO THE LONG-TERM APP ARRAYS
                self.chat_history.append({"role": "user", "content": command})
                self.chat_history.append({"role": "assistant", "content": reply})
                
                # Prevent memory overflow lag by keeping only the last 20 context exchanges
                if len(self.chat_history) > 20:
                    self.chat_history = self.chat_history[-20:]

                speak_text(reply)
            except Exception as e:
                self.append_log(f"❌ Core link drop exception: {e}\n", "err")

        self.set_status("⚡ SYSTEM STATUS: READY", "#00ffcc")

# --------------------------------------------------
# APPLICATION RUNNER GATEWAY
# --------------------------------------------------
if __name__ == "__main__":
    app_root = tk.Tk()
    app_instance = AceGUIApp(app_root)
    app_root.mainloop()

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import scrolledtext
import threading
import sys
import os
import time
import ollama

# Import your locked, functional modules
from audio_provider import speak_text, listen_to_user
from council import run_council_debate

# 🤖 THE HYBRID ENGINE DECK
FAST_MODEL = "llama3.2:1b"
SMART_MODEL = "qwen2.5-coder:latest"

class AceGUIApp:
    def __init__(self, root):
        self.root = root
        self.root.title("ACE: Autonomous Console Engine // [ARYAN.H.O.PROTOCOL.O]")
        self.root.geometry("700x550")
        self.root.configure(bg="#121212") # Futuristic Dark Theme Base

        # 🧠 ACTIVE SHORT-TERM MEMORY BUFFER
        self.chat_history = []

        # --------------------------------------------------
        # 🎨 Sophisticated HUD INTERFACE LAYOUT
        # --------------------------------------------------
        # Top Status Indicator Bar
        self.status_label = tk.Label(root, text="⚡ SYSTEM STATUS: ONLINE [ARYAN.H.O.HYBRID.DECK]", 
                                     font=("Consolas", 10, "bold"), bg="#1a1a1a", fg="#00ffcc", anchor="w", pady=5)
        self.status_label.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=10, pady=(10, 5))

        # Core Console Readout Display Log
        self.log_display = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(root, wrap=tk.WORD, font=("Consolas", 11), 
                                                     bg="#1e1e1e", fg="#ffffff", insertbackground="#00ffcc")
        self.log_display.pack(fill=tk.BOTH, expand=True, padx=10, pady=5)
        
        # Configure unique colored tagging text streams
        self.log_display.tag_config("sys", foreground="#00ffcc")   # Neon Teal System Alert
        self.log_display.tag_config("aryan", foreground="#ffcc00") # Amber Aryan Output
        self.log_display.tag_config("ace", foreground="#ffffff")   # Clean White Response
        self.log_display.tag_config("err", foreground="#ff3333")   # Crimson Pipeline Failure

        # Bottom Input Dock Framework
        self.input_frame = tk.Frame(root, bg="#121212")
        self.input_frame.pack(fill=tk.X, padx=10, pady=10)

        # Manual Entry Field
        self.entry_field = tk.Entry(self.input_frame, font=("Consolas", 12), bg="#1e1e1e", fg="#ffffff", 
                                    insertbackground="#00ffcc", borderwidth=1, relief=tk.SOLID)
        self.entry_field.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.X, expand=True, ipady=4)
        self.entry_field.bind("<Return>", lambda event: self.process_text_input())

        # Operation Action Buttons
        self.send_btn = tk.Button(self.input_frame, text="SEND", font=("Consolas", 10, "bold"), 
                                  bg="#00ffcc", fg="#121212", activebackground="#00cc99", 
                                  command=self.process_text_input, width=8, relief=tk.FLAT)
        self.send_btn.pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=5)

        self.mic_btn = tk.Button(self.input_frame, text="🎙️ MIC", font=("Consolas", 10, "bold"), 
                                 bg="#ffcc00", fg="#121212", activebackground="#cc9900", 
                                 command=self.trigger_voice_thread, width=8, relief=tk.FLAT)
        self.mic_btn.pack(side=tk.LEFT)

        # Print initial boot diagnostics to the log display window
        self.append_log("🚀 Ace Protocol Initialized. Standby for input connection...\n", "sys")
        
        # Run standard startup greeting voice inside a safe non-blocking background thread
        threading.Thread(target=lambda: speak_text("System active, Aryan. Standing by."), daemon=True).start()

    # --------------------------------------------------
    # 🧠 CORE ENGINE INTELLIGENCE MATRIX
    # --------------------------------------------------
    def append_log(self, text, tag):
        """Appends formatted messages to the GUI display log safely."""
        self.log_display.insert(tk.END, text, tag)
        self.log_display.see(tk.END)

    def set_status(self, text, color="#00ffcc"):
        """Dynamically switches the text color and readout message of the top HUD bar."""
        self.status_label.config(text=text, fg=color)

    def should_trigger_council(self, text):
        """Checks for council trigger keywords while respecting intent negation modifiers."""
        text_lower = text.lower()
        triggers = ["council", "debate", "evaluate"]
        negations = ["don't", "dont", "do not", "never", "without", "skip", "stop"]
        
        if not any(kw in text_lower for kw in triggers):
            return False
            
        for neg in negations:
            if neg in text_lower:
                for kw in triggers:
                    if kw in text_lower and text_lower.find(neg) < text_lower.find(kw):
                        return False
        return True

    def process_text_input(self):
        """Extracts the manual string from the entry box and boots the computing pipeline."""
        query = self.entry_field.get().strip()
        if not query:
            return
            
        self.entry_field.delete(0, tk.END)
        
        if query.lower() in ["exit", "quit"]:
            self.set_status("🚪 DETACHING CLIENT NODE... GOODBYE", "#ff3333")
            self.append_log(f"\n📝 Command captured: \"{query}\"\n", "sys")
            threading.Thread(target=lambda: [speak_text("Systems shutting down. Goodbye, Aryan."), self.root.quit()], daemon=True).start()
            return

        threading.Thread(target=self.execute_pipeline, args=(query, "Typed Input"), daemon=True).start()

    def trigger_voice_thread(self):
        """Fires off an independent worker thread to poll mic data without freezing the window UI."""
        threading.Thread(target=self.execute_voice_capture, daemon=True).start()

    def execute_voice_capture(self):
        """Controls audio capturing state mechanics cleanly."""
        self.set_status("🎙️ LISTENING TO AMBIENT MIC WAVEFORM...", "#ffcc00")
        self.append_log("\n🎙️ [Microphone Channel Open: Speak now]\n", "sys")
        
        spoken_text = listen_to_user()
        if not spoken_text:
            self.set_status("⚡ SYSTEM STATUS: READY", "#00ffcc")
            self.append_log("⚠️ [No vocal input data recognized. Loop aborted.]\n", "err")
            return
            
        self.execute_pipeline(spoken_text, "Vocal Stream")

    def execute_pipeline(self, command, source_type):
        """Main computational pipeline. Routes data streams and manages model generation."""
        self.append_log(f"\n👤 ARYAN ({source_type}): \"{command}\"\n", "aryan")
        
        if self.should_trigger_council(command):
            self.set_status("👥 COUNCIL ASSEMBLED: AGENTS GENERATING DATA...", "#ffcc00")
            self.append_log("⏳ Calling Council Boardroom Nodes (Contrarian -> Synergist -> Chairman)...\n", "sys")
            
            debate_packet = run_council_debate(command)
            
            self.append_log(f"\n🎭 [THE CONTRARIAN OUTLOOK]:\n{debate_packet['contrarian']}\n", "ace")
            speak_text("Analyzing the risk layout from the contrarian.")
            speak_text(debate_packet['contrarian'])
            
            self.append_log(f"\n🚀 [THE SYNERGIST SOLUTION]:\n{debate_packet['synergist']}\n", "ace")
            speak_text("Reviewing the strategy modification from the synergist.")
            speak_text(debate_packet['synergist'])
            
            self.append_log(f"\n🏛️ [CHAIRMAN SUMMARY & EVALUATION]:\n{debate_packet['chairman']}\n", "sys")
            speak_text("The chairman's final evaluation and takeaways.")
            speak_text(debate_packet['chairman'])

        else:
            text_lower = command.lower()
            if "think deeply" in text_lower or "smart mode" in text_lower or "analyze" in text_lower:
                active_model = SMART_MODEL
                self.set_status(f"🧠 RUNNING HEAVY LOGIC LAYER ({active_model})...", "#ffcc00")
                self.append_log(f"🧠 Routing to High-Capacity Logic Engine ({active_model})...\n", "sys")
            else:
                active_model = FAST_MODEL
                self.set_status(f"⚡ RUNNING OPTIMAL SPEED LAYER ({active_model})...", "#00ffcc")
                self.append_log(f"⚡ Routing to Low-Latency Speed Engine ({active_model})...\n", "sys")

            messages_payload = [
                {"role": "system", "content": "You are Ace, an elite, highly intelligent desktop GUI AI assistant customized for Aryan."}
            ]
            messages_payload.extend(self.chat_history)
            messages_payload.append({"role": "user", "content": command})

            try:
                response = ollama.chat(model=active_model, messages=messages_payload)
                reply = response['message']['content']
                self.append_log(f"🤖 ACE: {reply}\n", "ace")
                
                self.chat_history.append({"role": "user", "content": command})
                self.chat_history.append({"role": "assistant", "content": reply})
                
                if len(self.chat_history) > 20:
                    self.chat_history = self.chat_history[-20:]

                speak_text(reply)
            except Exception as e:
                self.append_log(f"❌ Core link drop exception: {e}\n", "err")

        self.set_status("⚡ SYSTEM STATUS: READY", "#00ffcc")

# --------------------------------------------------
# 🚀 THE ENGINE STARTER (CRITICAL: Make sure this is saved!)
# --------------------------------------------------
if __name__ == "__main__":
    app_root = tk.Tk()
    app_instance = AceGUIApp(app_root)
    app_root.mainloop()

    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/three.js/r128/three.min.js"></script>
    <script>
        let scene, camera, renderer, starParticles, orbMesh, orbGlow;
        let voiceBrightTarget = 0.0, currentVoiceBright = 0.0;
        let isListening = false;

        // --------------------------------------------------
        // 🌌 THREE.JS SCENE PROTOCOLS (Orb & Space Ecosystem)
        // --------------------------------------------------
        function initSpaceScene() {
            const container = document.getElementById('canvas-container');
            
            scene = new THREE.Scene();
            camera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(60, window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight, 0.1, 1000);
            camera.position.z = 5;

            renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({ antialias: true, alpha: false });
            renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
            renderer.setPixelRatio(window.devicePixelRatio);
            container.appendChild(renderer.domElement);

            // 1) Cosmic Twinkling Starfield Setup
            const starGeometry = new THREE.BufferGeometry();
            const starCount = 1200;
            const starPositions = new Float32Array(starCount * 3);
            for(let i=0; i < starCount * 3; i++) {
                starPositions[i] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 15;
            }
            starGeometry.setAttribute('position', new THREE.BufferAttribute(starPositions, 3));
            const starMaterial = new THREE.PointsMaterial({ color: 0xffffff, size: 0.02, transparent: true, opacity: 0.8 });
            starParticles = new THREE.Points(starGeometry, starMaterial);
            scene.add(starParticles);

            // 2) Luminous Core Teal Orb Setup (Layered Spheres for Bloom Simulation)
            const orbGeometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.6, 64, 64);
            const orbMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color: 0x2DD4A8 });
            orbMesh = new THREE.Mesh(orbGeometry, orbMaterial);
            scene.add(orbMesh);

            // Halo Core Layer 2
            const glowGeometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.8, 32, 32);
            const glowMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color: 0x2DD4A8, transparent: true, opacity: 0.25, side: THREE.BackSide });
            orbGlow = new THREE.Mesh(glowGeometry, glowMaterial);
            scene.add(orbGlow);

            window.addEventListener('resize', onWindowResize);
            animateLoop();
        }

        function animateLoop() {
            requestAnimationFrame(animateLoop);

            const time = Date.now() * 0.001;

            // Idle Breathing Sinusoidal Loop (~4s cycle)
            let breathing = Math.sin(time * 1.5) * 0.04;
            
            // Interpolate towards voice activity indicators dynamically
            currentVoiceBright += (voiceBrightTarget - currentVoiceBright) * 0.1;
            
            let scalingFactor = 1.0 + breathing + (currentVoiceBright * 0.3);
            orbMesh.scale.set(scalingFactor, scalingFactor, scalingFactor);
            orbGlow.scale.set(scalingFactor * 1.2, scalingFactor * 1.2, scalingFactor * 1.2);
            
            // Slow cosmic system rotation mechanics
            starParticles.rotation.y = time * 0.02;

            renderer.render(scene, camera);
        }

        function onWindowResize() {
            camera.aspect = window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight;
            camera.updateProjectionMatrix();
            renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
        }

        // --------------------------------------------------
        // ⚡ COMMAND PIPELINE & BACKEND SERVER INTERACTION
        # This channels textual or vocal vectors out to the Python Flask microservice
        // --------------------------------------------------
        function postCommandToBackend(payloadText) {
            updateSystemUIState("processing");
            appendResponseCard("User Request", payloadText);

            fetch('/api/command', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ command: payloadText })
            })
            .then(res => res.json())
            .then(data => {
                updateSystemUIState("idle");
                
                // If it is an objective multi-agent response structure, iterate cleanly
                if (typeof data.response === 'object') {
                    if(data.response.contrarian) appendResponseCard("🎭 The Contrarian", data.response.contrarian);
                    if(data.response.synergist) appendResponseCard("🚀 The Synergist", data.response.synergist);
                    if(data.response.chairman) appendResponseCard("🏛️ The Chairman Summary", data.response.chairman);
                } else {
                    appendResponseCard("Ace Intelligence", data.response);
                }
                
                // Visual spark response processing visualization modulation
                simulateVoiceActivity();
            })
            .catch(err => {
                updateSystemUIState("idle");
                appendResponseCard("System Error", "Could not negotiate structural link execution with Python Server backend pipeline.");
            });
        }

        function handleTextSubmit(event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter') {
                const inputElement = document.getElementById('chat-entry');
                const commandText = inputElement.value.strip ? inputElement.value.strip() : inputElement.value;
                if (!commandText) return;
                inputElement.value = "";
                postCommandToBackend(commandText);
            }
        }

        function toggleVoiceCapture() {
            const btn = document.getElementById('master-mic-btn');
            const svgIcon = document.getElementById('mic-icon-svg');
            
            if (!isListening) {
                // Enter active recording state context
                isListening = true;
                btn.classList.add('active');
                updateSystemUIState("listening");
                // Modify the visual asset markup dynamically into a square stop tracking path box
                svgIcon.innerHTML = `<rect x="6" y="6" width="12" height="12"/>`;
                
                // Initialize modern audio streaming transaction link
                startBrowserVoiceCapture();
            } else {
                stopVoiceProcessingState();
            }
        }

        function stopVoiceProcessingState() {
            const btn = document.getElementById('master-mic-btn');
            const svgIcon = document.getElementById('mic-icon-svg');
            isListening = false;
            btn.classList.remove('active');
            svgIcon.innerHTML = `<path d="M12 14c1.66 0 3-1.34 3-3V5c0-1.66-1.34-3-3-3S9 3.34 9 5v6c0 1.66 1.34 3 3 3zm5.3-3c0 3-2.54 5.1-5.3 5.1S6.7 14 6.7 11H5c0 3.41 2.72 6.23 6 6.72V21h2v-3.28c3.28-.48 6-3.3 6-6.72h-1.7z"/>`;
        }

        function startBrowserVoiceCapture() {
            // Check native capture hardware interfaces safely
            if (!('webkitSpeechRecognition' in window) && !('SpeechRecognition' in window)) {
                appendResponseCard("Hardware Alert", "Speech recognition structures not supported in native hosting container browser engine environment. Use the input box to type safely.");
                stopVoiceProcessingState();
                updateSystemUIState("idle");
                return;
            }

            const SpeechRecognition = window.SpeechRecognition || window.webkitSpeechRecognition;
            const recognition = new SpeechRecognition();
            recognition.lang = 'en-US';
            recognition.interimResults = false;
            recognition.maxAlternatives = 1;

            recognition.onresult = (event) => {
                const vocalString = event.results[0][0].transcript;
                postCommandToBackend(vocalString);
            };

            recognition.onerror = () => {
                appendResponseCard("System Log", "Voice processing matrix encountered tracking silence parameters.");
                stopVoiceProcessingState();
                updateSystemUIState("idle");
            };

            recognition.onend = () => {
                stopVoiceProcessingState();
            };

            recognition.start();
        }

        // UI Decorator Manipulators
        function updateSystemUIState(state) {
            const text = document.getElementById('system-status-text');
            const dot = document.getElementById('global-status-dot');
            dot.className = "status-dot";
            
            if(state === "listening") { text.innerText = "LISTENING"; dot.classList.add('listening'); }
            else if(state === "processing") { text.innerText = "PROCESSING"; dot.classList.add('processing'); }
            else { text.innerText = "ONLINE"; }
        }

        function appendResponseCard(speaker, message) {
            const stack = document.getElementById('response-stack');
            const card = document.createElement('div');
            card.className = 'response-card';
            card.innerHTML = `<div class="speaker-tag">${speaker}</div><div>${message}</div>`;
            
            // Enforce unified display limits by popping out ancestral cards
            if(stack.children.length >= 3) stack.removeChild(stack.children[0]);
            stack.appendChild(card);
        }

        function simulateVoiceActivity() {
            voiceBrightTarget = 1.0;
            setTimeout(() => { voiceBrightTarget = 0.0; }, 800);
        }

        function togglePanel() {
            document.getElementById('activity-panel').classList.toggle('collapsed');
        }

        // Initialize spatial rendering engine stack on document boot
        window.onload = initSpaceScene;
    </script>
</body>
</html>


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------


from flask import Flask, request, jsonify, send_from_string, render_template_string
import os
import sys
import threading
import time
import ollama

# Import your locked, functional core speech assets
from audio_provider import speak_text
from council import run_council_debate

app = Flask(__name__)

# 🤖 THE HYBRID ENGINE DECK REGISTERED WITH LOCAL SYSTEM TAGS
FAST_MODEL = "llama3.2:1b"
SMART_MODEL = "qwen2.5-coder:latest"

# Storage array for state processing history memory loads
chat_history = []

def should_trigger_council(text):
    """Analyzes intent to prevent false-positives when trigger words are in a negative context."""
    text_lower = text.lower()
    triggers = ["council", "debate", "evaluate"]
    negations = ["don't", "dont", "do not", "never", "without", "skip", "stop"]
    
    if not any(kw in text_lower for kw in triggers):
        return False
        
    for neg in negations:
        if neg in text_lower:
            for kw in triggers:
                if kw in text_lower and text_lower.find(neg) < text_lower.find(kw):
                    return False
    return True

@app.route('/')
def serve_dashboard_console():
    """Serves index.html directly into local browser sessions."""
    try:
        with open('index.html', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            return f.read()
    except Exception as e:
        return f"System Matrix Failure: Could not locate index.html framework in active working folder path. Error: {e}"

@app.route('/api/command', methods=['POST'])
def orchestrate_command_routing():
    """Main routing engine gateway for both text and voice entries."""
    global chat_history
    data = request.get_json() or {}
    command = data.get('command', '').strip()
    
    if not command:
        return jsonify({"response": "Empty vector transaction payload abandoned."})
        
    print(f"\n📥 Incoming transaction request logged: \"{command}\"")

    # CASE A: MULTI-AGENT COUNCIL ROUTING PATHWAY
    if should_trigger_council(command):
        print("👥 Assembling Council Matrix Boardroom Core...")
        debate_packet = run_council_debate(command)
        
        # Deploy a non-blocking daemon background worker thread to read back responses safely without bottlenecking network sockets
        def narrate_council():
            speak_text("Analyzing the risk layout from the contrarian.")
            speak_text(debate_packet['contrarian'])
            time.sleep(0.3)
            speak_text("Reviewing the strategy modification from the synergist.")
            speak_text(debate_packet['synergist'])
            time.sleep(0.3)
            speak_text("The chairman's final evaluation and takeaways.")
            speak_text(debate_packet['chairman'])

        threading.Thread(target=narrate_council, daemon=True).start()
        return jsonify({"response": debate_packet})

    # CASE B: CONTEXTUAL DICTIONARY CHAT ROUTING PATHWAY
    else:
        text_lower = command.lower()
        if "think deeply" in text_lower or "smart mode" in text_lower or "analyze" in text_lower:
            active_model = SMART_MODEL
            print(f"🧠 Escalating computation layer -> routing through {active_model}")
        else:
            active_model = FAST_MODEL
            print(f"⚡ Pacing transaction optimally -> routing through {active_model}")

        # Construct short-term payload arrays to track conversations accurately
        messages_payload = [
            {"role": "system", "content": "You are Ace, an elite, highly intelligent desktop Jarvis-style AI companion customized for Aryan."}
        ]
        messages_payload.extend(chat_history)
        messages_payload.append({"role": "user", "content": command})

        try:
            response = ollama.chat(model=active_model, messages=messages_payload)
            reply = response['message']['content']
            
            # Write transaction to application history logs
            chat_history.append({"role": "user", "content": command})
            chat_history.append({"role": "assistant", "content": reply})
            
            # Slide memory arrays window to prevent resource overflow limits
            if len(chat_history) > 20:
                chat_history = chat_history[-20:]

            # Stream audio output in background thread to prevent browser socket hanging
            threading.Thread(target=lambda: speak_text(reply), daemon=True).start()
            return jsonify({"response": reply})

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"❌ Ollama transaction execution drop: {e}")
            return jsonify({"response": f"Core framework loop dropped processing link transaction safely: {e}"})

if __name__ == '__main__':
    print("\n========================================================")
    # Exposing port 5000 allows local network devices to hook directly into the system parameters
    print(" 🔥 ACE CORE SERVER: RUNNING AT http://127.0.0.1:5000")
    print("      Open this address in any browser to launch interface")
    print("========================================================\n")
    app.run(host='0.0.0.0', port=5000, debug=False)

from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
import os
import sys
import threading
import time
import ollama

# Import your locked, functional core speech assets
from audio_provider import speak_text
from council import run_council_debate

# 🤖 THE HYBRID ENGINE DECK REGISTERED WITH LOCAL SYSTEM TAGS
FAST_MODEL = "llama3.2:1b"
SMART_MODEL = "qwen2.5-coder:latest"

# Storage array for state processing history memory loads
chat_history = []

def should_trigger_council(text):
    """Analyzes intent to prevent false-positives when trigger words are in a negative context."""
    text_lower = text.lower()
    triggers = ["council", "debate", "evaluate"]
    negations = ["don't", "dont", "do not", "never", "without", "skip", "stop"]
    
    if not any(kw in text_lower for kw in triggers):
        return False
        
    for neg in negations:
        if neg in text_lower:
            for kw in triggers:
                if kw in text_lower and text_lower.find(neg) < text_lower.find(kw):
                    return False
    return True

def serve_dashboard_console():
    """Serves index.html directly into local browser sessions."""

        with open('index.html', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            return f.read()

            speak_text("Reviewing the strategy modification from the synergist.")
            speak_text(debate_packet['synergist'])

                        <path d="M12 14c1.66 0 3-1.34 3-3V5c0-1.66-1.34-3-3-3S9 3.34 9 5v6c0 1.66 1.34 3 3 3zm5.3-3c0 3-2.54 5.1-5.3 5.1S6.7 14 6.7 11H5c0 3.41 2.72 6.23 6 6.72V21h2v-3.28c3.28-.48 6-3.3 6-6.72h-1.7z"/>
                    </svg>

    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/three.js/r128/three.min.js"></script>
    <script>
        let scene, camera, renderer, starParticles, orbMesh, orbGlow;
        let voiceBrightTarget = 0.0, currentVoiceBright = 0.0;
        let isListening = false;

        // 🌌 THREE.JS SCENE PROTOCOLS
        function initSpaceScene() {
            const container = document.getElementById('canvas-container');
            
            scene = new THREE.Scene();
            camera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(60, window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight, 0.1, 1000);
            camera.position.z = 5;

            renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({ antialias: true, alpha: false });
            renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
            renderer.setPixelRatio(window.devicePixelRatio);
            container.appendChild(renderer.domElement);

            const starGeometry = new THREE.BufferGeometry();
            const starCount = 1200;
            const starPositions = new Float32Array(starCount * 3);
            for(let i=0; i < starCount * 3; i++) {
                starPositions[i] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 15;
            }
            starGeometry.setAttribute('position', new THREE.BufferAttribute(starPositions, 3));
            const starMaterial = new THREE.PointsMaterial({ color: 0xffffff, size: 0.02, transparent: true, opacity: 0.8 });
            starParticles = new THREE.Points(starGeometry, starMaterial);
            scene.add(starParticles);

            const orbGeometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.6, 64, 64);
            const orbMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color: 0x2DD4A8 });
            orbMesh = new THREE.Mesh(orbGeometry, orbMaterial);
            scene.add(orbMesh);

            const glowGeometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.8, 32, 32);
            const glowMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color: 0x2DD4A8, transparent: true, opacity: 0.25, side: THREE.BackSide });
            orbGlow = new THREE.Mesh(glowGeometry, glowMaterial);
            scene.add(glowGlow || orbGlow);

            window.addEventListener('resize', onWindowResize);
            animateLoop();
        }

        function animateLoop() {
            requestAnimationFrame(animateLoop);
            const time = Date.now() * 0.001;

            let breathing = Math.sin(time * 1.5) * 0.04;
            currentVoiceBright += (voiceBrightTarget - currentVoiceBright) * 0.1;
            
            let scalingFactor = 1.0 + breathing + (currentVoiceBright * 0.3);
            if (orbMesh) orbMesh.scale.set(scalingFactor, scalingFactor, scalingFactor);
            if (orbGlow) orbGlow.scale.set(scalingFactor * 1.2, scalingFactor * 1.2, scalingFactor * 1.2);
            
            if (starParticles) starParticles.rotation.y = time * 0.02;
            renderer.render(scene, camera);
        }

        function onWindowResize() {
            camera.aspect = window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight;
            camera.updateProjectionMatrix();
            renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
        }

        // ⚡ COMMAND PIPELINE & BACKEND SERVER INTERACTION
        // This channels textual or vocal vectors out to the Python Flask microservice safely
        function postCommandToBackend(payloadText) {
            updateSystemUIState("processing");
            appendResponseCard("User Request", payloadText);

            fetch('/api/command', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ command: payloadText })
            })
            .then(res => res.json())
            .then(data => {
                updateSystemUIState("idle");
                
                if (typeof data.response === 'object') {
                    if(data.response.contrarian) appendResponseCard("🎭 The Contrarian", data.response.contrarian);
                    if(data.response.synergist) appendResponseCard("🚀 The Synergist", data.response.synergist);
                    if(data.response.chairman) appendResponseCard("🏛️ The Chairman Summary", data.response.chairman);
                } else {
                    appendResponseCard("Ace Intelligence", data.response);
                }
                simulateVoiceActivity();
            })
            .catch(err => {
                updateSystemUIState("idle");
                appendResponseCard("System Error", "Could not negotiate structural link execution with Python Server backend pipeline.");
            });
        }

        function handleTextSubmit(event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter') {
                const inputElement = document.getElementById('chat-entry');
                const commandText = inputElement.value.trim();
                if (!commandText) return;
                inputElement.value = "";
                postCommandToBackend(commandText);
            }
        }

        function toggleVoiceCapture() {
            const btn = document.getElementById('master-mic-btn');
            const svgIcon = document.getElementById('mic-icon-svg');
            
            if (!isListening) {
                isListening = true;
                btn.classList.add('active');
                updateSystemUIState("listening");
                svgIcon.innerHTML = `<rect x="6" y="6" width="12" height="12"/>`;
                startBrowserVoiceCapture();
            } else {
                stopVoiceProcessingState();
            }
        }

        function stopVoiceProcessingState() {
            const btn = document.getElementById('master-mic-btn');
            const svgIcon = document.getElementById('mic-icon-svg');
            isListening = false;
            if (btn) btn.classList.remove('active');
            if (svgIcon) svgIcon.innerHTML = `<path d="M12 14c1.66 0 3-1.34 3-3V5c0-1.66-1.34-3-3-3S9 3.34 9 5v6c0 1.66 1.34 3 3 3zm5.3-3c0 3-2.54 5.1-5.3 5.1S6.7 14 6.7 11H5c0 3.41 2.72 6.23 6 6.72V21h2v-3.28c3.28-.48 6-3.3 6-6.72h-1.7z"/>`;
        }

        function startBrowserVoiceCapture() {
            if (!('webkitSpeechRecognition' in window) && !('SpeechRecognition' in window)) {
                appendResponseCard("Hardware Alert", "Speech recognition structures not supported in native browser engine container. Use the text input box to type safely.");
                stopVoiceProcessingState();
                updateSystemUIState("idle");
                return;
            }

            const SpeechRecognition = window.SpeechRecognition || window.webkitSpeechRecognition;
            const recognition = new SpeechRecognition();
            recognition.lang = 'en-US';
            recognition.interimResults = false;
            recognition.maxAlternatives = 1;

            recognition.onresult = (event) => {
                const vocalString = event.results[0][0].transcript;
                postCommandToBackend(vocalString);
            };

            recognition.onerror = () => {
                appendResponseCard("System Log", "Voice processing matrix encountered tracking silence parameters.");
                stopVoiceProcessingState();
                updateSystemUIState("idle");
            };

            recognition.onend = () => {
                stopVoiceProcessingState();
            };

            recognition.start();
        }

        function updateSystemUIState(state) {
            const text = document.getElementById('system-status-text');
            const dot = document.getElementById('global-status-dot');
            if (!dot) return;
            dot.className = "status-dot";
            
            if(state === "listening") { if(text) text.innerText = "LISTENING"; dot.classList.add('listening'); }
            else if(state === "processing") { if(text) text.innerText = "PROCESSING"; dot.classList.add('processing'); }
            else { if(text) text.innerText = "ONLINE"; }
        }

        function appendResponseCard(speaker, message) {
            const stack = document.getElementById('response-stack');
            const card = document.createElement('div');
            card.className = 'response-card';
            card.innerHTML = `<div class="speaker-tag">${speaker}</div><div>${message}</div>`;
            
            if(stack.children.length >= 3) stack.removeChild(stack.children[0]);
            stack.appendChild(card);
        }

        function simulateVoiceActivity() {
            voiceBrightTarget = 1.0;
            setTimeout(() => { voiceBrightTarget = 0.0; }, 800);
        }

        function togglePanel() {
            document.getElementById('activity-panel').classList.toggle('collapsed');
        }

        window.onload = initSpaceScene;
    </script>
</body>
</html>

        </div>
    </div>

    <div id="activity-panel" class="glass-panel">

            </div>
            
            <div class="mic-container">
                <div class="mic-button" id="master-mic-btn" onclick="toggleVoiceCapture()">
                    <svg id="mic-icon-svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                        <path d="M12 14c1.66 0 3-1.34 3-3V5c0-1.66-1.34-3-3-3S9 3.34 9 5v6c0 1.66 1.34 3 3 3zm5.3-3c0 3-2.54 5.1-5.3 5.1S6.7 14 6.7 11H5c0 3.41 2.72 6.23 6 6.72V21h2v-3.28c3.28-.48 6-3.3 6-6.72h-1.7z"/>
                    </svg>
                </div>
                <div class="pulse-ring"></div>
            </div>
