    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/three.js/r128/three.min.js"></script>
    <script>
        let scene, camera, renderer, starParticles, orbMesh, orbGlow;
        let voiceBrightTarget = 0.0, currentVoiceBright = 0.0;
        
        // Unified Voice Stream State Variables
        let recognition;
        let isListeningMode = false; // false = ambient "Hi Ace" scan, true = active command logging

        // 🌌 THREE.JS SCENE PROTOCOLS
        function initSpaceScene() {
            const container = document.getElementById('canvas-container');
            
            scene = new THREE.Scene();
            camera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(60, window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight, 0.1, 1000);
            camera.position.z = 5;

            renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({ antialias: true, alpha: false });
            renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
            renderer.setPixelRatio(window.devicePixelRatio);
            container.appendChild(renderer.domElement);

            const starGeometry = new THREE.BufferGeometry();
            const starCount = 1200;
            const starPositions = new Float32Array(starCount * 3);
            for(let i=0; i < starCount * 3; i++) {
                starPositions[i] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 15;
            }
            starGeometry.setAttribute('position', new THREE.BufferAttribute(starPositions, 3));
            const starMaterial = new THREE.PointsMaterial({ color: 0xffffff, size: 0.02, transparent: true, opacity: 0.8 });
            starParticles = new THREE.Points(starGeometry, starMaterial);
            scene.add(starParticles);

            const orbGeometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.6, 64, 64);
            const orbMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color: 0x2DD4A8 });
            orbMesh = new THREE.Mesh(orbGeometry, orbMaterial);
            scene.add(orbMesh);

            const glowGeometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.8, 32, 32);
            const glowMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color: 0x2DD4A8, transparent: true, opacity: 0.25, side: THREE.BackSide });
            orbGlow = new THREE.Mesh(glowGeometry, glowMaterial);
            scene.add(orbGlow); // Fixed structural latent variable link here

            window.addEventListener('resize', onWindowResize);
            
            // Register Keyboard Hook Interfaces
            document.addEventListener('keydown', handleGlobalKeydown);

            // Launch Unified Speech Matrix
            initUnifiedSpeechEngine();
            animateLoop();
        }

        function animateLoop() {
            requestAnimationFrame(animateLoop);
            const time = Date.now() * 0.001;

            let breathing = Math.sin(time * 1.5) * 0.04;
            currentVoiceBright += (voiceBrightTarget - currentVoiceBright) * 0.1;
            
            let scalingFactor = 1.0 + breathing + (currentVoiceBright * 0.3);
            if (orbMesh) orbMesh.scale.set(scalingFactor, scalingFactor, scalingFactor);
            if (orbGlow) orbGlow.scale.set(scalingFactor * 1.2, scalingFactor * 1.2, scalingFactor * 1.2);
            
            if (starParticles) starParticles.rotation.y = time * 0.02;
            renderer.render(scene, camera);
        }

        function onWindowResize() {
            camera.aspect = window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight;
            camera.updateProjectionMatrix();
            renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
        }

        // 🎙️ UNIFIED SPEECH RECOGNITION PERSISTENT CORE
        function initUnifiedSpeechEngine() {
            if (!('webkitSpeechRecognition' in window) && !('SpeechRecognition' in window)) {
                appendResponseCard("Hardware Alert", "Speech recognition structures not supported in browser environment.");
                return;
            }

            const SpeechRecognition = window.SpeechRecognition || window.webkitSpeechRecognition;
            recognition = new SpeechRecognition();
            recognition.continuous = true;
            recognition.interimResults = false;
            recognition.lang = 'en-US';

            recognition.onresult = (event) => {
                const lastIndex = event.resultIndex;
                const transcript = event.results[lastIndex][0].transcript.trim();
                const transcriptLower = transcript.toLowerCase();
                
                console.log("Speech parsed transaction packet:", transcript);

                // PATHWAY 1: ACTIVE LISTEN MODE LOGGED
                if (isListeningMode) {
                    postCommandToBackend(transcript);
                    switchToAmbientMode();
                } 
                // PATHWAY 2: PASSIVE AMBIENT SCANNING ("Hi Ace" Tracking)
                else {
                    if (transcriptLower.includes("hi ace")) {
                        let triggerIndex = transcriptLower.indexOf("hi ace") + 6;
                        let trailingCommand = transcript.substring(triggerIndex).trim();
                        
                        if (trailingCommand.length > 0) {
                            // Captured wake phrase and task description together
                            postCommandToBackend(trailingCommand);
                        } else {
                            // Captured wake phrase only, activate listening mode
                            switchToActiveListeningMode();
                        }
                    }
                }
            };

            recognition.onerror = (e) => {
                console.log("Speech framework exception bypassed safely:", e);
            };

            recognition.onend = () => {
                // Ensure persistent runtime looping
                recognition.start();
            };

            recognition.start();
        }

        function switchToActiveListeningMode() {
            isListeningMode = true;
            const btn = document.getElementById('master-mic-btn');
            const svgIcon = document.getElementById('mic-icon-svg');
            if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
            updateSystemUIState("listening");
            if (svgIcon) svgIcon.innerHTML = `<rect x="6" y="6" width="12" height="12"/>`;
        }

        function switchToAmbientMode() {
            isListeningMode = false;
            const btn = document.getElementById('master-mic-btn');
            const svgIcon = document.getElementById('mic-icon-svg');
            if (btn) btn.classList.remove('active');
            updateSystemUIState("idle");
            if (svgIcon) svgIcon.innerHTML = `<path d="M12 14c1.66 0 3-1.34 3-3V5c0-1.66-1.34-3-3-3S9 3.34 9 5v6c0 1.66 1.34 3 3 3zm5.3-3c0 3-2.54 5.1-5.3 5.1S6.7 14 6.7 11H5c0 3.41 2.72 6.23 6 6.72V21h2v-3.28c3.28-.48 6-3.3 6-6.72h-1.7z"/>`;
        }

        function toggleVoiceCapture() {
            if (!isListeningMode) {
                switchToActiveListeningMode();
            } else {
                switchToAmbientMode();
            }
        }

        // ⌨️ KEYBOARD ENTRY HANDLERS
        function handleGlobalKeydown(event) {
            // If the user hits Enter while NOT typing inside the input field, trigger the mic
            if (event.key === 'Enter' && document.activeElement !== document.getElementById('chat-entry')) {
                event.preventDefault();
                toggleVoiceCapture();
            }
        }

        function handleTextSubmit(event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter') {
                const inputElement = document.getElementById('chat-entry');
                const commandText = inputElement.value.trim();
                if (!commandText) return;
                inputElement.value = "";
                postCommandToBackend(commandText);
            }
        }

        // ⚡ WEB DATA EXCHANGE PIPELINE
        function postCommandToBackend(payloadText) {
            updateSystemUIState("processing");
            appendResponseCard("User Request", payloadText);

            fetch('/api/command', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ command: payloadText })
            })
            .then(res => res.json())
            .then(data => {
                updateSystemUIState("idle");
                
                if (typeof data.response === 'object') {
                    if(data.response.contrarian) appendResponseCard("🎭 The Contrarian", data.response.contrarian);
                    if(data.response.synergist) appendResponseCard("🚀 The Synergist", data.response.synergist);
                    if(data.response.chairman) appendResponseCard("🏛️ The Chairman Summary", data.response.chairman);
                } else {
                    appendResponseCard("Ace Intelligence", data.response);
                }
                simulateVoiceActivity();
            })
            .catch(err => {
                updateSystemUIState("idle");
                appendResponseCard("System Error", "Could not negotiate link transaction execution.");
            });
        }

        // 🛠️ CHROME DECORATOR FUNCTION INTERFACES
        function triggerMapModule() {
            appendResponseCard("Tactical Map Matrix", "Initializing grid array scan layers... Local host framework layout verified nominal.");
        }

        function triggerAlertsModule() {
            appendResponseCard("Alerts Sub-Console", "All telemetry metrics currently reading nominal. Zero network intrusion profiles detected.");
        }

        function updateSystemUIState(state) {
            const text = document.getElementById('system-status-text');
            const dot = document.getElementById('global-status-dot');
            if (!dot) return;
            dot.className = "status-dot";
            
            if(state === "listening") { if(text) text.innerText = "LISTENING"; dot.classList.add('listening'); }
            else if(state === "processing") { if(text) text.innerText = "PROCESSING"; dot.classList.add('processing'); }
            else { if(text) text.innerText = "ONLINE"; }
        }

        function appendResponseCard(speaker, message) {
            const stack = document.getElementById('response-stack');
            const card = document.createElement('div');
            card.className = 'response-card';
            card.innerHTML = `<div class="speaker-tag">${speaker}</div><div>${message}</div>`;
            
            if(stack.children.length >= 3) stack.removeChild(stack.children[0]);
            stack.appendChild(card);
        }

        function simulateVoiceActivity() {
            voiceBrightTarget = 1.0;
            setTimeout(() => { voiceBrightTarget = 0.0; }, 1200);
        }

        function togglePanel() {
            document.getElementById('activity-panel').classList.toggle('collapsed');
        }

        window.onload = initSpaceScene;
    </script>
</body>
</html>

            top: 70px; right: 10px; width: 260px; height: calc(100% - 210px);
            border-radius: 8px; padding: 15px; display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 20px;
        }
        #activity-panel.collapsed { width: 36px; padding: 15px 5px; overflow: hidden; }
        .panel-toggle { position: absolute; top: 10px; left: 10px; cursor: pointer; color: #2DD4A8; font-size: 12px; font-weight: bold; }
        .panel-content { display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 20px; width: 230px; margin-top: 20px; }
        .section-header { font-size: 10px; font-weight: 600; color: rgba(255,255,255,0.4); letter-spacing: 0.08em; display: flex; justify-content: space-between; }
        .panel-entry { font-size: 12px; color: rgba(255,255,255,0.8); background: rgba(255,255,255,0.03); padding: 8px; border-radius: 4px; border-left: 2px solid #2DD4A8; transform: translateX(0); animation: slideIn 300ms cubic-bezier(0.16, 1, 0.3, 1); }

        /* 3) Floating Dynamic Response Display Stack */
        #response-stack { position: absolute; top: 120px; left: 30px; z-index: 2; display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 15px; pointer-events: none; }
        .response-card {
            width: 280px; background: rgba(22, 23, 29, 0.75); border-radius: 6px;
            border-top: 2px solid #2DD4A8; padding: 15px; font-size: 13px; line-height: 1.5;
            box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(0,0,0,0.5); pointer-events: auto;
            transform: rotateX(8deg); animation: floatAnim 4s ease-in-out infinite, entryRotate 400ms cubic-bezier(0.16, 1, 0.3, 1);
        }
        .response-card .speaker-tag { font-size: 10px; font-weight: bold; text-transform: uppercase; letter-spacing: 0.05em; margin-bottom: 5px; color: #2DD4A8; }

        /* 🎙️ FIXED BOTTOM INTERACTIVE CONTROL DOCK */
        #control-dock {
            position: absolute; bottom: 0; left: 0; width: 100%; height: 130px;
            z-index: 2; display: flex; flex-direction: column; align-items: center;
            justify-content: center; pointer-events: none; gap: 10px;
        }
        .interactive-elements { display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 20px; pointer-events: auto; }
        
        .chat-input-wrapper {
            background: rgba(14, 15, 19, 0.4); backdrop-filter: blur(10px);
            border: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.08); border-radius: 20px;
            padding: 5px 15px; display: flex; align-items: center; width: 320px;
        }
        .chat-input-wrapper input { background: none; border: none; outline: none; color: #ffffff; font-family: 'Inter', sans-serif; font-size: 13px; width: 100%; }
        .chat-input-wrapper input::placeholder { color: rgba(255,255,255,0.3); }

        .mic-container { position: relative; width: 64px; height: 64px; }
        .mic-button {
            width: 64px; height: 64px; border-radius: 50%; background: #16171D;
            border: 1px solid rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.08); display: flex; align-items: center;
            justify-content: center; cursor: pointer; transition: all 0.3s cubic-bezier(0.16, 1, 0.3, 1);
        }
        .mic-button svg { width: 22px; height: 22px; fill: #ffffff; transition: fill 0.3s; }
        
        .mic-button.active {
            border-color: #2DD4A8;
            box-shadow: 0 0 24px rgba(45, 212, 168, 0.5);
        }
        .mic-button.active svg { fill: #2DD4A8; }
        .pulse-ring {
            position: absolute; top: 0; left: 0; width: 64px; height: 64px;
            border-radius: 50%; border: 2px solid #2DD4A8; pointer-events: none;
            opacity: 0; transform: scale(1);
        }
        .mic-button.active + .pulse-ring { animation: ringSpread 1.4s infinite cubic-bezier(0.16, 1, 0.3, 1); }

        .hint-text { font-size: 11px; font-family: monospace; text-transform: uppercase; color: rgba(255,255,255,0.4); letter-spacing: 0.08em; }

        @keyframes ringSpread { 0% { transform: scale(1); opacity: 1; } 100% { transform: scale(1.3); opacity: 0; } }
        @keyframes floatAnim { 0%, 100% { transform: translateY(0px) rotateX(8deg); } 50% { transform: translateY(-6px) rotateX(8deg); } }
        @keyframes entryRotate { 0% { opacity: 0; transform: scale(0.9) translateY(10px); } 100% { opacity: 1; transform: scale(1) translateY(0); } }
        @keyframes slideIn { 0% { opacity: 0; transform: translateX(20px); } 100% { opacity: 1; transform: translateX(0); } }
        @keyframes pulseGlow { 0%, 100% { opacity: 0.6; } 50% { opacity: 1; } }

<body>

    <div id="response-stack">
        <div class="response-card" id="welcome-card">
            <div class="speaker-tag">System Core</div>
            Console engine online, Aryan. Interactive audio matrix initialized. Speak freely or type below.
        </div>
    </div>

    <div id="activity-panel" class="glass-panel">
        <div class="panel-toggle" onclick="togglePanel()">🗲</div>
        <div class="panel-content" id="panel-content-area">
            <div>
                <div class="section-header">INBOX REPLIES <span>0</span></div>
            </div>
            <div>
                <div class="section-header">SCOUT TASKS <span>READY</span></div>
                <div class="panel-entry">Neural path verified.</div>
            </div>
            <div>
                <div class="section-header">FLUX SEGMENTS <span>ACTIVE</span></div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <div id="control-dock">
        <div class="interactive-elements">
            <div class="chat-input-wrapper">
                <input type="text" id="chat-entry" placeholder="Send manual system execution command..." onkeypress="handleTextSubmit(event)">
            </div>
            
            <div class="mic-container">
                <div class="mic-button" id="master-mic-btn" onclick="toggleVoiceCapture()">
                    <svg id="mic-icon-svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                        <path d="M12 14c1.66 0 3-1.34 3-3V5c0-1.66-1.34-3-3-3S9 3.34 9 5v6c0 1.66 1.34 3 3 3zm5.3-3c0 3-2.54 5.1-5.3 5.1S6.7 14 6.7 11H5c0 3.41 2.72 6.23 6 6.72V21h2v-3.28c3.28-.48 6-3.3 6-6.72h-1.7z"/>
                    </svg>
                </div>
                <div class="pulse-ring"></div>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="hint-text">SAY "HI ACE" OR HIT GLOBAL ENTER TO SPEAK // USER: ARYAN</div>

    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/three.js/r128/three.min.js"></script>
    <script>
        let scene, camera, renderer, starParticles, orbMesh, orbGlow;
        let recognition;
        let isListeningMode = false;

        // 🎙️ HTML5 WEB AUDIO MATRIX REGISTERS
        let audioContext, audioAnalyser, audioDataArray;
        let liveMicrophoneAmplitude = 0.0;

        // 🌌 THREE.JS SCENE PROTOCOLS
        function initSpaceScene() {
            const container = document.getElementById('canvas-container');
            
            scene = new THREE.Scene();
            camera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(60, window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight, 0.1, 1000);
            camera.position.z = 5;

            renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({ antialias: true, alpha: false });
            renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
            renderer.setPixelRatio(window.devicePixelRatio);
            container.appendChild(renderer.domElement);

            const starGeometry = new THREE.BufferGeometry();
            const starCount = 1200;
            const starPositions = new Float32Array(starCount * 3);
            for(let i=0; i < starCount * 3; i++) {
                starPositions[i] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 15;
            }
            starGeometry.setAttribute('position', new THREE.BufferAttribute(starPositions, 3));
            const starMaterial = new THREE.PointsMaterial({ color: 0xffffff, size: 0.02, transparent: true, opacity: 0.8 });
            starParticles = new THREE.Points(starGeometry, starMaterial);
            scene.add(starParticles);

            const orbGeometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.6, 64, 64);
            const orbMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color: 0x2DD4A8 });
            orbMesh = new THREE.Mesh(orbGeometry, orbMaterial);
            scene.add(orbMesh);

            const glowGeometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.8, 32, 32);
            const glowMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color: 0x2DD4A8, transparent: true, opacity: 0.25, side: THREE.BackSide });
            orbGlow = new THREE.Mesh(glowGeometry, glowMaterial);
            scene.add(orbGlow);

            window.addEventListener('resize', onWindowResize);
            document.addEventListener('keydown', handleGlobalKeydown);

            // Launch Unified Speech Matrix and Request Hardware Accel Audio
            initUnifiedSpeechEngine();
            initHardwareAudioAnalyzer();
            animateLoop();
        }

        // 🎛️ REAL-TIME HARDWARE ACOUSTIC TRACKER
        function initHardwareAudioAnalyzer() {
            navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ audio: true })
            .then(stream => {
                const AudioContextClass = window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext;
                audioContext = new AudioContextClass();
                const sourceNode = audioContext.createMediaStreamSource(stream);
                
                audioAnalyser = audioContext.createAnalyser();
                audioAnalyser.fftSize = 256; // Fast Fourier Transform window sizing
                
                const bufferLength = audioAnalyser.frequencyBinCount;
                audioDataArray = new Uint8Array(bufferLength);
                
                sourceNode.connect(audioAnalyser);
                console.log("🔒 Audio Link Established: Hardware hardware visual metrics active.");
            })
            .catch(err => {
                console.log("⚠️ Audio Analyzer hardware permission deferred until manual toggle event:", err);
            });
        }

        function animateLoop() {
            requestAnimationFrame(animateLoop);
            const time = Date.now() * 0.001;

            // 1) Idle Breathing Cosine Baseline Loop (~4s)
            let breathingFactor = Math.sin(time * 1.5) * 0.04;
            
            // 2) Parse Live Audio Frequencies from Node Arrays
            if (audioAnalyser && audioDataArray) {
                audioAnalyser.getByteFrequencyData(audioDataArray);
                let totalFrequencySum = 0;
                for (let i = 0; i < audioDataArray.length; i++) {
                    totalFrequencySum += audioDataArray[i];
                }
                // Calculate average volume amplitude (Scale from 0.0 to 1.0 context values)
                let calculatedAverage = totalFrequencySum / audioDataArray.length;
                let targetAmplitude = calculatedAverage / 128.0; // Normalized factor map
                
                // Interpolate movement smoothly to remove visual jittering
                liveMicrophoneAmplitude += (targetAmplitude - liveMicrophoneAmplitude) * 0.2;
            }

            // 3) Apply Merged Transform Scale Targets to the Core Orb Structures
            // The orb expands up to 2.2x its original footprint during spike audio surges
            let finalScalingFactor = 1.0 + breathingFactor + (liveMicrophoneAmplitude * 1.2);
            
            if (orbMesh) orbMesh.scale.set(finalScalingFactor, finalScalingFactor, finalScalingFactor);
            if (orbGlow) orbGlow.scale.set(finalScalingFactor * 1.25, finalScalingFactor * 1.25, finalScalingFactor * 1.25);
            
            if (starParticles) starParticles.rotation.y = time * 0.02;
            renderer.render(scene, camera);
        }

        function onWindowResize() {
            camera.aspect = window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight;
            camera.updateProjectionMatrix();
            renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
        }

        // 🎙️ UNIFIED SPEECH RECOGNITION PERSISTENT CORE
        function initUnifiedSpeechEngine() {
            if (!('webkitSpeechRecognition' in window) && !('SpeechRecognition' in window)) {
                appendResponseCard("Hardware Alert", "Speech recognition structures not supported in browser environment.");
                return;
            }

            const SpeechRecognition = window.SpeechRecognition || window.webkitSpeechRecognition;
            recognition = new SpeechRecognition();
            recognition.continuous = true;
            recognition.interimResults = false;
            recognition.lang = 'en-US';

            recognition.onresult = (event) => {
                const lastIndex = event.resultIndex;
                const transcript = event.results[lastIndex][0].transcript.trim();
                const transcriptLower = transcript.toLowerCase();
                
                if (isListeningMode) {
                    postCommandToBackend(transcript);
                    switchToAmbientMode();
                } else {
                    if (transcriptLower.includes("hi ace")) {
                        let triggerIndex = transcriptLower.indexOf("hi ace") + 6;
                        let trailingCommand = transcript.substring(triggerIndex).trim();
                        
                        if (trailingCommand.length > 0) {
                            postCommandToBackend(trailingCommand);
                        } else {
                            switchToActiveListeningMode();
                        }
                    }
                }
            };

            recognition.onerror = (e) => {
                if(e.error === 'not-allowed' && audioContext) {
                    // Prompt immediate reactivation loops if state gets locked down
                    initHardwareAudioAnalyzer();
                }
            };

            recognition.onend = () => { recognition.start(); };
            recognition.start();
        }

        function switchToActiveListeningMode() {
            isListeningMode = true;
            // Force resume the audio context context state mapping if the browser suspended it
            if (audioContext && audioContext.state === 'suspended') {
                audioContext.resume();
            }
            const btn = document.getElementById('master-mic-btn');
            const svgIcon = document.getElementById('mic-icon-svg');
            if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
            updateSystemUIState("listening");
            if (svgIcon) svgIcon.innerHTML = `<rect x="6" y="6" width="12" height="12"/>`;
        }

        function switchToAmbientMode() {
            isListeningMode = false;
            const btn = document.getElementById('master-mic-btn');
            const svgIcon = document.getElementById('mic-icon-svg');
            if (btn) btn.classList.remove('active');
            updateSystemUIState("idle");
            if (svgIcon) svgIcon.innerHTML = `<path d="M12 14c1.66 0 3-1.34 3-3V5c0-1.66-1.34-3-3-3S9 3.34 9 5v6c0 1.66 1.34 3 3 3zm5.3-3c0 3-2.54 5.1-5.3 5.1S6.7 14 6.7 11H5c0 3.41 2.72 6.23 6 6.72V21h2v-3.28c3.28-.48 6-3.3 6-6.72h-1.7z"/>`;
        }

        function toggleVoiceCapture() {
            if (!isListeningMode) {
                switchToActiveListeningMode();
            } else {
                switchToAmbientMode();
            }
        }

        // ⌨️ INPUT INTERACTION ENTRY HANDLERS
        function handleGlobalKeydown(event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter' && document.activeElement !== document.getElementById('chat-entry')) {
                event.preventDefault();
                toggleVoiceCapture();
            }
        }

        function handleTextSubmit(event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter') {
                const inputElement = document.getElementById('chat-entry');
                const commandText = inputElement.value.trim();
                if (!commandText) return;
                inputElement.value = "";
                postCommandToBackend(commandText);
            }
        }

        // ⚡ WEB DATA EXCHANGE PIPELINE
        function postCommandToBackend(payloadText) {
            updateSystemUIState("processing");
            appendResponseCard("User Request", payloadText);

            fetch('/api/command', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ command: payloadText })
            })
            .then(res => res.json())
            .then(data => {
                updateSystemUIState("idle");
                
                if (typeof data.response === 'object') {
                    if(data.response.contrarian) appendResponseCard("🎭 The Contrarian", data.response.contrarian);
                    if(data.response.synergist) appendResponseCard("🚀 The Synergist", data.response.synergist);
                    if(data.response.chairman) appendResponseCard("🏛️ The Chairman Summary", data.response.chairman);
                } else {
                    appendResponseCard("Ace Intelligence", data.response);
                }
            })
            .catch(err => {
                updateSystemUIState("idle");
                appendResponseCard("System Error", "Could not negotiate data exchange execution.");
            });
        }

        function triggerMapModule() {
            appendResponseCard("Tactical Map Matrix", "Initializing grid array scan layers... Local host framework layout verified nominal.");
        }

        function triggerAlertsModule() {
            appendResponseCard("Alerts Sub-Console", "All telemetry metrics currently reading nominal. Zero network intrusion profiles detected.");
        }

        function updateSystemUIState(state) {
            const text = document.getElementById('system-status-text');
            const dot = document.getElementById('global-status-dot');
            if (!dot) return;
            dot.className = "status-dot";
            
            if(state === "listening") { if(text) text.innerText = "LISTENING"; dot.classList.add('listening'); }
            else if(state === "processing") { if(text) text.innerText = "PROCESSING"; dot.classList.add('processing'); }
            else { if(text) text.innerText = "ONLINE"; }
        }

        function appendResponseCard(speaker, message) {
            const stack = document.getElementById('response-stack');
            const card = document.createElement('div');
            card.className = 'response-card';
            card.innerHTML = `<div class="speaker-tag">${speaker}</div><div>${message}</div>`;
            
            if(stack.children.length >= 3) stack.removeChild(stack.children[0]);
            stack.appendChild(card);
        }

        function togglePanel() {
            document.getElementById('activity-panel').classList.toggle('collapsed');
        }

        window.onload = initSpaceScene;
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <div id="canvas-container"></div>

    <header class="glass-panel">
        <div class="wordmark">ACE<span>.</span></div>
        <div class="header-right">
            <button class="ghost-btn" onclick="triggerMapModule()">MAP</button>
            <button class="ghost-btn" onclick="triggerAlertsModule()">ALERTS</button>
            <div class="status-container">
                <span id="system-status-text">ONLINE</span>
                <div id="global-status-dot" class="status-dot"></div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </header>

    <div id="response-stack">
        <div class="response-card" id="welcome-card">
            <div class="speaker-tag">System Core</div>
            Console engine online, Aryan. Ambient system listening matrix fully synchronized.
        </div>
    </div>

    <div id="activity-panel" class="glass-panel">
        <div class="panel-toggle" onclick="togglePanel()">🗲</div>
        <div class="panel-content" id="panel-content-area">
            <div>
                <div class="section-header">INBOX REPLIES <span>0</span></div>
            </div>
            <div>
                <div class="section-header">SCOUT TASKS <span>READY</span></div>
                <div class="panel-entry">Neural path verified.</div>
            </div>
            <div>
                <div class="section-header">FLUX SEGMENTS <span>ACTIVE</span></div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <div id="control-dock">
        <div class="interactive-elements">
            <div class="chat-input-wrapper">
                <input type="text" id="chat-entry" placeholder="Send manual system execution command..." onkeypress="handleTextSubmit(event)">
            </div>
            
            <div class="mic-container">
                <div class="mic-button" id="master-mic-btn" onclick="toggleVoiceCapture()">
                    <svg id="mic-icon-svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                        <path d="M12 14c1.66 0 3-1.34 3-3V5c0-1.66-1.34-3-3-3S9 3.34 9 5v6c0 1.66 1.34 3 3 3zm5.3-3c0 3-2.54 5.1-5.3 5.1S6.7 14 6.7 11H5c0 3.41 2.72 6.23 6 6.72V21h2v-3.28c3.28-.48 6-3.3 6-6.72h-1.7z"/>
                    </svg>
                </div>
                <div class="pulse-ring"></div>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="hint-text">HI ACE / HEY ACE / WAKE UP ACE / OK ACE // USER: ARYAN</div>
    </div>

    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/three.js/r128/three.min.js"></script>
    <script>
        let scene, camera, renderer, starParticles, orbMesh, orbGlow;
        let recognition;
        let isListeningMode = false;

        let audioContext, audioAnalyser, audioDataArray;
        let liveMicrophoneAmplitude = 0.0;

        // 🌌 THREE.JS SCENE PROTOCOLS
        function initSpaceScene() {
            const container = document.getElementById('canvas-container');
            
            scene = new THREE.Scene();
            camera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(60, window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight, 0.1, 1000);
            camera.position.z = 5;

            renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({ antialias: true, alpha: false });
            renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
            renderer.setPixelRatio(window.devicePixelRatio);
            container.appendChild(renderer.domElement);

            const starGeometry = new THREE.BufferGeometry();
            const starCount = 1200;
            const starPositions = new Float32Array(starCount * 3);
            for(let i=0; i < starCount * 3; i++) {
                starPositions[i] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 15;
            }
            starGeometry.setAttribute('position', new THREE.BufferAttribute(starPositions, 3));
            const starMaterial = new THREE.PointsMaterial({ color: 0xffffff, size: 0.02, transparent: true, opacity: 0.8 });
            starParticles = new THREE.Points(starGeometry, starMaterial);
            scene.add(starParticles);

            const orbGeometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.6, 64, 64);
            const orbMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color: 0x2DD4A8 });
            orbMesh = new THREE.Mesh(orbGeometry, orbMaterial);
            scene.add(orbMesh);

            const glowGeometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.8, 32, 32);
            const glowMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color: 0x2DD4A8, transparent: true, opacity: 0.25, side: THREE.BackSide });
            orbGlow = new THREE.Mesh(glowGeometry, glowMaterial);
            scene.add(orbGlow);

            window.addEventListener('resize', onWindowResize);
            document.addEventListener('keydown', handleGlobalKeydown);

            initUnifiedSpeechEngine();
            initHardwareAudioAnalyzer();
            animateLoop();
        }

        function initHardwareAudioAnalyzer() {
            navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ audio: true })
            .then(stream => {
                const AudioContextClass = window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext;
                audioContext = new AudioContextClass();
                const sourceNode = audioContext.createMediaStreamSource(stream);
                
                audioAnalyser = audioContext.createAnalyser();
                audioAnalyser.fftSize = 256;
                
                const bufferLength = audioAnalyser.frequencyBinCount;
                audioDataArray = new Uint8Array(bufferLength);
                
                sourceNode.connect(audioAnalyser);
                console.log("🔒 Audio Link Established: Hardware visual metrics active.");
            })
            .catch(err => {
                console.log("⚠️ Audio Analyzer hardware link delayed:", err);
            });
        }

        function animateLoop() {
            requestAnimationFrame(animateLoop);
            const time = Date.now() * 0.001;

            let breathingFactor = Math.sin(time * 1.5) * 0.04;
            
            if (audioAnalyser && audioDataArray) {
                audioAnalyser.getByteFrequencyData(audioDataArray);
                let totalFrequencySum = 0;
                for (let i = 0; i < audioDataArray.length; i++) {
                    totalFrequencySum += audioDataArray[i];
                }
                let calculatedAverage = totalFrequencySum / audioDataArray.length;
                let targetAmplitude = calculatedAverage / 128.0;
                
                liveMicrophoneAmplitude += (targetAmplitude - liveMicrophoneAmplitude) * 0.2;
            }

            let finalScalingFactor = 1.0 + breathingFactor + (liveMicrophoneAmplitude * 1.2);
            
            if (orbMesh) orbMesh.scale.set(finalScalingFactor, finalScalingFactor, finalScalingFactor);
            if (orbGlow) orbGlow.scale.set(finalScalingFactor * 1.25, finalScalingFactor * 1.25, finalScalingFactor * 1.25);
            
            if (starParticles) starParticles.rotation.y = time * 0.02;
            renderer.render(scene, camera);
        }

        function onWindowResize() {
            camera.aspect = window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight;
            camera.updateProjectionMatrix();
            renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
        }

        // 🎙️ UNIFIED SPEECH RECOGNITION PERSISTENT CORE
        function initUnifiedSpeechEngine() {
            if (!('webkitSpeechRecognition' in window) && !('SpeechRecognition' in window)) {
                appendResponseCard("Hardware Alert", "Speech recognition structures not supported.");
                return;
            }

            const SpeechRecognition = window.SpeechRecognition || window.webkitSpeechRecognition;
            recognition = new SpeechRecognition();
            recognition.continuous = true;
            recognition.interimResults = false;
            recognition.lang = 'en-US';

            recognition.onresult = (event) => {
                const lastIndex = event.resultIndex;
                const transcript = event.results[lastIndex][0].transcript.trim();
                const transcriptLower = transcript.toLowerCase();
                
                console.log("Speech text matrix token:", transcript);

                // PATHWAY 1: ACTIVE LISTEN MODE
                if (isListeningMode) {
                    postCommandToBackend(transcript);
                    switchToAmbientMode();
                } 
                // PATHWAY 2: PASSIVE MULTI-WAKE WORD LOOKUP MATRIX
                else {
                    const functionalTriggers = ["hi ace", "hey ace", "wake up ace", "ok ace"];
                    let targetTriggerMatch = null;
                    
                    for (let trigger of functionalTriggers) {
                        if (transcriptLower.includes(trigger)) {
                            targetTriggerMatch = trigger;
                            break;
                        }
                    }

                    if (targetTriggerMatch) {
                        // Locate bounds of the matched trigger string token
                        let triggerPosition = transcriptLower.indexOf(targetTriggerMatch) + targetTriggerMatch.length;
                        let isolatedTrailingCommand = transcript.substring(triggerPosition).trim();
                        
                        if (isolatedTrailingCommand.length > 0) {
                            // User issued wake phrase and structural task prompt inline seamlessly
                            postCommandToBackend(isolatedTrailingCommand);
                        } else {
                            // Wake phrase captured in isolation, prompt full listen mode shift
                            switchToActiveListeningMode();
                        }
                    }
                }
            };

            recognition.onerror = (e) => {
                if(e.error === 'not-allowed' && audioContext) {
                    initHardwareAudioAnalyzer();
                }
            };

            recognition.onend = () => { recognition.start(); };
            recognition.start();
        }

        function switchToActiveListeningMode() {
            isListeningMode = true;
            if (audioContext && audioContext.state === 'suspended') {
                audioContext.resume();
            }
            const btn = document.getElementById('master-mic-btn');
            const svgIcon = document.getElementById('mic-icon-svg');
            if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
            updateSystemUIState("listening");
            if (svgIcon) svgIcon.innerHTML = `<rect x="6" y="6" width="12" height="12"/>`;
        }

        function switchToAmbientMode() {
            isListeningMode = false;
            const btn = document.getElementById('master-mic-btn');
            const svgIcon = document.getElementById('mic-icon-svg');
            if (btn) btn.classList.remove('active');
            updateSystemUIState("idle");
            if (svgIcon) svgIcon.innerHTML = `<path d="M12 14c1.66 0 3-1.34 3-3V5c0-1.66-1.34-3-3-3S9 3.34 9 5v6c0 1.66 1.34 3 3 3zm5.3-3c0 3-2.54 5.1-5.3 5.1S6.7 14 6.7 11H5c0 3.41 2.72 6.23 6 6.72V21h2v-3.28c3.28-.48 6-3.3 6-6.72h-1.7z"/>`;
        }

        function toggleVoiceCapture() {
            if (!isListeningMode) {
                switchToActiveListeningMode();
            } else {
                switchToAmbientMode();
            }
        }

        // ⌨️ INPUT INTERACTION HANDLERS
        function handleGlobalKeydown(event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter' && document.activeElement !== document.getElementById('chat-entry')) {
                event.preventDefault();
                toggleVoiceCapture();
            }
        }

        function handleTextSubmit(event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter') {
                const inputElement = document.getElementById('chat-entry');
                const commandText = inputElement.value.trim();
                if (!commandText) return;
                inputElement.value = "";
                postCommandToBackend(commandText);
            }
        }

        // ⚡ WEB DATA EXCHANGE PIPELINE
        function postCommandToBackend(payloadText) {
            updateSystemUIState("processing");
            appendResponseCard("User Request", payloadText);

            fetch('/api/command', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ command: payloadText })
            })
            .then(res => res.json())
            .then(data => {
                updateSystemUIState("idle");
                
                if (typeof data.response === 'object') {
                    if(data.response.contrarian) appendResponseCard("🎭 The Contrarian", data.response.contrarian);
                    if(data.response.synergist) appendResponseCard("🚀 The Synergist", data.response.synergist);
                    if(data.response.chairman) appendResponseCard("🏛️ The Chairman Summary", data.response.chairman);
                } else {
                    appendResponseCard("Ace Intelligence", data.response);
                }
            })
            .catch(err => {
                updateSystemUIState("idle");
                appendResponseCard("System Error", "Could not negotiate data exchange execution.");
            });
        }

        function triggerMapModule() {
            appendResponseCard("Tactical Map Matrix", "Initializing grid array scan layers... Local host framework layout verified nominal.");
        }

        function triggerAlertsModule() {
            appendResponseCard("Alerts Sub-Console", "All telemetry metrics currently reading nominal. Zero network intrusion profiles detected.");
        }

        function updateSystemUIState(state) {
            const text = document.getElementById('system-status-text');
            const dot = document.getElementById('global-status-dot');
            if (!dot) return;
            dot.className = "status-dot";
            
            if(state === "listening") { if(text) text.innerText = "LISTENING"; dot.classList.add('listening'); }
            else if(state === "processing") { if(text) text.innerText = "PROCESSING"; dot.classList.add('processing'); }
            else { if(text) text.innerText = "ONLINE"; }
        }

        function appendResponseCard(speaker, message) {
            const stack = document.getElementById('response-stack');
            const card = document.createElement('div');
            card.className = 'response-card';
            card.innerHTML = `<div class="speaker-tag">${speaker}</div><div>${message}</div>`;
            
            if(stack.children.length >= 3) stack.removeChild(stack.children[0]);
            stack.appendChild(card);
        }

        function togglePanel() {
            document.getElementById('activity-panel').classList.toggle('collapsed');
        }

        window.onload = initSpaceScene;
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/three.js/r128/three.min.js"></script>
    <script>
        let scene, camera, renderer, starParticles, orbMesh, orbGlow;
        let recognition;
        let isListeningMode = false;

        let audioContext, audioAnalyser, audioDataArray;
        let liveMicrophoneAmplitude = 0.0;

        // THREE.JS SCENE PROTOCOLS
        function initSpaceScene() {
            const container = document.getElementById('canvas-container');
            
            scene = new THREE.Scene();
            camera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(60, window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight, 0.1, 1000);
            camera.position.z = 5;

            renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({ antialias: true, alpha: false });
            renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
            renderer.setPixelRatio(window.devicePixelRatio);
            container.appendChild(renderer.domElement);

            const starGeometry = new THREE.BufferGeometry();
            const starCount = 1200;
            const starPositions = new Float32Array(starCount * 3);
            for(let i=0; i < starCount * 3; i++) {
                starPositions[i] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 15;
            }
            starGeometry.setAttribute('position', new THREE.BufferAttribute(starPositions, 3));
            const starMaterial = new THREE.PointsMaterial({ color: 0xffffff, size: 0.02, transparent: true, opacity: 0.8 });
            starParticles = new THREE.Points(starGeometry, starMaterial);
            scene.add(starParticles);

            const orbGeometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.6, 64, 64);
            const orbMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color: 0x2DD4A8 });
            orbMesh = new THREE.Mesh(orbGeometry, orbMaterial);
            scene.add(orbMesh);

            const glowGeometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.8, 32, 32);
            const glowMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color: 0x2DD4A8, transparent: true, opacity: 0.25, side: THREE.BackSide });
            orbGlow = new THREE.Mesh(glowGeometry, glowMaterial);
            scene.add(orbGlow);

            window.addEventListener('resize', onWindowResize);
            document.addEventListener('keydown', handleGlobalKeydown);

            initUnifiedSpeechEngine();
            initHardwareAudioAnalyzer();
            animateLoop();
        }

        function initHardwareAudioAnalyzer() {
            navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ audio: true })
            .then(stream => {
                const AudioContextClass = window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext;
                audioContext = new AudioContextClass();
                const sourceNode = audioContext.createMediaStreamSource(stream);
                
                audioAnalyser = audioContext.createAnalyser();
                audioAnalyser.fftSize = 256;
                
                const bufferLength = audioAnalyser.frequencyBinCount;
                audioDataArray = new Uint8Array(bufferLength);
                
                sourceNode.connect(audioAnalyser);
            })
            .catch(err => {
                console.log("⚠️ Audio Analyzer hardware permission deferred until manual toggle event:", err);
            });
        }

        function animateLoop() {
            requestAnimationFrame(animateLoop);
            const time = Date.now() * 0.001;

            let breathingFactor = Math.sin(time * 1.5) * 0.04;
            
            if (audioAnalyser && audioDataArray) {
                audioAnalyser.getByteFrequencyData(audioDataArray);
                let totalFrequencySum = 0;
                for (let i = 0; i < audioDataArray.length; i++) {
                    totalFrequencySum += audioDataArray[i];
                }
                let calculatedAverage = totalFrequencySum / audioDataArray.length;
                let targetAmplitude = calculatedAverage / 128.0;
                
                liveMicrophoneAmplitude += (targetAmplitude - liveMicrophoneAmplitude) * 0.2;
            }

            let finalScalingFactor = 1.0 + breathingFactor + (liveMicrophoneAmplitude * 1.2);
            
            if (orbMesh) orbMesh.scale.set(finalScalingFactor, finalScalingFactor, finalScalingFactor);
            if (orbGlow) orbGlow.scale.set(finalScalingFactor * 1.25, finalScalingFactor * 1.25, finalScalingFactor * 1.25);
            
            if (starParticles) starParticles.rotation.y = time * 0.02;
            renderer.render(scene, camera);
        }

        function onWindowResize() {
            camera.aspect = window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight;
            camera.updateProjectionMatrix();
            renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
        }

        // UNIFIED SPEECH RECOGNITION PERSISTENT CORE
        function initUnifiedSpeechEngine() {
            if (!('webkitSpeechRecognition' in window) && !('SpeechRecognition' in window)) {
                appendResponseCard("Hardware Alert", "Speech recognition structures not supported.");
                return;
            }

            const SpeechRecognition = window.SpeechRecognition || window.webkitSpeechRecognition;
            recognition = new SpeechRecognition();
            recognition.continuous = true;
            recognition.interimResults = false;
            recognition.lang = 'en-US';

            recognition.onresult = (event) => {
                const lastIndex = event.resultIndex;
                const transcript = event.results[lastIndex][0].transcript.trim();
                const transcriptLower = transcript.toLowerCase();
                
                // Explicitly tags outbound voice payload flags
                if (isListeningMode) {
                    postCommandToBackend(transcript, 'voice');
                    switchToAmbientMode();
                } 
                else {
                    const functionalTriggers = ["hi ace", "hey ace", "wake up ace", "ok ace"];
                    let targetTriggerMatch = null;
                    
                    for (let trigger of functionalTriggers) {
                        if (transcriptLower.includes(trigger)) {
                            targetTriggerMatch = trigger;
                            break;
                        }
                    }

                    if (targetTriggerMatch) {
                        let triggerPosition = transcriptLower.indexOf(targetTriggerMatch) + targetTriggerMatch.length;
                        let isolatedTrailingCommand = transcript.substring(triggerPosition).trim();
                        
                        if (isolatedTrailingCommand.length > 0) {
                            postCommandToBackend(isolatedTrailingCommand, 'voice');
                        } else {
                            switchToActiveListeningMode();
                        }
                    }
                }
            };

            recognition.onerror = (e) => {
                if(e.error === 'not-allowed' && audioContext) {
                    initHardwareAudioAnalyzer();
                }
            };

            recognition.onend = () => { recognition.start(); };
            recognition.start();
        }

        function switchToActiveListeningMode() {
            isListeningMode = true;
            if (audioContext && audioContext.state === 'suspended') {
                audioContext.resume();
            }
            const btn = document.getElementById('master-mic-btn');
            const svgIcon = document.getElementById('mic-icon-svg');
            if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
            updateSystemUIState("listening");
            if (svgIcon) svgIcon.innerHTML = `<rect x="6" y="6" width="12" height="12"/>`;
        }

        function switchToAmbientMode() {
            isListeningMode = false;
            const btn = document.getElementById('master-mic-btn');
            const svgIcon = document.getElementById('mic-icon-svg');
            if (btn) btn.classList.remove('active');
            updateSystemUIState("idle");
            if (svgIcon) svgIcon.innerHTML = `<path d="M12 14c1.66 0 3-1.34 3-3V5c0-1.66-1.34-3-3-3S9 3.34 9 5v6c0 1.66 1.34 3 3 3zm5.3-3c0 3-2.54 5.1-5.3 5.1S6.7 14 6.7 11H5c0 3.41 2.72 6.23 6 6.72V21h2v-3.28c3.28-.48 6-3.3 6-6.72h-1.7z"/>`;
        }

        function toggleVoiceCapture() {
            if (!isListeningMode) {
                switchToActiveListeningMode();
            } else {
                switchToAmbientMode();
            }
        }

        function handleGlobalKeydown(event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter' && document.activeElement !== document.getElementById('chat-entry')) {
                event.preventDefault();
                toggleVoiceCapture();
            }
        }

        function handleTextSubmit(event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter') {
                const inputElement = document.getElementById('chat-entry');
                const commandText = inputElement.value.trim();
                if (!commandText) return;
                inputElement.value = "";
                // Explicitly tags outbound text payload flags
                postCommandToBackend(commandText, 'text');
            }
        }

        // WEB DATA EXCHANGE PIPELINE
        function postCommandToBackend(payloadText, source) {
            updateSystemUIState("processing");
            appendResponseCard(source === 'voice' ? "Aryan (Voice)" : "Aryan (Keyboard)", payloadText);

            fetch('/api/command', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ command: payloadText, source: source })
            })
            .then(res => res.json())
            .then(data => {
                updateSystemUIState("idle");
                
                if (typeof data.response === 'object') {
                    if(data.response.contrarian) appendResponseCard("🎭 The Contrarian", data.response.contrarian);
                    if(data.response.synergist) appendResponseCard("🚀 The Synergist", data.response.synergist);
                    if(data.response.chairman) appendResponseCard("🏛️ The Chairman Summary", data.response.chairman);
                } else {
                    appendResponseCard("Ace Intelligence", data.response);
                }
            })
            .catch(err => {
                updateSystemUIState("idle");
                appendResponseCard("System Error", "Could not negotiate data exchange execution.");
            });
        }

        function triggerMapModule() {
            appendResponseCard("Tactical Map Matrix", "Initializing grid scan layers... Active path nominal.");
        }

        function triggerAlertsModule() {
            appendResponseCard("Alerts Sub-Console", "Telemetry reading nominal. Zero network intrusion profiles detected.");
        }

        function updateSystemUIState(state) {
            const text = document.getElementById('system-status-text');
            const dot = document.getElementById('global-status-dot');
            if (!dot) return;
            dot.className = "status-dot";
            
            if(state === "listening") { if(text) text.innerText = "LISTENING"; dot.classList.add('listening'); }
            else if(state === "processing") { if(text) text.innerText = "PROCESSING"; dot.classList.add('processing'); }
            else { if(text) text.innerText = "ONLINE"; }
        }

        function appendResponseCard(speaker, message) {
            const stack = document.getElementById('response-stack');
            const card = document.createElement('div');
            card.className = 'response-card';
            card.innerHTML = `<div class="speaker-tag">${speaker}</div><div>${message}</div>`;
            
            if(stack.children.length >= 3) stack.removeChild(stack.children[0]);
            stack.appendChild(card);
        }

        function togglePanel() {
            document.getElementById('activity-panel').classList.toggle('collapsed');
        }

        window.onload = initSpaceScene;
    </script>
</body>
</html>


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
import os
import sys
import threading
import time
import ollama

# Import your locked, functional core speech assets
from audio_provider import speak_text
from council import run_council_debate

app = Flask(__name__)

# 🤖 THE HYBRID ENGINE DECK REGISTERED WITH LOCAL SYSTEM TAGS
FAST_MODEL = "llama3.2:1b"
SMART_MODEL = "qwen2.5-coder:latest"

# Storage array for state processing history memory loads
chat_history = []

def should_trigger_council(text):
    """Its primary utility is to prevent false-positives when trigger words are in a negative context."""
    text_lower = text.lower()
    triggers = ["council", "debate", "evaluate"]
    negations = ["don't", "dont", "do not", "never", "without", "skip", "stop"]
    
    if not any(kw in text_lower for kw in triggers):
        return False
        
    for neg in negations:
        if neg in text_lower:
            for kw in triggers:
                if kw in text_lower and text_lower.find(neg) < text_lower.find(kw):
                    return False
    return True

@app.route('/')
def serve_dashboard_console():
    """Serves index.html directly into local browser sessions."""
    try:
        with open('index.html', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            return f.read()
    except Exception as e:
        return f"System Matrix Failure: Could not locate index.html framework. Error: {e}"

@app.route('/api/command', methods=['POST'])
def orchestrate_command_routing():
    """Main routing engine gateway for processing input command payloads."""
    global chat_history
    data = request.get_json() or {}
    command = data.get('command', '').strip()
    source = data.get('source', 'text') # Extract interaction origin vector tracking flag
    
    if not command:
        return jsonify({"response": "Empty vector transaction payload abandoned."})
        
    print(f"\n📥 Transaction received from [{source.upper()}]: \"{command}\"")

    # CASE A: MULTI-AGENT COUNCIL ROUTING PATHWAY
    if should_trigger_council(command):
        print("👥 Assembling Council Matrix Boardroom Core...")
        debate_packet = run_council_debate(command)
        
        # Deploy a non-blocking background thread to narrate ONLY if triggered via voice interface
        if source == 'voice':
            def narrate_council():
                speak_text("Analyzing the risk layout from the contrarian.")
                speak_text(debate_packet['contrarian'])
                time.sleep(0.3)
                speak_text("Reviewing the strategy modification from the synergist.")
                speak_text(debate_packet['synergist'])
                time.sleep(0.3)
                speak_text("The chairman's final evaluation and takeaways.")
                speak_text(debate_packet['chairman'])
            threading.Thread(target=narrate_council, daemon=True).start()
        else:
            print("📝 Council assembly executed silently via typed terminal override.")

        return jsonify({"response": debate_packet})

    # CASE B: CONTEXTUAL CHAT ROUTING PATHWAY
    else:
        text_lower = command.lower()
        if "think deeply" in text_lower or "smart mode" in text_lower or "analyze" in text_lower:
            active_model = SMART_MODEL
            print(f"🧠 Escalating layer -> routing through {active_model}")
        else:
            active_model = FAST_MODEL
            print(f"⚡ Pacing layer optimally -> routing through {active_model}")

        # Construct short-term payload arrays with high-priority brevity rules injected
        messages_payload = [
            {
                "role": "system", 
                "content": (
                    "You are Ace, an elite desktop Jarvis-style AI assistant for Aryan. "
                    "CRITICAL DIRECTIVE: Keep all responses extremely concise, brief, and to the point. "
                    "Do not include pleasantries, conversational filler, or introductions. Provide direct data immediately."
                )
            }
        ]
        messages_payload.extend(chat_history)
        messages_payload.append({"role": "user", "content": command})

        try:
            response = ollama.chat(model=active_model, messages=messages_payload)
            reply = response['message']['content']
            
            chat_history.append({"role": "user", "content": command})
            chat_history.append({"role": "assistant", "content": reply})
            
            if len(chat_history) > 20:
                chat_history = chat_history[-20:]

            # Audio routing gatekeeper: triggers speech processing thread ONLY for oral pathways
            if source == 'voice':
                threading.Thread(target=lambda: speak_text(reply), daemon=True).start()
            else:
                print("🔇 Text payload detected. Vocal feedback engine bypassed.")

            return jsonify({"response": reply})

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"❌ Ollama execution link exception dropped: {e}")
            return jsonify({"response": f"Core framework loop failed transaction routing link safely: {e}"})

if __name__ == '__main__':
    print("\n========================================================")
    print(" 🔥 ACE CORE SERVER: RUNNING AT http://127.0.0.1:5000")
    print("========================================================\n")
    app.run(host='0.0.0.0', port=5000, debug=False)

from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
import os
import sys
import threading
import time
import ollama

# Import your locked, functional core speech assets
from audio_provider import speak_text
from council import run_council_debate

def should_trigger_council(text):
    """Prevents false-positives when trigger words are in a negative context."""
    text_lower = text.lower()
    triggers = ["council", "debate", "evaluate"]
    negations = ["don't", "dont", "do not", "never", "without", "skip", "stop"]

        return False
        
    for neg in negations:

            for kw in triggers:
                if kw in text_lower and text_lower.find(neg) < text_lower.find(kw):
                    return False
    return True

def execute_audio_playback(text_to_speak):
    """Safely runs speech playback inside an isolated thread with strict error logging."""
    try:
        print(f"🔊 [Audio Engine: Vocalizing response via system hardware...]")
        speak_text(text_to_speak)
        print(f"✅ [Audio Engine: Playback transaction complete.]")
    except Exception as tts_error:
        print(f"❌ [Audio Engine Crash]: Failed to play voice in background thread. Reason: {tts_error}")

        if source == 'voice':
            def narrate_council():
                execute_audio_playback("Analyzing the risk layout from the contrarian.")
                execute_audio_playback(debate_packet['contrarian'])
                time.sleep(0.3)
                execute_audio_playback("Reviewing the strategy modification from the synergist.")
                execute_audio_playback(debate_packet['synergist'])
                time.sleep(0.3)
                execute_audio_playback("The chairman's final evaluation and takeaways.")
                execute_audio_playback(debate_packet['chairman'])
            threading.Thread(target=narrate_council, daemon=True).start()
        else:
            print("To override silence, use a vocal trigger phrase.")

        return jsonify({"response": debate_packet})

    # CASE B: CONTEXTUAL CHAT ROUTING PATHWAY
    else:
        text_lower = command.lower()
        if "think deeply" in text_lower or "smart mode" in text_lower or "analyze" in text_lower:
            active_model = SMART_MODEL
            print(f"🧠 Escalating layer -> routing through {active_model}")

            active_model = FAST_MODEL
            print(f"⚡ Pacing layer optimally -> routing through {active_model}")

            {

            }
        ]

        messages_payload.append({"role": "user", "content": command})

        try:
            response = ollama.chat(model=active_model, messages=messages_payload)
            reply = response['message']['content']
            
            chat_history.append({"role": "user", "content": command})
            chat_history.append({"role": "assistant", "content": reply})
            
            if len(chat_history) > 20:
                chat_history = chat_history[-20:]

            # Dynamic voice tracking gateway
            if source == 'voice':
                threading.Thread(target=execute_audio_playback, args=(reply,), daemon=True).start()
            else:
                print("静 [Mute System Activated]: Text payload routing used. Audio skipped.")

            return jsonify({"response": reply})

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"❌ Ollama execution link exception dropped: {e}")
            return jsonify({"response": f"Core framework loop failed transaction routing link safely: {e}"})

if __name__ == '__main__':

from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
import os
import sys
import threading
import time
import ollama

# Import your locked, functional core speech assets
from audio_provider import speak_text
from council import run_council_debate

SMART_MODEL = "qwen2.5-coder:latest"

# Storage array for state processing history memory loads

def should_trigger_council(text):
    """Prevents false-positives when trigger words are in a negative context."""
    text_lower = text.lower()
    triggers = ["council", "debate", "evaluate"]
    negations = ["don't", "dont", "do not", "never", "without", "skip", "stop"]

        return False
        
    for neg in negations:

            for kw in triggers:
                if kw in text_lower and text_lower.find(neg) < text_lower.find(kw):
                    return False
    return True

def execute_audio_playback(text_to_speak):
    """Safely initializes the Windows audio subsystem and runs voice generation inside Flask."""
    try:
        # 🔑 THE WIN32 COM LOCKPICK
        # If using standard Windows TTS, background threads require explicit COM initialization
        try:
            import pythoncom
            pythoncom.CoInitialize()
        except ImportError:
            pass # Engine skips if running on an alternative TTS environment
            
        print(f"🔊 [Audio Engine: Vocalizing response via system hardware...]")
        speak_text(text_to_speak)
        print(f"✅ [Audio Engine: Playback transaction complete.]")
    except Exception as tts_error:
        print(f"❌ [Audio Engine Crash]: Failed to play voice in background thread. Reason: {tts_error}")

    """Serves index.html directly into local browser sessions."""

            return f.read()
    except Exception as e:
        return f"System Matrix Failure: Could not locate index.html framework. Error: {e}"

        # Balances lightning speed, human syntax, and a smooth conversational persona
        messages_payload = [
            {
                "role": "system", 
                "content": (
                    "You are Ace, an authentic, highly intelligent desktop AI assistant customized for Aryan. "
                    "Speak with a natural, conversational, human-like cadence—with a touch of wit, like Jarvis. "
                    "Keep your responses very brief, concise, and scannable (maximum 2-3 sentences). "
                    "Do not dump random bullet points or robotic statistics unless directly requested by the user."
                )
            }
        ]
        messages_payload.extend(chat_history)
        messages_payload.append({"role": "user", "content": command})

        try:
            response = ollama.chat(model=active_model, messages=messages_payload)
            reply = response['message']['content']
            
            chat_history.append({"role": "user", "content": command})
            chat_history.append({"role": "assistant", "content": reply})
            
            if len(chat_history) > 20:
                chat_history = chat_history[-20:]

            # Safe audio deployment gateway
            if source == 'voice':
                threading.Thread(target=execute_audio_playback, args=(reply,), daemon=True).start()
            else:
                print("🔇 [Mute System Activated]: Text payload routing used. Audio skipped.")

            return jsonify({"response": reply})

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"❌ Ollama execution link exception dropped: {e}")
            return jsonify({"response": f"Core framework loop failed transaction routing link safely: {e}"})

if __name__ == '__main__':
    print("\n========================================================")

from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
import os
import sys
import threading
import time
import ollama

# Import your locked, functional core speech assets
from audio_provider import speak_text
from council import run_council_debate

app = Flask(__name__)

# 🤖 THE HYBRID ENGINE DECK REGISTERED WITH LOCAL SYSTEM TAGS
FAST_MODEL = "llama3.2:1b"
SMART_MODEL = "qwen2.5-coder:latest"

# Storage array for state processing history memory loads
chat_history = []

def should_trigger_council(text):
    """Prevents false-positives when trigger words are in a negative context."""
    text_lower = text.lower()
    triggers = ["council", "debate", "evaluate"]
    negations = ["don't", "dont", "do not", "never", "without", "skip", "stop"]
    
    if not any(kw in text_lower for kw in triggers):
        return False
        
    for neg in negations:
        if neg in text_lower:
            for kw in triggers:
                if kw in text_lower and text_lower.find(neg) < text_lower.find(kw):
                    return False
    return True

def execute_audio_playback(text_to_speak):
    """Safely initializes the Windows audio subsystem and runs voice generation inside Flask."""
    try:
        try:
            import pythoncom
            pythoncom.CoInitialize()
        except ImportError:
            pass
            
        print(f"🔊 [Audio Engine: Vocalizing response via system hardware...]")
        speak_text(text_to_speak)
        print(f"✅ [Audio Engine: Playback transaction complete.]")
    except Exception as tts_error:
        print(f"❌ [Audio Engine Crash]: Failed to play voice in background thread. Reason: {tts_error}")

@app.route('/')
def serve_dashboard_console():
    """Serves index.html directly into local browser sessions."""
    try:
        with open('index.html', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            return f.read()
    except Exception as e:
        return f"System Matrix Failure: Could not locate index.html framework. Error: {e}"

@app.route('/api/command', methods=['POST'])
def orchestrate_command_routing():
    """Main routing engine gateway for processing input command payloads."""
    global chat_history
    data = request.get_json() or {}
    command = data.get('command', '').strip()
    source = data.get('source', 'text')
    
    if not command:
        return jsonify({"response": "Empty vector transaction payload abandoned."})
        
    print(f"\n📥 Transaction received from [{source.upper()}]: \"{command}\"")

    # CASE A: MULTI-AGENT COUNCIL ROUTING PATHWAY
    if should_trigger_council(command):
        print("👥 Assembling Council Matrix Boardroom Core...")
        debate_packet = run_council_debate(command)
        
        if source == 'voice':
            def narrate_council():
                execute_audio_playback("Analyzing the risk layout from the contrarian.")
                execute_audio_playback(debate_packet['contrarian'])
                time.sleep(0.3)
                execute_audio_playback("Reviewing the strategy modification from the synergist.")
                execute_audio_playback(debate_packet['synergist'])
                time.sleep(0.3)
                execute_audio_playback("The chairman's final evaluation and takeaways.")
                execute_audio_playback(debate_packet['chairman'])
            threading.Thread(target=narrate_council, daemon=True).start()

        return jsonify({"response": debate_packet})

    # CASE B: CONTEXTUAL CHAT ROUTING PATHWAY
    else:
        text_lower = command.lower()
        if "think deeply" in text_lower or "smart mode" in text_lower or "analyze" in text_lower:
            active_model = SMART_MODEL
            print(f"🧠 Escalating layer -> routing through {active_model}")
        else:
            active_model = FAST_MODEL
            print(f"⚡ Pacing layer optimally -> routing through {active_model}")

        # 🧠 THE RE-TUNED BRIEF SYSTEM DIRECTIVE
        # Dynamically commands the model to cap output at 1-2 lines maximum.
        messages_payload = [
            {
                "role": "system", 
                "content": (
                    "You are Ace, an elite desktop AI assistant for Aryan, speaking with a witty, human cadence like Jarvis. "
                    "CRITICAL LENGTH DIRECTIVE: Keep your response extremely short and limited to only 1 or 2 sentences maximum (around a few lines of text total). "
                    "Get straight to the answer with zero conversational fluff, preambles, or filler introductions."
                )
            }
        ]
        messages_payload.extend(chat_history)
        messages_payload.append({"role": "user", "content": command})

        try:
            response = ollama.chat(model=active_model, messages=messages_payload)
            reply = response['message']['content']
            
            chat_history.append({"role": "user", "content": command})
            chat_history.append({"role": "assistant", "content": reply})
            
            if len(chat_history) > 20:
                chat_history = chat_history[-20:]

            # Safe audio deployment gateway
            if source == 'voice':
                threading.Thread(target=execute_audio_playback, args=(reply,), daemon=True).start()
            else:
                print("🔇 [Mute System Activated]: Text payload routing used. Audio skipped.")

            return jsonify({"response": reply})

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"❌ Ollama execution link exception dropped: {e}")
            return jsonify({"response": f"Core framework loop failed transaction routing link safely: {e}"})

if __name__ == '__main__':
    print("\n========================================================")
    print(" 🔥 ACE CORE SERVER: RUNNING AT http://127.0.0.1:5000")
    print("========================================================\n")
    app.run(host='0.0.0.0', port=5000, debug=False)

                    <svg id="mic-icon-svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
