    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/three.js/r128/three.min.js"></script>
    <script>
        let scene, camera, renderer, starParticles, orbMesh, orbGlow;
        let recognition;
        let isListeningMode = false; // Key flag: Controls continuous audio streaming states

        let audioContext, audioAnalyser, audioDataArray;
        let liveMicrophoneAmplitude = 0.0;

        // THREE.JS SCENE PROTOCOLS
        function initSpaceScene() {
            const container = document.getElementById('canvas-container');
            
            scene = new THREE.Scene();
            camera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(60, window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight, 0.1, 1000);
            camera.position.z = 5;

            renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({ antialias: true, alpha: false });
            renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
            renderer.setPixelRatio(window.devicePixelRatio);
            container.appendChild(renderer.domElement);

            const starGeometry = new THREE.BufferGeometry();
            const starCount = 1200;
            const starPositions = new Float32Array(starCount * 3);
            for(let i=0; i < starCount * 3; i++) {
                starPositions[i] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 15;
            }
            starGeometry.setAttribute('position', new THREE.BufferAttribute(starPositions, 3));
            const starMaterial = new THREE.PointsMaterial({ color: 0xffffff, size: 0.02, transparent: true, opacity: 0.8 });
            starParticles = new THREE.Points(starGeometry, starMaterial);
            scene.add(starParticles);

            const orbGeometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.6, 64, 64);
            const orbMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color: 0x2DD4A8 });
            orbMesh = new THREE.Mesh(orbGeometry, orbMaterial);
            scene.add(orbMesh);

            const glowGeometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.8, 32, 32);
            const glowMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color: 0x2DD4A8, transparent: true, opacity: 0.25, side: THREE.BackSide });
            orbGlow = new THREE.Mesh(glowGeometry, glowMaterial);
            scene.add(orbGlow);

            window.addEventListener('resize', onWindowResize);
            document.addEventListener('keydown', handleGlobalKeydown);

            initUnifiedSpeechEngine();
            initHardwareAudioAnalyzer();
            animateLoop();
        }

        function initHardwareAudioAnalyzer() {
            navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ audio: true })
            .then(stream => {
                const AudioContextClass = window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext;
                audioContext = new AudioContextClass();
                const sourceNode = audioContext.createMediaStreamSource(stream);
                audioAnalyser = audioContext.createAnalyser();
                audioAnalyser.fftSize = 256;
                const bufferLength = audioAnalyser.frequencyBinCount;
                audioDataArray = new Uint8Array(bufferLength);
                sourceNode.connect(audioAnalyser);
            })
            .catch(err => { console.log("⚠️ Audio Hardware analyzer block:", err); });
        }

        function animateLoop() {
            requestAnimationFrame(animateLoop);
            const time = Date.now() * 0.001;
            let breathingFactor = Math.sin(time * 1.5) * 0.04;
            
            if (audioAnalyser && audioDataArray) {
                audioAnalyser.getByteFrequencyData(audioDataArray);
                let totalFrequencySum = 0;
                for (let i = 0; i < audioDataArray.length; i++) { totalFrequencySum += audioDataArray[i]; }
                let calculatedAverage = totalFrequencySum / audioDataArray.length;
                let targetAmplitude = calculatedAverage / 128.0;
                liveMicrophoneAmplitude += (targetAmplitude - liveMicrophoneAmplitude) * 0.2;
            }

            let finalScalingFactor = 1.0 + breathingFactor + (liveMicrophoneAmplitude * 1.2);
            if (orbMesh) orbMesh.scale.set(finalScalingFactor, finalScalingFactor, finalScalingFactor);
            if (orbGlow) orbGlow.scale.set(finalScalingFactor * 1.25, finalScalingFactor * 1.25, finalScalingFactor * 1.25);
            if (starParticles) starParticles.rotation.y = time * 0.02;
            renderer.render(scene, camera);
        }

        function onWindowResize() {
            camera.aspect = window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight;
            camera.updateProjectionMatrix();
            renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
        }

        // 🎙️ UNIFIED SPEECH RECOGNITION PERSISTENT CORE
        function initUnifiedSpeechEngine() {
            if (!('webkitSpeechRecognition' in window) && !('SpeechRecognition' in window)) {
                appendResponseCard("Hardware Alert", "Speech recognition structures not supported.");
                return;
            }

            const SpeechRecognition = window.SpeechRecognition || window.webkitSpeechRecognition;
            recognition = new SpeechRecognition();
            recognition.continuous = true;
            recognition.interimResults = false;
            recognition.lang = 'en-US';

            recognition.onresult = (event) => {
                const lastIndex = event.resultIndex;
                const transcript = event.results[lastIndex][0].transcript.trim();
                const transcriptLower = transcript.toLowerCase();
                
                console.log("Speech captured:", transcript);

                // 🚪 CORE CONDITION A: ACTIVE CONTINUOUS STREAMING CHANNEL
                if (isListeningMode) {
                    // Check for explicit vocal deactivation commands
                    if (transcriptLower.includes("switch to text mode only") || transcriptLower.includes("turn microphone off")) {
                        switchToAmbientMode();
                        // Ping server to say goodbye vocally before closing out the loop
                        postCommandToBackend("Deactivate continuous voice mode and wrap up snappy.", 'voice');
                    } else {
                        // Forward request over to LLM nodes. Notice: Switch to ambient mode is omitted!
                        postCommandToBackend(transcript, 'voice');
                    }
                } 
                // 🔓 CORE CONDITION B: PASSIVE AMBIENT SCANNING
                else {
                    const functionalTriggers = ["hi ace", "hey ace", "wake up ace", "ok ace", "activate voice mode", "turn on microphone"];
                    let targetTriggerMatch = null;
                    
                    for (let trigger of functionalTriggers) {
                        if (transcriptLower.includes(trigger)) {
                            targetTriggerMatch = trigger;
                            break;
                        }
                    }

                    if (targetTriggerMatch) {
                        switchToActiveListeningMode();
                        let triggerPosition = transcriptLower.indexOf(targetTriggerMatch) + targetTriggerMatch.length;
                        let isolatedTrailingCommand = transcript.substring(triggerPosition).trim();
                        
                        if (isolatedTrailingCommand.length > 0) {
                            postCommandToBackend(isolatedTrailingCommand, 'voice');
                        } else {
                            appendResponseCard("System Core", "Voice link channel locked open. Awaiting instructions...");
                        }
                    }
                }
            };

            recognition.onerror = (e) => { console.log("Speech system glitch bypassed:", e); };
            recognition.onend = () => { recognition.start(); }; // Keeps recognition loop indestructible
            recognition.start();
        }

        function switchToActiveListeningMode() {
            isListeningMode = true;
            if (audioContext && audioContext.state === 'suspended') { audioContext.resume(); }
            const btn = document.getElementById('master-mic-btn');
            const svgIcon = document.getElementById('mic-icon-svg');
            if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
            updateSystemUIState("listening");
            if (svgIcon) svgIcon.innerHTML = `<rect x="6" y="6" width="12" height="12"/>`;
        }

        function switchToAmbientMode() {
            isListeningMode = false;
            const btn = document.getElementById('master-mic-btn');
            const svgIcon = document.getElementById('mic-icon-svg');
            if (btn) btn.classList.remove('active');
            updateSystemUIState("idle");
            if (svgIcon) svgIcon.innerHTML = `<path d="M12 14c1.66 0 3-1.34 3-3V5c0-1.66-1.34-3-3-3S9 3.34 9 5v6c0 1.66 1.34 3 3 3zm5.3-3c0 3-2.54 5.1-5.3 5.1S6.7 14 6.7 11H5c0 3.41 2.72 6.23 6 6.72V21h2v-3.28c3.28-.48 6-3.3 6-6.72h-1.7z"/>`;
        }

        function toggleVoiceCapture() {
            if (!isListeningMode) { switchToActiveListeningMode(); } 
            else { switchToAmbientMode(); }
        }

        function handleGlobalKeydown(event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter' && document.activeElement !== document.getElementById('chat-entry')) {
                event.preventDefault();
                toggleVoiceCapture();
            }
        }

        function handleTextSubmit(event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter') {
                const inputElement = document.getElementById('chat-entry');
                const commandText = inputElement.value.trim();
                if (!commandText) return;
                inputElement.value = "";
                postCommandToBackend(commandText, 'text');
            }
        }

        function postCommandToBackend(payloadText, source) {
            updateSystemUIState("processing");
            appendResponseCard(source === 'voice' ? "Aryan (Voice)" : "Aryan (Keyboard)", payloadText);

            fetch('/api/command', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ command: payloadText, source: source })
            })
            .then(res => res.json())
            .then(data => {
                updateSystemUIState(isListeningMode ? "listening" : "idle");
                
                if (typeof data.response === 'object') {
                    if(data.response.contrarian) appendResponseCard("🎭 The Contrarian", data.response.contrarian);
                    if(data.response.synergist) appendResponseCard("🚀 The Synergist", data.response.synergist);
                    if(data.response.chairman) appendResponseCard("🏛️ The Chairman Summary", data.response.chairman);
                } else {
                    appendResponseCard("Ace Intelligence", data.response);
                }
            })
            .catch(err => {
                updateSystemUIState(isListeningMode ? "listening" : "idle");
                appendResponseCard("System Error", "Connection timed out.");
            });
        }

        function triggerMapModule() { appendResponseCard("Tactical Map Matrix", "Initializing grid scan layers... Active path nominal."); }
        function triggerAlertsModule() { appendResponseCard("Alerts Sub-Console", "All telemetry indicators nominal."); }

        function updateSystemUIState(state) {
            const text = document.getElementById('system-status-text');
            const dot = document.getElementById('global-status-dot');
            if (!dot) return;
            dot.className = "status-dot";
            
            if(state === "listening") { if(text) text.innerText = "LISTENING"; dot.classList.add('listening'); }
            else if(state === "processing") { if(text) text.innerText = "PROCESSING"; dot.classList.add('processing'); }
            else { if(text) text.innerText = "ONLINE"; }
        }

        function appendResponseCard(speaker, message) {
            const stack = document.getElementById('response-stack');
            const card = document.createElement('div');
            card.className = 'response-card';
            card.innerHTML = `<div class="speaker-tag">${speaker}</div><div>${message}</div>`;
            if(stack.children.length >= 3) stack.removeChild(stack.children[0]);
            stack.appendChild(card);
        }

        function togglePanel() { document.getElementById('activity-panel').classList.toggle('collapsed'); }

        window.onload = initSpaceScene;
    </script>
</body>
</html>

        }
        .wordmark { font-weight: 600; font-size: 16px; letter-spacing: 0.05em; display: flex; align-items: center; }
        .wordmark span { color: #2DD4A8; margin-left: 2px; font-size: 20px; }
        .header-right { display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 20px; }
        .ghost-btn { background: none; border: none; color: rgba(255,255,255,0.6); font-size: 11px; font-family: monospace; letter-spacing: 0.05em; cursor: pointer; transition: color 0.2s; }
        .ghost-btn:hover { color: #2DD4A8; }
        
        /* Pulse Status Indicator Dot */
        .status-container { display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 8px; font-size: 11px; font-family: monospace; letter-spacing: 0.05em; color: rgba(255,255,255,0.5); }

        /* Collapsible Right Activity Panel */
        #activity-panel {
            top: 70px; right: 10px; width: 260px; height: calc(100% - 210px);

        /* Floating Dynamic Response Display Stack */
        #response-stack { position: absolute; top: 120px; left: 30px; z-index: 2; display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 15px; pointer-events: none; }
        .response-card {
            width: 280px; background: rgba(22, 23, 29, 0.75); border-radius: 6px;

        /* FIXED BOTTOM INTERACTIVE CONTROL DOCK */
        #control-dock {
            position: absolute; bottom: 0; left: 0; width: 100%; height: 130px;
            z-index: 2; display: flex; flex-direction: column; align-items: center;
            justify-content: center; pointer-events: none; gap: 10px;
        }
        .interactive-elements { display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 20px; pointer-events: auto; }
        
        .chat-input-wrapper {
            background: rgba(14, 15, 19, 0.4); backdrop-filter: blur(10px);

        }
        .chat-input-wrapper input { background: none; border: none; outline: none; color: #ffffff; font-family: 'Inter', sans-serif; font-size: 13px; width: 100%; }

            width: 64px; height: 64px; border-radius: 50%; background: #16171D;

            border-color: #2DD4A8;
            box-shadow: 0 0 24px rgba(45, 212, 168, 0.5);
        }
        .mic-button.active svg { fill: #2DD4A8; }
        .pulse-ring {
            position: absolute; top: 0; left: 0; width: 64px; height: 64px;
            border-radius: 50%; border: 2px solid #2DD4A8; pointer-events: none;
            opacity: 0; transform: scale(1);
        }
        .mic-button.active + .pulse-ring { animation: ringSpread 1.4s infinite cubic-bezier(0.16, 1, 0.3, 1); }

        .hint-text { font-size: 11px; font-family: monospace; text-transform: uppercase; color: rgba(255,255,255,0.4); letter-spacing: 0.08em; }

        @keyframes slideIn { 0% { opacity: 0; transform: translateX(20px); } 100% { opacity: 1; transform: translateX(0); } }

</head>
<body>

                <div class="mic-button" id="master-mic-btn" onclick="toggleVoiceCapture()">
                    <svg id="mic-icon-svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
                        <path d="M12 14c1.66 0 3-1.34 3-3V5c0-1.66-1.34-3-3-3S9 3.34 9 5v6c0 1.66 1.34 3 3 3zm5.3-3c0 3-2.54 5.1-5.3 5.1S6.7 14 6.7 11H5c0 3.41 2.72 6.23 6 6.72V21h2v-3.28c3.28-.48 6-3.3 6-6.72h-1.7z"/>
                    </svg>
                </div>

    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/three.js/r128/three.min.js"></script>
    <script>
        let scene, camera, renderer, starParticles, orbMesh, orbGlow;
        let recognition;
        
        // 🛠️ MULTI-STATE AUDIO ENGINE VARIABLES
        let isListeningMode = false;       // True = Continuous response tracking active
        let shouldRunSpeechEngine = true;  // Universal master power line for browser audio capturing

        let audioContext, audioAnalyser, audioDataArray;
        let liveMicrophoneAmplitude = 0.0;

        // THREE.JS SCENE PROTOCOLS
        function initSpaceScene() {
            const container = document.getElementById('canvas-container');
            
            scene = new THREE.Scene();
            camera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(60, window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight, 0.1, 1000);
            camera.position.z = 5;

            renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({ antialias: true, alpha: false });
            renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
            renderer.setPixelRatio(window.devicePixelRatio);
            container.appendChild(renderer.domElement);

            const starGeometry = new THREE.BufferGeometry();
            const starCount = 1200;
            const starPositions = new Float32Array(starCount * 3);
            for(let i=0; i < starCount * 3; i++) {
                starPositions[i] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 15;
            }
            starGeometry.setAttribute('position', new THREE.BufferAttribute(starPositions, 3));
            const starMaterial = new THREE.PointsMaterial({ color: 0xffffff, size: 0.02, transparent: true, opacity: 0.8 });
            starParticles = new THREE.Points(starGeometry, starMaterial);
            scene.add(starParticles);

            const orbGeometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.6, 64, 64);
            const orbMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color: 0x2DD4A8 });
            orbMesh = new THREE.Mesh(orbGeometry, orbMaterial);
            scene.add(orbMesh);

            const glowGeometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.8, 32, 32);
            const glowMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color: 0x2DD4A8, transparent: true, opacity: 0.25, side: THREE.BackSide });
            orbGlow = new THREE.Mesh(glowGeometry, glowMaterial);
            scene.add(orbGlow);

            window.addEventListener('resize', onWindowResize);
            document.addEventListener('keydown', handleGlobalKeydown);

            initUnifiedSpeechEngine();
            initHardwareAudioAnalyzer();
            animateLoop();
        }

        function initHardwareAudioAnalyzer() {
            navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ audio: true })
            .then(stream => {
                const AudioContextClass = window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext;
                audioContext = new AudioContextClass();
                const sourceNode = audioContext.createMediaStreamSource(stream);
                audioAnalyser = audioContext.createAnalyser();
                audioAnalyser.fftSize = 256;
                const bufferLength = audioAnalyser.frequencyBinCount;
                audioDataArray = new Uint8Array(bufferLength);
                sourceNode.connect(audioAnalyser);
            })
            .catch(err => { console.log("⚠️ Acoustic analyzer link standby."); });
        }

        function animateLoop() {
            requestAnimationFrame(animateLoop);
            const time = Date.now() * 0.001;
            let breathingFactor = Math.sin(time * 1.5) * 0.04;
            
            if (shouldRunSpeechEngine && audioAnalyser && audioDataArray) {
                audioAnalyser.getByteFrequencyData(audioDataArray);
                let totalFrequencySum = 0;
                for (let i = 0; i < audioDataArray.length; i++) { totalFrequencySum += audioDataArray[i]; }
                let calculatedAverage = totalFrequencySum / audioDataArray.length;
                let targetAmplitude = calculatedAverage / 128.0;
                liveMicrophoneAmplitude += (targetAmplitude - liveMicrophoneAmplitude) * 0.2;
            } else {
                // Decay back to smooth absolute zero if hardware line is cut down
                liveMicrophoneAmplitude += (0.0 - liveMicrophoneAmplitude) * 0.1;
            }

            let finalScalingFactor = 1.0 + breathingFactor + (liveMicrophoneAmplitude * 1.2);
            if (orbMesh) orbMesh.scale.set(finalScalingFactor, finalScalingFactor, finalScalingFactor);
            if (orbGlow) orbGlow.scale.set(finalScalingFactor * 1.25, finalScalingFactor * 1.25, finalScalingFactor * 1.25);
            if (starParticles) starParticles.rotation.y = time * 0.02;
            renderer.render(scene, camera);
        }

        function onWindowResize() {
            camera.aspect = window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight;
            camera.updateProjectionMatrix();
            renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
        }

        // 🎙️ UNIFIED SPEECH RECOGNITION PERSISTENT CORE
        function initUnifiedSpeechEngine() {
            if (!('webkitSpeechRecognition' in window) && !('SpeechRecognition' in window)) {
                appendResponseCard("Hardware Alert", "Speech recognition structures not supported.");
                return;
            }

            const SpeechRecognition = window.SpeechRecognition || window.webkitSpeechRecognition;
            recognition = new SpeechRecognition();
            recognition.continuous = true;
            recognition.interimResults = false;
            recognition.lang = 'en-US';

            recognition.onresult = (event) => {
                if (!shouldRunSpeechEngine) return; // Prevent dead stream leakage
                
                const lastIndex = event.resultIndex;
                const transcript = event.results[lastIndex][0].transcript.trim();
                const transcriptLower = transcript.toLowerCase();
                
                console.log("Core Captured token:", transcript);

                // Check for loose vocal hardware cutoff instructions
                if (transcriptLower.includes("microphone off") || transcriptLower.includes("text mode only") || transcriptLower.includes("turn microphone off")) {
                    turnMicrophoneCompletelyOff();
                    postCommandToBackend("Deactivate voice channels completely.", 'text');
                    return;
                }

                // STATE 2: ACTIVE CONTINUOUS CAPTURE PROCESSING
                if (isListeningMode) {
                    postCommandToBackend(transcript, 'voice');
                } 
                // STATE 1: PASSIVE STANDBY WAKE SCANNING
                else {
                    const functionalTriggers = ["hi ace", "hey ace", "wake up ace", "ok ace", "activate voice mode", "turn on microphone"];
                    let targetTriggerMatch = null;
                    
                    for (let trigger of functionalTriggers) {
                        if (transcriptLower.includes(trigger)) {
                            targetTriggerMatch = trigger;
                            break;
                        }
                    }

                    if (targetTriggerMatch) {
                        switchToActiveListeningMode();
                        let triggerPosition = transcriptLower.indexOf(targetTriggerMatch) + targetTriggerMatch.length;
                        let isolatedTrailingCommand = transcript.substring(triggerPosition).trim();
                        
                        if (isolatedTrailingCommand.length > 0) {
                            postCommandToBackend(isolatedTrailingCommand, 'voice');
                        } else {
                            appendResponseCard("System Core", "Vocal stream link channel locked open. Speak freely...");
                        }
                    }
                }
            };

            recognition.onerror = (e) => { console.log("Speech tracking exception ignored."); };
            
            recognition.onend = () => { 
                // Only restart the stream loop if the master power line remains true
                if (shouldRunSpeechEngine) {
                    try { recognition.start(); } catch(err) {}
                }
            };

            if (shouldRunSpeechEngine) { recognition.start(); }
        }

        function switchToActiveListeningMode() {
            shouldRunSpeechEngine = true;
            isListeningMode = true;
            if (audioContext && audioContext.state === 'suspended') { audioContext.resume(); }
            
            const btn = document.getElementById('master-mic-btn');
            const svgIcon = document.getElementById('mic-icon-svg');
            if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
            updateSystemUIState("listening");
            if (svgIcon) svgIcon.innerHTML = `<rect x="6" y="6" width="12" height="12"/>`;
        }

        // STATE 0: TOTAL HARDWARE DISENGAGEMENT
        function turnMicrophoneCompletelyOff() {
            isListeningMode = false;
            shouldRunSpeechEngine = false;
            
            if (recognition) {
                recognition.stop(); // Breaks browser hardware session loop immediately
            }
            
            const btn = document.getElementById('master-mic-btn');
            const svgIcon = document.getElementById('mic-icon-svg');
            if (btn) btn.classList.remove('active');
            updateSystemUIState("muted");
            if (svgIcon) svgIcon.innerHTML = `<path d="M12 14c1.66 0 3-1.34 3-3V5c0-1.66-1.34-3-3-3S9 3.34 9 5v6c0 1.66 1.34 3 3 3zm5.3-3c0 3-2.54 5.1-5.3 5.1S6.7 14 6.7 11H5c0 3.41 2.72 6.23 6 6.72V21h2v-3.28c3.28-.48 6-3.3 6-6.72h-1.7z"/>`;
            appendResponseCard("System Core", "Microphone pipeline terminated. Browser channel dropped. Pure Text Mode Active.");
        }

        function switchToAmbientMode() {
            // Drops down to background passive hotword scanning state
            isListeningMode = false;
            shouldRunSpeechEngine = true;
            const btn = document.getElementById('master-mic-btn');
            const svgIcon = document.getElementById('mic-icon-svg');
            if (btn) btn.classList.remove('active');
            updateSystemUIState("idle");
            if (svgIcon) svgIcon.innerHTML = `<path d="M12 14c1.66 0 3-1.34 3-3V5c0-1.66-1.34-3-3-3S9 3.34 9 5v6c0 1.66 1.34 3 3 3zm5.3-3c0 3-2.54 5.1-5.3 5.1S6.7 14 6.7 11H5c0 3.41 2.72 6.23 6 6.72V21h2v-3.28c3.28-.48 6-3.3 6-6.72h-1.7z"/>`;
        }

        function toggleVoiceCapture() {
            if (!shouldRunSpeechEngine || !isListeningMode) { 
                switchToActiveListeningMode();
                try { recognition.start(); } catch(err) {}
            } else { 
                turnMicrophoneCompletelyOff();
                postCommandToBackend("Deactivate voice channels completely.", 'text');
            }
        }

        function handleGlobalKeydown(event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter' && document.activeElement !== document.getElementById('chat-entry')) {
                event.preventDefault();
                toggleVoiceCapture();
            }
        }

        function handleTextSubmit(event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter') {
                const inputElement = document.getElementById('chat-entry');
                const commandText = inputElement.value.trim();
                if (!commandText) return;
                inputElement.value = "";
                
                const lowerCmd = commandText.toLowerCase();
                
                // Intercept text overrides to manage mic states via input box
                if (lowerCmd.includes("activate voice mode") || lowerCmd.includes("turn on microphone") || lowerCmd.includes("voice mode")) {
                    switchToActiveListeningMode();
                    try { recognition.start(); } catch(err) {}
                    postCommandToBackend(commandText, 'voice');
                } else if (lowerCmd.includes("turn microphone off") || lowerCmd.includes("text mode only") || lowerCmd.includes("microphone off")) {
                    turnMicrophoneCompletelyOff();
                    postCommandToBackend(commandText, 'text');
                } else {
                    postCommandToBackend(commandText, isListeningMode ? 'voice' : 'text');
                }
            }
        }

        function postCommandToBackend(payloadText, source) {
            updateSystemUIState("processing");
            appendResponseCard(source === 'voice' ? "Aryan (Voice)" : "Aryan (Keyboard)", payloadText);

            fetch('/api/command', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ command: payloadText, source: source })
            })
            .then(res => res.json())
            .then(data => {
                if (!shouldRunSpeechEngine) updateSystemUIState("muted");
                else updateSystemUIState(isListeningMode ? "listening" : "idle");
                
                if (typeof data.response === 'object') {
                    if(data.response.contrarian) appendResponseCard("🎭 The Contrarian", data.response.contrarian);
                    if(data.response.synergist) appendResponseCard("🚀 The Synergist", data.response.synergist);
                    if(data.response.chairman) appendResponseCard("🏛️ The Chairman Summary", data.response.chairman);
                } else {
                    appendResponseCard("Ace Intelligence", data.response);
                }
            })
            .catch(err => {
                if (!shouldRunSpeechEngine) updateSystemUIState("muted");
                else updateSystemUIState(isListeningMode ? "listening" : "idle");
                appendResponseCard("System Error", "Link dropped.");
            });
        }

        function triggerMapModule() { 
            // Now fully dynamic, talking straight to backend routing endpoints
            postCommandToBackend("Compile data map diagnostics overlay summary.", isListeningMode ? 'voice' : 'text');
        }
        
        function triggerAlertsModule() { 
            postCommandToBackend("Review active telemetry alerts logs.", isListeningMode ? 'voice' : 'text');
        }

        function updateSystemUIState(state) {
            const text = document.getElementById('system-status-text');
            const dot = document.getElementById('global-status-dot');
            if (!dot) return;
            dot.className = "status-dot";
            
            if(state === "listening") { if(text) text.innerText = "LISTENING"; dot.classList.add('listening'); }
            else if(state === "processing") { if(text) text.innerText = "PROCESSING"; dot.classList.add('processing'); }
            else if(state === "muted") { if(text) text.innerText = "MUTED"; dot.classList.add('muted'); }
            else { if(text) text.innerText = "ONLINE"; }
        }

        function appendResponseCard(speaker, message) {
            const stack = document.getElementById('response-stack');
            const card = document.createElement('div');
            card.className = 'response-card';
            card.innerHTML = `<div class="speaker-tag">${speaker}</div><div>${message}</div>`;
            if(stack.children.length >= 3) stack.removeChild(stack.children[0]);
            stack.appendChild(card);
        }

        function togglePanel() { document.getElementById('activity-panel').classList.toggle('collapsed'); }

        window.onload = initSpaceScene;
    </script>
</body>
</html>

from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
import os
import sys
import threading
import time
import ollama

# Import your locked, functional core speech assets
from audio_provider import speak_text
from council import run_council_debate

app = Flask(__name__)

FAST_MODEL = "llama3.2:1b"
SMART_MODEL = "qwen2.5-coder:latest"
chat_history = []

def should_trigger_council(text):
    text_lower = text.lower()
    triggers = ["council", "debate", "evaluate"]
    negations = ["don't", "dont", "do not", "never", "without", "skip", "stop"]
    if not any(kw in text_lower for kw in triggers): return False
    for neg in negations:
        if neg in text_lower:
            for kw in triggers:
                if kw in text_lower and text_lower.find(neg) < text_lower.find(kw): return False
    return True

def execute_audio_playback(text_to_speak):
    try:
        try:
            import pythoncom
            pythoncom.CoInitialize()
        except ImportError:
            pass
        print(f"🔊 [Audio Engine: Vocalizing response via system hardware...]")
        speak_text(text_to_speak)
        print(f"✅ [Audio Engine: Playback transaction complete.]")
    except Exception as tts_error:
        print(f"❌ [Audio Engine Crash]: Reason: {tts_error}")

@app.route('/')
def serve_dashboard_console():
    try:
        with open('index.html', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: return f.read()
    except Exception as e: return f"System Matrix Failure: {e}"

@app.route('/api/command', methods=['POST'])
def orchestrate_command_routing():
    global chat_history
    data = request.get_json() or {}
    command = data.get('command', '').strip()
    source = data.get('source', 'text')
    
    if not command: return jsonify({"response": "Empty transaction payload."})
    print(f"\n📥 Transaction received from [{source.upper()}]: \"{command}\"")
    lower_cmd = command.lower()

    # 🛠️ HARD-CODED MIC MANAGEMENT COMPLIANCE TRIPS
    if "turn microphone off" in lower_cmd or "deactivate voice channels" in lower_cmd or "microphone off" in lower_cmd:
        reply = "Understood, Aryan. Severing local microphone lines immediately. Pure text communication framework active."
        # Speak one final confirmation out loud before the channel shuts down completely
        if source == 'voice':
            threading.Thread(target=execute_audio_playback, args=(reply,), daemon=True).start()
        return jsonify({"response": reply})
        
    if "activate voice mode" in lower_cmd or "turn on microphone" in lower_cmd or "voice mode" in lower_cmd:
        reply = "Vocal arrays online, Aryan. Audio tracking channel locked open. Continuous feed active."
        threading.Thread(target=execute_audio_playback, args=(reply,), daemon=True).start()
        return jsonify({"response": reply})

    # CASE A: MULTI-AGENT COUNCIL ROUTING
    if should_trigger_council(command):
        print("👥 Assembling Council Matrix Boardroom Core...")
        debate_packet = run_council_debate(command)
        if source == 'voice':
            def narrate_council():
                execute_audio_playback("Analyzing the risk layout from the contrarian.")
                execute_audio_playback(debate_packet['contrarian'])
                time.sleep(0.3)
                execute_audio_playback("Reviewing the strategy modification from the synergist.")
                execute_audio_playback(debate_packet['synergist'])
                time.sleep(0.3)
                execute_audio_playback("The chairman's final evaluation and takeaways.")
                execute_audio_playback(debate_packet['chairman'])
            threading.Thread(target=narrate_council, daemon=True).start()
        return jsonify({"response": debate_packet})

    # CASE B: snappy CHAT ROTATION
    else:
        if "think deeply" in lower_cmd or "smart mode" in lower_cmd or "analyze" in lower_cmd:
            active_model = SMART_MODEL
            print(f"🧠 Escalating layer -> routing through {active_model}")
        else:
            active_model = FAST_MODEL
            print(f"⚡ Pacing layer optimally -> routing through {active_model}")

        messages_payload = [
            {
                "role": "system", 
                "content": (
                    "You are Ace, an elite desktop AI assistant for Aryan, speaking with a witty cadence like Jarvis. "
                    "Keep your response extremely short and limited to only 1 or 2 sentences maximum. "
                    "Get straight to the point with zero conversational preambles or filler introductions."
                )
            }
        ]
        messages_payload.extend(chat_history)
        messages_payload.append({"role": "user", "content": command})

        try:
            response = ollama.chat(model=active_model, messages=messages_payload)
            reply = response['message']['content']
            
            chat_history.append({"role": "user", "content": command})
            chat_history.append({"role": "assistant", "content": reply})
            
            if len(chat_history) > 20: chat_history = chat_history[-20:]

            if source == 'voice':
                threading.Thread(target=execute_audio_playback, args=(reply,), daemon=True).start()

            return jsonify({"response": reply})
        except Exception as e:
            return jsonify({"response": f"Core pipeline dropped: {e}"})

if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(host='0.0.0.0', port=5000, debug=False)


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------


from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
import os
import sys
import threading
import time
import ollama

# Import your locked, functional core speech assets
from audio_provider import speak_text
from council import run_council_debate

app = Flask(__name__)

FAST_MODEL = "llama3.2:1b"
SMART_MODEL = "qwen2.5-coder:latest"

# 🧠 SYSTEM CONTEXT STORAGE REGISTERS
chat_history = []
pending_memory_clear = False  # Locks state engine when confirmation is required

def should_trigger_council(text):
    text_lower = text.lower()
    triggers = ["council", "debate", "evaluate"]
    negations = ["don't", "dont", "do not", "never", "without", "skip", "stop"]
    if not any(kw in text_lower for kw in triggers): return False
    for neg in negations:
        if neg in text_lower:
            for kw in triggers:
                if kw in text_lower and text_lower.find(neg) < text_lower.find(kw): return False
    return True

def execute_audio_playback(text_to_speak):
    try:
        try:
            import pythoncom
            pythoncom.CoInitialize()
        except ImportError:
            pass
        print(f"🔊 [Audio Engine: Vocalizing response via system hardware...]")
        speak_text(text_to_speak)
        print(f"✅ [Audio Engine: Playback transaction complete.]")
    except Exception as tts_error:
        print(f"❌ [Audio Engine Crash]: Reason: {tts_error}")

@app.route('/')
def serve_dashboard_console():
    try:
        with open('index.html', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: return f.read()
    except Exception as e: return f"System Matrix Failure: {e}"

@app.route('/api/command', methods=['POST'])
def orchestrate_command_routing():
    global chat_history, pending_memory_clear
    data = request.get_json() or {}
    command = data.get('command', '').strip()
    source = data.get('source', 'text')
    
    if not command: return jsonify({"response": "Empty transaction payload."})
    print(f"\n📥 Transaction received from [{source.upper()}]: \"{command}\"")
    lower_cmd = command.lower()

    # 🛑 MEMORY PURGE PHASE 2: CONFIRMATION CHECK
    if pending_memory_clear:
        if "yes" in lower_cmd or "confirm" in lower_cmd or "do it" in lower_cmd:
            chat_history = []
            pending_memory_clear = False
            reply = "Memory banks cleared. Active conversation logs are fully purged, Aryan."
            if source == 'voice':
                threading.Thread(target=execute_audio_playback, args=(reply,), daemon=True).start()
            return jsonify({"response": reply})
        elif "no" in lower_cmd or "cancel" in lower_cmd or "abort" in lower_cmd:
            pending_memory_clear = False
            reply = "Purge canceled. Memory logs preserved safely, Aryan."
            if source == 'voice':
                threading.Thread(target=execute_audio_playback, args=(reply,), daemon=True).start()
            return jsonify({"response": reply})
        else:
            pending_memory_clear = False  # Reset if user says something completely irrelevant
            reply = "Invalid confirmation vector. Purge sequence aborted to protect data integrity."
            if source == 'voice':
                threading.Thread(target=execute_audio_playback, args=(reply,), daemon=True).start()
            return jsonify({"response": reply})

    # 🚨 MEMORY PURGE PHASE 1: INTERCEPT DETECTION
    if "clear memory" in lower_cmd or "wipe history" in lower_cmd or "reset memory" in lower_cmd:
        pending_memory_clear = True
        reply = "Are you absolutely sure you want to purge my active memory logs, Aryan? Please confirm with a 'yes' or 'no'."
        if source == 'voice':
            threading.Thread(target=execute_audio_playback, args=(reply,), daemon=True).start()
        return jsonify({"response": reply})

    # HARD-CODED MIC MANAGEMENT COMPLIANCE TRIPS
    if "turn microphone off" in lower_cmd or "deactivate voice channels" in lower_cmd or "microphone off" in lower_cmd:
        reply = "Understood, Aryan. Severing local microphone lines immediately. Pure text communication framework active."
        if source == 'voice':
            threading.Thread(target=execute_audio_playback, args=(reply,), daemon=True).start()
        return jsonify({"response": reply})
        
    if "activate voice mode" in lower_cmd or "turn on microphone" in lower_cmd or "voice mode" in lower_cmd:
        reply = "Vocal arrays online, Aryan. Audio tracking channel locked open. Continuous feed active."
        threading.Thread(target=execute_audio_playback, args=(reply,), daemon=True).start()
        return jsonify({"response": reply})

    # CASE A: MULTI-AGENT COUNCIL ROUTING
    if should_trigger_council(command):
        print("👥 Assembling Council Matrix Boardroom Core...")
        debate_packet = run_council_debate(command)
        if source == 'voice':
            def narrate_council():
                execute_audio_playback("Analyzing the risk layout from the contrarian.")
                execute_audio_playback(debate_packet['contrarian'])
                time.sleep(0.3)
                execute_audio_playback("Reviewing the strategy modification from the synergist.")
                execute_audio_playback(debate_packet['synergist'])
                time.sleep(0.3)
                execute_audio_playback("The chairman's final evaluation and takeaways.")
                execute_audio_playback(debate_packet['chairman'])
            threading.Thread(target=narrate_council, daemon=True).start()
        return jsonify({"response": debate_packet})

    # CASE B: SNAPPY CHAT ROTATION
    else:
        if "think deeply" in lower_cmd or "smart mode" in lower_cmd or "analyze" in lower_cmd:
            active_model = SMART_MODEL
            print(f"🧠 Escalating layer -> routing through {active_model}")
        else:
            active_model = FAST_MODEL
            print(f"⚡ Pacing layer optimally -> routing through {active_model}")

        # Construct short-term payload arrays with high-priority brevity rules injected
        messages_payload = [
            {
                "role": "system", 
                "content": (
                    "You are Ace, an elite desktop AI assistant for Aryan, speaking with a witty cadence like Jarvis. "
                    "CRITICAL LENGTH DIRECTIVE: Keep your response extremely short and limited to only 1 or 2 sentences maximum. "
                    "Get straight to the point with zero conversational preambles or filler introductions."
                )
            }
        ]
        messages_payload.extend(chat_history)
        messages_payload.append({"role": "user", "content": command})

        try:
            response = ollama.chat(model=active_model, messages=messages_payload)
            reply = response['message']['content']
            
            chat_history.append({"role": "user", "content": command})
            chat_history.append({"role": "assistant", "content": reply})
            
            if len(chat_history) > 20: chat_history = chat_history[-20:]

            if source == 'voice':
                threading.Thread(target=execute_audio_playback, args=(reply,), daemon=True).start()

            return jsonify({"response": reply})
        except Exception as e:
            return jsonify({"response": f"Core pipeline dropped: {e}"})

if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(host='0.0.0.0', port=5000, debug=False)

SMART_MODEL = "qwen2.5-coder:latest"
chat_history = []
pending_memory_clear = False  # Locks state engine when confirmation is required

def should_trigger_council(text):
    text_lower = text.lower()
    triggers = ["council", "debate", "evaluate"]
    negations = ["don't", "dont", "do not", "never", "without", "skip", "stop"]
    if not any(kw in text_lower for kw in triggers): return False
    for neg in negations:
        if neg in text_lower:
            for kw in triggers:
                if kw in text_lower and text_lower.find(neg) < text_lower.find(kw): return False
    return True

def execute_audio_playback(text_to_speak):
    try:
        try:
            import pythoncom
            pythoncom.CoInitialize()
        except ImportError:
            pass
        print(f"🔊 [Audio Engine: Vocalizing response via system hardware...]")
        speak_text(text_to_speak)
        print(f"✅ [Audio Engine: Playback transaction complete.]")
    except Exception as tts_error:

            pending_memory_clear = False

            pending_memory_clear = False

            if source == 'voice':
                threading.Thread(target=execute_audio_playback, args=(reply,), daemon=True).start()
            return jsonify({"response": reply})

    # 🚨 MEMORY PURGE PHASE 1: ADVANCED INTERCEPT MATRIX
    # Scans for ANY dangerous combo (e.g., "delete" + "logs", "forget" + "history")
    purge_actions = ["clear", "wipe", "reset", "delete", "purge", "forget", "erase"]
    memory_targets = ["memory", "history", "logs", "context", "cache"]
    
    hit_action = any(action in lower_cmd for action in purge_actions)
    hit_target = any(target in lower_cmd for target in memory_targets)
    
    if hit_action and hit_target:
        pending_memory_clear = True
        reply = "Are you absolutely sure you want to purge my active memory logs, Aryan? Please confirm with a 'yes' or 'no'."

            threading.Thread(target=execute_audio_playback, args=(reply,), daemon=True).start()

        reply = "Understood, Aryan. Severing local microphone lines immediately. Pure text communication framework active."
        if source == 'voice':
            threading.Thread(target=execute_audio_playback, args=(reply,), daemon=True).start()

    if "activate voice mode" in lower_cmd or "turn on microphone" in lower_cmd or "voice mode" in lower_cmd:

    if should_trigger_council(command):
        print("👥 Assembling Council Matrix Boardroom Core...")
        debate_packet = run_council_debate(command)
        if source == 'voice':
            def narrate_council():
                execute_audio_playback("Analyzing the risk layout from the contrarian.")
                execute_audio_playback(debate_packet['contrarian'])
                time.sleep(0.3)
                execute_audio_playback("Reviewing the strategy modification from the synergist.")
                execute_audio_playback(debate_packet['synergist'])
                time.sleep(0.3)
                execute_audio_playback("The chairman's final evaluation and takeaways.")
                execute_audio_playback(debate_packet['chairman'])
            threading.Thread(target=narrate_council, daemon=True).start()
        return jsonify({"response": debate_packet})

    # CASE B: SNAPPY CHAT ROTATION
    else:

            active_model = SMART_MODEL

# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-
import os
import json
import requests
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify, send_from_directory

app = Flask(__name__)

# Configuration for Local Ollama Instance
OLLAMA_URL = "http://localhost:11434/api/chat"
FAST_MODEL = "llama3.2:1b"
SMART_MODEL = "qwen2.5-coder:latest"

# Helper function to call your local Ollama engine
def call_local_llm(model_name, system_prompt, user_message):
    payload = {
        "model": model_name,
        "messages": [
            {"role": "system", "content": system_prompt},
            {"role": "user", "content": user_message}
        ],
        "stream": False
    }
    try:
        response = requests.post(OLLAMA_URL, json=payload, timeout=30)
        if response.status_code == 200:
            return response.json().get("message", {}).get("content", "No response generated.")
        return f"Ollama Error: Status code {response.status_code}"
    except Exception as e:
        return f"Failed to reach local Ollama engine: {str(e)}"

# Simulated 5-Agent Council Logic (Tier 2 & Tier 5 Framework)
def run_council_chain(complex_prompt):
    print(f"[Council] Activating 5-Agent Think Tank for heavy task...")
    
    # Define system personas
    personas = {
        "Contrastor": "Play devil's advocate. Find flaws or edge cases in this request.",
        "First Principles": "Break this problem down to its absolute foundational truths and axioms.",
        "Expansionist": "Brainstorm creative alternatives and massive scale additions for this concept.",
        "Outsider": "Look at this problem from an completely unconventional, non-technical angle.",
        "Executor": "Provide the most optimal, production-ready implementation logic or code blocks."
    }
    
    council_insights = {}
    for agent, role in personas.items():
        print(f"[Council] Querying {agent}...")
        system_instructions = f"You are the {agent} agent inside a thinking council. {role} Keep your response brief and razor-focused."
        council_insights[agent] = call_local_llm(SMART_MODEL, system_instructions, complex_prompt)
    
    # Format insights for the Chairman
    chairman_context = "You are the Executive Chairman of the AI Council. Synthesize the insights from your agents into one final definitive answer:\n"
    for agent, insight in council_insights.items():
        chairman_context += f"\n--- {agent} Insight ---\n{insight}\n"
        
    print("[Council] Submitting insights to Executive Chairman...")
    final_decision = call_local_llm(SMART_MODEL, chairman_context, complex_prompt)
    return final_decision

@app.route('/')
def index():
    # Serves index.html if placed in the same root directory
    return send_from_directory('.', 'index.html')

@app.route('/api/chat', methods=['POST'])
def handle_chat():
    data = request.get_json() or {}
    user_message = data.get('message', '').strip()
    
    # Tier 4 Safety Catch: Empty packet or background click protection
    if not user_message:
        return jsonify({
            "status": "ignored", 
            "reason": "Empty or silent audio payload filtered by backend safety gate."
        }), 200
        
    # Ambient Noise Gate: Filters out stray room pops or clicks
    if len(user_message) < 2:
         return jsonify({
             "status": "ignored", 
             "reason": "Input length too short. Filtered as background ambient spike."
         }), 200

    print(f"\n[User Input Received]: {user_message}")

    # Audit Trail Logging (Tier 6 Compliance)
    print(f"[Audit Log] Payload authorized. Processing routing matrix...")

    # Hybrid Model Routing Logic Matrix
    # Determine complexity: Is it a greeting/short small-talk, or a complex coding/logic prompt?
    complex_keywords = ['build', 'code', 'fix', 'why', 'create', 'write', 'how to', 'program', 'system']
    is_complex = any(keyword in user_message.lower() for keyword in complex_keywords) or len(user_message) > 60

    if is_complex:
        print(f"[Routing Matrix] Routing heavy task to Smart Model ({SMART_MODEL}) via Council System.")
        ai_response = run_council_chain(user_message)
    else:
        print(f"[Routing Matrix] Routing simple query to Fast Model ({FAST_MODEL}) for immediate response.")
        system_prompt = "You are Ace, a responsive, polite personal assistant. Keep your response conversational and short."
        ai_response = call_local_llm(FAST_MODEL, system_prompt, user_message)

    # Placeholder Hook for Text-to-Speech (piper_mega.py / audio_provider.py)
    # Example: generate_speech_file(ai_response)

    return jsonify({
        "status": "success",
        "response": ai_response,
        "routed_to": "Council (Qwen-2.5)" if is_complex else f"Direct ({FAST_MODEL})"
    })

if __name__ == '__main__':
    # Running on local port 5000 with interactive debugger active
    app.run(host='0.0.0.0', port=5000, debug=True)

    </div>

    <script>
        const chatLog = document.getElementById('chatLog');
        const textInput = document.getElementById('textInput');
        const sendBtn = document.getElementById('sendBtn');
        const micToggle = document.getElementById('micToggle');
        const statusPanel = document.getElementById('statusPanel');
        const gateFeedback = document.getElementById('gateFeedback');

        let isListening = false;
        let recognition = null;
        let debounceTimer = null;
        const DEBOUNCE_DELAY = 1000; // Tier 3: 1 Second Debounce Buffer Window

        // Main Payload Transmission Engine
        function appendMessage(sender, text, routeInfo = null) {
            const msgDiv = document.createElement('div');
            msgDiv.classList.add('message', sender.toLowerCase());
            msgDiv.textContent = text;
            
            if (routeInfo) {
                const stamp = document.createElement('span');
                stamp.classList.add('routing-stamp');
                stamp.textContent = `Routed via: ${routeInfo}`;
                msgDiv.appendChild(stamp);
            }
            
            chatLog.appendChild(msgDiv);
            chatLog.scrollTop = chatLog.scrollHeight;
        }

        async function sendMessageToServer(messageText) {
            const cleanMessage = messageText.trim();
            
            // Tier 1 Gatekeeper: Drop completely empty text packet streams
            if (!cleanMessage) return;

            appendMessage('User', cleanMessage);
            statusPanel.textContent = "Ace is thinking...";

            try {
                const response = await fetch('/api/chat', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ message: cleanMessage })
                });
                
                const data = await response.json();
                
                if (data.status === "success") {
                    statusPanel.textContent = "Engine Connected";
                    appendMessage('Ace', data.response, data.routed_to);
                } else {
                    statusPanel.textContent = "Payload Filtered";
                    console.warn("Server dropped package:", data.reason);
                    gateFeedback.textContent = `Server Alert: ${data.reason}`;
                }
            } catch (err) {
                statusPanel.textContent = "Connection Error";
                appendMessage('Ace', "Error connecting to the Flask local server. Ensure server.py is executing on port 5000.");
            }
        }

        // Initialize Speech Loop with Web Speech API
        function initializeSpeechEngine() {
            const SpeechEngine = window.SpeechRecognition || window.webkitSpeechRecognition;
            if (!SpeechEngine) {
                gateFeedback.textContent = "Web Speech Error: Browser infrastructure unsupported.";
                return;
            }

            recognition = new SpeechEngine();
            recognition.continuous = true;
            recognition.interimResults = true;
            recognition.lang = 'en-US';

            recognition.onstart = () => {
                isListening = true;
                micToggle.classList.add('listening');
                statusPanel.textContent = "Listening...";
                gateFeedback.textContent = "Vocal Gatekeepers: Active & Monitoring Feed";
            };

            recognition.onerror = (event) => {
                console.error("Speech system error:", event.error);
                if (event.error !== 'no-speech') {
                    gateFeedback.textContent = `Engine Error: ${event.error}`;
                }
            };

            recognition.onend = () => {
                if (isListening) {
                    // Force restart loop if toggle remains active
                    recognition.start();
                } else {
                    micToggle.classList.remove('listening');
                    statusPanel.textContent = "Engine Connected";
                    gateFeedback.textContent = "Vocal Gatekeepers: Standby";
                }
            };

            recognition.onresult = (event) => {
                let currentTranscript = '';
                
                for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; ++i) {
                    if (event.results[i].isFinal) {
                        currentTranscript += event.results[i][0].transcript;
                    }
                }

                // Tier 1 Gatekeeper: Reject blank spaces/silence
                if (!currentTranscript.trim()) {
                    return;
                }

                // Tier 2 Gatekeeper: Filter microambient room clicks (ambient cutoff length)
                if (currentTranscript.trim().length < 2) {
                    gateFeedback.textContent = "Gatekeeper: Ambient noise filtered.";
                    return;
                }

                gateFeedback.textContent = `Vocal Activity Tracking: "${currentTranscript.trim()}"`;

                // Tier 3 Gatekeeper: 1-Second Complete Silent Debounce Window
                // Instantly wipe the countdown trigger if the user keeps speaking
                clearTimeout(debounceTimer);

                // Initialize countdown: only transmit when speaker stops for 1 full second
                debounceTimer = setTimeout(() => {
                    const finalPhrase = currentTranscript.trim();
                    gateFeedback.textContent = "Gatekeeper: Speech finalized. Transmitting stream...";
                    sendMessageToServer(finalPhrase);
                    
                    // Stop and clear browser speech buffer memory state cleanly
                    isListening = false;
                    recognition.stop();
                }, DEBOUNCE_DELAY);
            };

            recognition.start();
        }

        // Trigger Listeners
        sendBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
            if (textInput.value.trim()) {
                sendMessageToServer(textInput.value);
                textInput.value = '';
            }
        });

        textInput.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
            if (e.key === 'Enter' && textInput.value.trim()) {
                sendMessageToServer(textInput.value);
                textInput.value = '';
            }
        });

        micToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
            if (!isListening) {
                initializeSpeechEngine();
            } else {
                isListening = false;
                if (recognition) recognition.stop();
                clearTimeout(debounceTimer);
            }
        });

        // Window Initialized
        window.addEventListener('load', () => {
            statusPanel.textContent = "Engine Connected";
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
import os
import sys
import threading
import time
import ollama

# Import your locked, functional core speech assets
from audio_provider import speak_text
from council import run_council_debate

app = Flask(__name__)

FAST_MODEL = "llama3.2:1b"
SMART_MODEL = "qwen2.5-coder:latest"
chat_history = []
pending_memory_clear = False  # Locks state engine when confirmation is required

def should_trigger_council(text):
    text_lower = text.lower()
    triggers = ["council", "debate", "evaluate"]
    negations = ["don't", "dont", "do not", "never", "without", "skip", "stop"]
    if not any(kw in text_lower for kw in triggers): return False
    for neg in negations:
        if neg in text_lower:
            for kw in triggers:
                if kw in text_lower and text_lower.find(neg) < text_lower.find(kw): return False
    return True

def execute_audio_playback(text_to_speak):
    try:
        try:
            import pythoncom
            pythoncom.CoInitialize()
        except ImportError:
            pass
        print(f"🔊 [Audio Engine: Vocalizing response via system hardware...]")
        speak_text(text_to_speak)
        print(f"✅ [Audio Engine: Playback transaction complete.]")
    except Exception as tts_error:
        print(f"❌ [Audio Engine Crash]: Reason: {tts_error}")

@app.route('/')
def serve_dashboard_console():
    try:
        with open('index.html', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: return f.read()
    except Exception as e: return f"System Matrix Failure: {e}"

@app.route('/api/command', methods=['POST'])
def orchestrate_command_routing():
    global chat_history, pending_memory_clear
    data = request.get_json() or {}
    command = data.get('command', '').strip()
    source = data.get('source', 'text')
    
    if not command: return jsonify({"response": "Empty transaction payload."})
    print(f"\n📥 Transaction received from [{source.upper()}]: \"{command}\"")
    lower_cmd = command.lower()

    # 🛑 MEMORY PURGE PHASE 2: CONFIRMATION CHECK
    if pending_memory_clear:
        if "yes" in lower_cmd or "confirm" in lower_cmd or "do it" in lower_cmd:
            chat_history = []
            pending_memory_clear = False
            reply = "Memory banks cleared. Active conversation logs are fully purged, Aryan."
            if source == 'voice':
                execute_audio_playback(reply)
            return jsonify({"response": reply})
        elif "no" in lower_cmd or "cancel" in lower_cmd or "abort" in lower_cmd:
            pending_memory_clear = False
            reply = "Purge canceled. Memory logs preserved safely, Aryan."
            if source == 'voice':
                execute_audio_playback(reply)
            return jsonify({"response": reply})
        else:
            pending_memory_clear = False  
            reply = "Invalid confirmation vector. Purge sequence aborted to protect data integrity."
            if source == 'voice':
                execute_audio_playback(reply)
            return jsonify({"response": reply})

    # 🚨 MEMORY PURGE PHASE 1: ADVANCED INTERCEPT MATRIX
    purge_actions = ["clear", "wipe", "reset", "delete", "purge", "forget", "erase"]
    memory_targets = ["memory", "history", "logs", "context", "cache"]
    
    hit_action = any(action in lower_cmd for action in purge_actions)
    hit_target = any(target in lower_cmd for target in memory_targets)
    
    if hit_action and hit_target:
        pending_memory_clear = True
        reply = "Are you absolutely sure you want to purge my active memory logs, Aryan? Please confirm with a 'yes' or 'no'."
        if source == 'voice':
            execute_audio_playback(reply)
        return jsonify({"response": reply})

    # HARD-CODED MIC MANAGEMENT COMPLIANCE TRIPS
    if "turn microphone off" in lower_cmd or "deactivate voice channels" in lower_cmd or "microphone off" in lower_cmd:
        reply = "Understood, Aryan. Severing local microphone lines immediately. Pure text communication framework active."
        if source == 'voice':
            execute_audio_playback(reply)
        return jsonify({"response": reply})
        
    if "activate voice mode" in lower_cmd or "turn on microphone" in lower_cmd or "voice mode" in lower_cmd:
        reply = "Vocal arrays online, Aryan. Audio tracking channel locked open. Continuous feed active."
        execute_audio_playback(reply)
        return jsonify({"response": reply})

    # CASE A: MULTI-AGENT COUNCIL ROUTING
    if should_trigger_council(command):
        print("👥 Assembling Council Matrix Boardroom Core...")
        debate_packet = run_council_debate(command)
        if source == 'voice':
            execute_audio_playback("Analyzing the risk layout from the contrarian.")
            execute_audio_playback(debate_packet['contrarian'])
            time.sleep(0.3)
            execute_audio_playback("Reviewing the strategy modification from the synergist.")
            execute_audio_playback(debate_packet['synergist'])
            time.sleep(0.3)
            execute_audio_playback("The chairman's final evaluation and takeaways.")
            execute_audio_playback(debate_packet['chairman'])
        return jsonify({"response": debate_packet})

    # CASE B: SNAPPY CHAT ROTATION
    else:
        if "think deeply" in lower_cmd or "smart mode" in lower_cmd or "analyze" in lower_cmd:
            active_model = SMART_MODEL
            print(f"🧠 Escalating layer -> routing through {active_model}")
        else:
            active_model = FAST_MODEL
            print(f"⚡ Pacing layer optimally -> routing through {active_model}")

        messages_payload = [
            {
                "role": "system", 
                "content": (
                    "You are Ace, an elite desktop AI assistant for Aryan, speaking with a witty cadence like Jarvis. "
                    "CRITICAL LENGTH DIRECTIVE: Keep your response extremely short and limited to only 1 or 2 sentences maximum. "
                    "Get straight to the point with zero conversational preambles or filler introductions."
                )
            }
        ]
        messages_payload.extend(chat_history)
        messages_payload.append({"role": "user", "content": command})

        try:
            response = ollama.chat(model=active_model, messages=messages_payload)
            reply = response['message']['content']
            
            chat_history.append({"role": "user", "content": command})
            chat_history.append({"role": "assistant", "content": reply})
            
            if len(chat_history) > 20: chat_history = chat_history[-20:]

            if source == 'voice':
                execute_audio_playback(reply)

            return jsonify({"response": reply})
        except Exception as e:
            return jsonify({"response": f"Core pipeline dropped: {e}"})

if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(host='0.0.0.0', port=5000, debug=False)
