    <script src="/three.min.js"></script>
    <script>
        let scene, camera, renderer, starParticles, orbMesh, orbGlow;
        let recognition;
        
        let isListeningMode = false;       
        let shouldRunSpeechEngine = true;  
        let isServerProcessing = false;    

        let audioContext, audioAnalyser, audioDataArray;
        let liveMicrophoneAmplitude = 0.0;

        function updateSystemTheme(hexColor) {
            document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--accent-glow', hexColor);
            document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--accent-card-border', hexColor);
            if (orbMesh && orbMesh.material) orbMesh.material.color.set(hexColor);
            if (orbGlow && orbGlow.material) orbGlow.material.color.set(hexColor);
        }

        function autoCorrectSpeechAndPunctuate(text) {
            let corrected = text.trim();
            if (!corrected) return "";

            const translationMap = {
                "quan": "Qwen",
                "quan 2.5": "Qwen 2.5",
                "queen 2.5": "Qwen 2.5",
                "quinn": "Qwen",
                "gwen": "Qwen",
                "lama": "Llama",
                "llama 3.2": "Llama 3.2",
                "ace": "Ace"
            };

            for (const [misheard, accurate] of Object.entries(translationMap)) {
                const regex = new RegExp(`\\b${misheard}\\b`, 'gi');
                corrected = corrected.replace(regex, accurate);
            }
            
            corrected = corrected.replace(/llama/gi, "Llama");
            corrected = corrected.replace(/qwen/gi, "Qwen");

            if (!/[.!?]$/.test(corrected)) {
                const lower = corrected.toLowerCase();
                const questionTriggers = ["who", "what", "where", "when", "why", "how", "can", "is", "are", "do", "does", "should", "could", "would"];
                const firstWord = lower.split(" ")[0];
                
                if (questionTriggers.includes(firstWord)) corrected += "?";
                else corrected += ".";
            }
            return corrected;
        }

        function initSpaceScene() {
            const container = document.getElementById('canvas-container');
            
            scene = new THREE.Scene();
            camera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(60, window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight, 0.1, 1000);
            camera.position.z = 5;

            renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({ antialias: true, alpha: false });
            renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
            renderer.setPixelRatio(window.devicePixelRatio);
            container.appendChild(renderer.domElement);

            const starGeometry = new THREE.BufferGeometry();
            const starCount = 1200;
            const starPositions = new Float32Array(starCount * 3);
            for(let i=0; i < starCount * 3; i++) {
                starPositions[i] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 15;
            }
            starGeometry.setAttribute('position', new THREE.BufferAttribute(starPositions, 3));
            const starMaterial = new THREE.PointsMaterial({ color: 0xffffff, size: 0.02, transparent: true, opacity: 0.8 });
            starParticles = new THREE.Points(starGeometry, starMaterial);
            scene.add(starParticles);

            const orbGeometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.6, 64, 64);
            const orbMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color: 0x2DD4A8 });
            orbMesh = new THREE.Mesh(orbGeometry, orbMaterial);
            scene.add(orbMesh);

            const glowGeometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.8, 32, 32);
            const glowMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color: 0x2DD4A8, transparent: true, opacity: 0.25, side: THREE.BackSide });
            orbGlow = new THREE.Mesh(glowGeometry, glowMaterial);
            scene.add(orbGlow);

            window.addEventListener('resize', onWindowResize);
            document.addEventListener('keydown', handleGlobalKeydown);

            initUnifiedSpeechEngine();
            initHardwareAudioAnalyzer();
            animateLoop();
        }

        function initHardwareAudioAnalyzer() {
            navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ audio: true })
            .then(stream => {
                const AudioContextClass = window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext;
                audioContext = new AudioContextClass();
                const sourceNode = audioContext.createMediaStreamSource(stream);
                audioAnalyser = audioContext.createAnalyser();
                audioAnalyser.fftSize = 256;
                const bufferLength = audioAnalyser.frequencyBinCount;
                audioDataArray = new Uint8Array(bufferLength);
                sourceNode.connect(audioAnalyser);
            })
            .catch(err => { console.log("⚠️ Acoustic analyzer link standby."); });
        }

        function animateLoop() {
            requestAnimationFrame(animateLoop);
            const time = Date.now() * 0.001;
            let breathingFactor = Math.sin(time * 1.5) * 0.04;
            
            if (shouldRunSpeechEngine && audioAnalyser && audioDataArray) {
                audioAnalyser.getByteFrequencyData(audioDataArray);
                let totalFrequencySum = 0;
                for (let i = 0; i < audioDataArray.length; i++) { totalFrequencySum += audioDataArray[i]; }
                let calculatedAverage = totalFrequencySum / audioDataArray.length;
                let targetAmplitude = calculatedAverage / 128.0;
                liveMicrophoneAmplitude += (targetAmplitude - liveMicrophoneAmplitude) * 0.2;
            } else {
                liveMicrophoneAmplitude += (0.0 - liveMicrophoneAmplitude) * 0.1;
            }

            let finalScalingFactor = 1.0 + breathingFactor + (liveMicrophoneAmplitude * 1.2);
            if (orbMesh) orbMesh.scale.set(finalScalingFactor, finalScalingFactor, finalScalingFactor);
            if (orbGlow) orbGlow.scale.set(finalScalingFactor * 1.25, finalScalingFactor * 1.25, finalScalingFactor * 1.25);
            if (starParticles) starParticles.rotation.y = time * 0.02;
            renderer.render(scene, camera);
        }

        function onWindowResize() {
            camera.aspect = window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight;
            camera.updateProjectionMatrix();
            renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
        }

        function initUnifiedSpeechEngine() {
            if (!('webkitSpeechRecognition' in window) && !('SpeechRecognition' in window)) {
                appendResponseCard("Hardware Alert", "Speech recognition structures not supported.");
                return;
            }

            const SpeechRecognition = window.SpeechRecognition || window.webkitSpeechRecognition;
            recognition = new SpeechRecognition();
            recognition.continuous = true;
            recognition.interimResults = false;
            recognition.lang = 'en-US';

            // 🔒 ON-DEVICE FORCED LOCALIZATION PARAMETERS: Prevents sending voice audio strings up to cloud endpoints
            if ('processLocally' in recognition) {
                recognition.processLocally = true;
            } else if ('localService' in recognition) {
                recognition.localService = true; 
            }

            recognition.onresult = (event) => {
                if (!shouldRunSpeechEngine || isServerProcessing) return; 
                
                const lastIndex = event.resultIndex;
                const rawTranscript = event.results[lastIndex][0].transcript.trim();
                const transcript = autoCorrectSpeechAndPunctuate(rawTranscript);
                const transcriptLower = transcript.toLowerCase();
                
                console.log("Core Captured token:", transcript);

                if (transcriptLower.includes("microphone off") || 
                    transcriptLower.includes("text mode only") || 
                    transcriptLower.includes("turn microphone off") || 
                    transcriptLower.includes("turn off voice mode") || 
                    transcriptLower.includes("voice mode off")) {
                    
                    switchToAmbientMode(); 
                    postCommandToBackend("turn off voice mode", 'voice');
                    return;
                }

                if (isListeningMode) {
                    postCommandToBackend(transcript, 'voice');
                } 
                else {
                    const functionalTriggers = ["hi ace", "hey ace", "wake up ace", "ok ace", "activate voice mode", "turn on microphone", "voice mode"];
                    let targetTriggerMatch = null;
                    
                    for (let trigger of functionalTriggers) {
                        if (transcriptLower.includes(trigger)) {
                            targetTriggerMatch = trigger;
                            break;
                        }
                    }

                    if (targetTriggerMatch) {
                        switchToActiveListeningMode();
                        let triggerPosition = transcriptLower.indexOf(targetTriggerMatch) + targetTriggerMatch.length;
                        let isolatedTrailingCommand = transcript.substring(triggerPosition).trim();
                        
                        if (isolatedTrailingCommand.length > 0) {
                            postCommandToBackend(autoCorrectSpeechAndPunctuate(isolatedTrailingCommand), 'voice');
                        } else {
                            appendResponseCard("System Core", "Advanced Cognitive Engine line wide open. Speak freely...");
                        }
                    }
                }
            };

            recognition.onerror = (e) => { console.log("Speech tracking exception ignored."); };
            
            recognition.onend = () => { 
                if (shouldRunSpeechEngine && !isServerProcessing) {
                    try { recognition.start(); } catch(err) {}
                }
            };

            if (shouldRunSpeechEngine) { recognition.start(); }
        }

        function switchToActiveListeningMode() {
            shouldRunSpeechEngine = true;
            isListeningMode = true;
            if (audioContext && audioContext.state === 'suspended') { audioContext.resume(); }
            
            const btn = document.getElementById('master-mic-btn');
            const svgIcon = document.getElementById('mic-icon-svg');
            if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
            updateSystemUIState("listening");
            if (svgIcon) svgIcon.innerHTML = `<rect x="6" y="6" width="12" height="12"/>`;
        }

        function turnMicrophoneCompletelyOff() {
            isListeningMode = false;
            shouldRunSpeechEngine = false;
            if (recognition) recognition.stop();
            
            const btn = document.getElementById('master-mic-btn');
            const svgIcon = document.getElementById('mic-icon-svg');
            if (btn) btn.classList.remove('active');
            updateSystemUIState("muted");
            if (svgIcon) svgIcon.innerHTML = `<path d="M12 14c1.66 0 3-1.34 3-3V5c0-1.66-1.34-3-3-3S9 3.34 9 5v6c0 1.66 1.34 3 3 3zm5.3-3c0 3-2.54 5.1-5.3 5.1S6.7 14 6.7 11H5c0 3.41 2.72 6.23 6 6.72V21h2v-3.28c3.28-.48 6-3.3 6-6.72h-1.7z"/>`;
            appendResponseCard("System Core", "Microphone pipeline terminated. Pure Text Mode Active.");
        }

        function switchToAmbientMode() {
            isListeningMode = false;
            shouldRunSpeechEngine = true;
            const btn = document.getElementById('master-mic-btn');
            const svgIcon = document.getElementById('mic-icon-svg');
            if (btn) btn.classList.remove('active');
            updateSystemUIState("idle");
            if (svgIcon) svgIcon.innerHTML = `<path d="M12 14c1.66 0 3-1.34 3-3V5c0-1.66-1.34-3-3-3S9 3.34 9 5v6c0 1.66 1.34 3 3 3zm5.3-3c0 3-2.54 5.1-5.3 5.1S6.7 14 6.7 11H5c0 3.41 2.72 6.23 6 6.72V21h2v-3.28c3.28-.48 6-3.3 6-6.72h-1.7z"/>`;
        }

        function toggleVoiceCapture() {
            if (!shouldRunSpeechEngine || !isListeningMode) { 
                switchToActiveListeningMode();
                try { recognition.start(); } catch(err) {}
            } else { 
                switchToAmbientMode();
                postCommandToBackend("turn off voice mode", 'voice');
            }
        }

        function handleGlobalKeydown(event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter' && document.activeElement !== document.getElementById('chat-entry')) {
                event.preventDefault();
                toggleVoiceCapture();
            }
        }

        function handleTextSubmit(event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter') {
                const inputElement = document.getElementById('chat-entry');
                let commandText = inputElement.value.trim();
                if (!commandText) return;
                inputElement.value = "";
                
                const lowerCmd = commandText.toLowerCase();
                
                if (lowerCmd.includes("activate voice mode") || lowerCmd.includes("turn on microphone") || lowerCmd.includes("voice mode")) {
                    switchToActiveListeningMode();
                    try { recognition.start(); } catch(err) {}
                    postCommandToBackend(commandText, 'voice');
                } else if (lowerCmd.includes("turn microphone off") || lowerCmd.includes("text mode only") || lowerCmd.includes("microphone off") || lowerCmd.includes("turn off voice mode")) {
                    switchToAmbientMode();
                    postCommandToBackend(commandText, 'voice');
                } else {
                    postCommandToBackend(commandText, isListeningMode ? 'voice' : 'text');
                }
            }
        }

        function postCommandToBackend(payloadText, source) {
            updateSystemUIState("processing");
            appendResponseCard(source === 'voice' ? "Aryan (Voice)" : "Aryan (Keyboard)", payloadText);

            document.getElementById('scout-status').innerText = "THINKING";
            document.getElementById('scout-entry').innerText = "Routing transaction package across local array nodes...";

            if (source === 'voice') {
                isServerProcessing = true;
                if (recognition) {
                    try { recognition.stop(); } catch(e) {}
                }
            }

            fetch('/api/command', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ command: payloadText, source: source })
            })
            .then(res => res.json())
            .then(data => {
                document.getElementById('inbox-counter').innerText = `${data.interaction_count} processed entries`;
                document.getElementById('flux-status').innerText = data.context_loaded;

                if (data.type === 'council' || (data.response && typeof data.response === 'object')) {
                    const debate = data.type === 'council' ? data.response : data.response;
                    
                    async function runVisualBoardroomChain() {
                        document.getElementById('scout-status').innerText = data.model.toUpperCase();
                        document.getElementById('scout-entry').innerText = "Boardroom debate analysis in active execution.";

                        updateSystemTheme('#FF453A');
                        appendResponseCard("🎭 The Contrarian", debate.contrarian, data.execution_time);
                        if (source === 'voice') {
                            await fetch('/api/speak', {
                                method: 'POST',
                                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                                body: JSON.stringify({ text: "Analyzing the risk layout from the contrarian. " + debate.contrarian })
                            });
                        } else { await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 1200)); }

                        updateSystemTheme('#BF5AF2');
                        appendResponseCard("🚀 The Synergist", debate.synergist, data.execution_time);
                        if (source === 'voice') {
                            await fetch('/api/speak', {
                                method: 'POST',
                                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                                body: JSON.stringify({ text: "Reviewing the strategy modification from the synergist. " + debate.synergist })
                            });
                        } else { await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 1200)); }

                        updateSystemTheme('#2DD4A8');
                        appendResponseCard("🏛️ The Chairman Summary", debate.chairman, data.execution_time);
                        if (source === 'voice') {
                            await fetch('/api/speak', {
                                method: 'POST',
                                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                                body: JSON.stringify({ text: "The chairman's final evaluation and takeaways. " + debate.chairman })
                            });
                        }

                        finalizeBoardroomTransaction(data.model);
                    }
                    runVisualBoardroomChain();
                } else {
                    if (data.type === 'coding') {
                        const stack = document.getElementById('response-stack');
                        const card = document.createElement('div');
                        card.className = 'response-card';
                        
                        let cleanText = data.response.replace(/```[a-z]*\n([\s\S]*?)```/g, '<pre>$1</pre>');
                        card.innerHTML = `
                            <div class="speaker-tag">Dev Core (${data.model})</div>
                            <div>${cleanText}</div>
                            <div style="font-size: 10px; opacity: 0.4; text-align: right; margin-top: 6px; font-family: monospace; letter-spacing: 0.05em;">LATENCY: ${data.execution_time}s</div>
                        `;
                        stack.appendChild(card);
                        stack.scrollTop = stack.scrollHeight;
                    } else {
                        appendResponseCard("Ace Intelligence", data.response, data.execution_time);
                    }
                    finalizeBoardroomTransaction(data.model);
                }
            })
            .catch(err => {
                appendResponseCard("System Error", "Link dropped.");
                finalizeBoardroomTransaction("OFFLINE");
            });

            function finalizeBoardroomTransaction(activeModelLabel) {
                isServerProcessing = false; 
                updateSystemTheme('#2DD4A8'); 

                document.getElementById('scout-status').innerText = activeModelLabel.toUpperCase();
                document.getElementById('scout-entry').innerText = `Transaction pipeline completed via ${activeModelLabel}.`;

                if (!shouldRunSpeechEngine) updateSystemUIState("muted");
                else updateSystemUIState(isListeningMode ? "listening" : "idle");

                if (source === 'voice' && shouldRunSpeechEngine && recognition) {
                    try { recognition.start(); } catch(e) {}
                }
            }
        }

        function triggerMapModule() { 
            const stack = document.getElementById('response-stack');
            const card = document.createElement('div');
            card.className = 'response-card';
            card.innerHTML = `
                <div class="speaker-tag">System Topology</div>
                <div style="font-family: monospace; font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.4; margin-top: 5px;">
                    [INPUT ROUTING LAYER]<br>
                    &nbsp;&nbsp;│<br>
                    &nbsp;&nbsp;├──► Banter ──► qwen3:4b<br>
                    &nbsp;&nbsp;├──► Scripts ─► qwen2.5-coder:14b<br>
                    &nbsp;&nbsp;└──► Debate ──► deepseek-r1:14b<br><br>
                    [VAD GATEKEEPER]: 1.0s Debounce<br>
                    [AUDIO LINE]: Local Sync Lock
                </div>
            `;
            stack.appendChild(card);
            stack.scrollTop = stack.scrollHeight;
        }
        
        function triggerAlertsModule() { 
            const stack = document.getElementById('response-stack');
            const card = document.createElement('div');
            card.className = 'response-card';
            card.innerHTML = `
                <div class="speaker-tag">Diagnostic Trace</div>
                <div style="font-family: monospace; font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.4; margin-top: 5px;">
                    HOST: localhost:5000<br>
                    EGRESS LEAKS: 0% (BLOCK ACTIVE)<br>
                    OLLAMA PORT: 11434 (STABLE)<br>
                    TTS HARDWARE: CONNECTED<br>
                    VRAM PROFILE: DEPLOYED SECURE
                </div>
            `;
            stack.appendChild(card);
            stack.scrollTop = stack.scrollHeight;
        }

        function updateSystemUIState(state) {
            const text = document.getElementById('system-status-text');
            const dot = document.getElementById('global-status-dot');
            if (!dot) return;
            dot.className = "status-dot";
            
            if(state === "listening") { if(text) text.innerText = "LISTENING"; dot.classList.add('listening'); }
            else if(state === "processing") { if(text) text.innerText = "PROCESSING"; dot.classList.add('processing'); }
            else if(state === "muted") { if(text) text.innerText = "MUTED"; dot.classList.add('muted'); }
            else { if(text) text.innerText = "ONLINE"; dot.classList.add('idle'); }
        }

        function appendResponseCard(speaker, message, duration = null) {
            const stack = document.getElementById('response-stack');
            const card = document.createElement('div');
            card.className = 'response-card';
            
            let durationMarkup = duration ? `<div style="font-size: 10px; opacity: 0.4; text-align: right; margin-top: 6px; font-family: monospace; letter-spacing: 0.05em;">LATENCY: ${duration}s</div>` : '';
            card.innerHTML = `<div class="speaker-tag">${speaker}</div><div>${message}</div>${durationMarkup}`;
            
            stack.appendChild(card);
            stack.scrollTop = stack.scrollHeight; 
        }

        function togglePanel() { document.getElementById('activity-panel').classList.toggle('collapsed'); }

        window.onload = initSpaceScene;
    </script>
</body>
</html>

from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
import os
import sys
import threading
import time
import ollama
import re

# Import Playwright's synchronous API for the browser harness
from playwright.sync_api import sync_playwright

# Import your locked, functional core speech assets
from audio_provider import speak_text
from council import run_council_debate

app = Flask(__name__)

# 🎛️ THE THREE-TIER MATRIX ARCHITECTURE ANCHORS
FAST_MODEL = "qwen3:4b"               # Snappy, highly accurate casual conversation
SMART_MODEL = "deepseek-r1:14b"       # Advanced deep reasoning for research & web synthesis
CODING_MODEL = "qwen2.5-coder:14b"    # Specialized software engineering agent

chat_history = []
interaction_session_counter = 0       # Tracks telemetry counter metrics
pending_memory_clear = False          # Locks state engine when confirmation is required

def should_trigger_council(text):
    text_lower = text.lower()
    triggers = ["council", "debate", "evaluate", "boardroom"]
    negations = ["don't", "dont", "do not", "never", "without", "skip", "stop"]
    if not any(kw in text_lower for kw in triggers): return False
    for neg in negations:
        if neg in text_lower:
            for kw in triggers:
                if kw in text_lower and text_lower.find(neg) < text_lower.find(kw): return False
    return True

def should_trigger_coding_agent(text):
    text_lower = text.lower()
    coding_keywords = [
        "code", "script", "program", "python", "javascript", "html", "css", 
        "function", "class", "compile", "debug", "refactor"
    ]
    return any(keyword in text_lower for keyword in coding_keywords)

# 🌐 BROWSER HARNESS GATEWAY: Detects if the intent requires live web extraction
def should_trigger_browser(text):
    text_lower = text.lower()
    browser_keywords = ["search", "browse", "look up", "website", "live info", "current price", "news about"]
    return any(keyword in text_lower for keyword in browser_keywords)

# 🤖 HERMES BROWSER HARNESS ENGINE: Launches automation tool to scrape data
def execute_browser_harness(user_query):
    print(f"🌐 [Browser Harness]: Initializing Chromium instance for query: '{user_query}'")
    
    # Step A: Use the fast model to formulate a clean search query or deduce an target URL
    search_prompt = f"Extract only the most ideal web search terms or direct URL from this request. Output nothing else but the raw search keywords or URL string: '{user_query}'"
    try:
        response = ollama.chat(model=FAST_MODEL, messages=[{"role": "user", "content": search_prompt}])
        target_search = response['message']['content'].strip().replace('"', '').replace("'", "")
    except:
        target_search = user_query

    # Fallback to duckduckgo for general text lookups if a direct URL wasn't provided
    if not target_search.startswith("http"):
        target_url = f"https://html.duckduckgo.com/html/?q={target_search.replace(' ', '+')}"
    else:
        target_url = target_search

    scraped_content = ""
    try:
        with sync_playwright() as p:
            # Launch headless browser securely
            browser = p.chromium.launch(headless=True)
            page = browser.new_page()
            
            print(f"🛰️ [Browser Harness]: Navigating to portal -> {target_url}")
            page.goto(target_url, timeout=10000)
            page.wait_for_load_state("domcontentloaded")
            
            # Extract raw inner text from body, filtering out script elements
            raw_text = page.inner_text("body")
            
            # Clean up excessive whitespace formatting
            clean_lines = [line.strip() for line in raw_text.splitlines() if line.strip()]
            scraped_content = " ".join(clean_lines[:40]) # Grab the top 40 compressed content lines
            browser.close()
            print("✅ [Browser Harness]: Automation pass completed. Context extracted successfully.")
    except Exception as browser_err:
        print(f"❌ [Browser Harness Failure]: Reason: {browser_err}")
        scraped_content = "Error: Unable to connect to the targeted live network node."

    return scraped_content

def execute_audio_playback(text_to_speak):
    try:
        try:
            import pythoncom
            pythoncom.CoInitialize()
        except ImportError:
            pass
        print(f"🔊 [Audio Engine: Vocalizing response via system hardware...]")
        speak_text(text_to_speak)
        print(f"✅ [Audio Engine: Playback transaction complete.]")
    except Exception as tts_error:
        print(f"❌ [Audio Engine Crash]: Reason: {tts_error}")

@app.route('/')
def serve_dashboard_console():
    try:
        with open('index.html', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: return f.read()
    except Exception as e: return f"System Matrix Failure: {e}"

@app.route('/three.min.js')
def serve_local_three_js():
    try:
        with open('three.min.js', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: 
            return f.read(), 200, {'Content-Type': 'application/javascript'}
    except Exception as e: 
        return f"Graphics Engine Asset Failure: {e}", 404

@app.route('/api/speak', methods=['POST'])
def handle_isolated_playback():
    data = request.get_json() or {}
    text = data.get('text', '').strip()
    if text:
        execute_audio_playback(text)
    return jsonify({"status": "vocalization_complete"})

@app.route('/api/command', methods=['POST'])
def orchestrate_command_routing():
    global chat_history, pending_memory_clear, interaction_session_counter
    start_time = time.time()
    
    data = request.get_json() or {}
    command = data.get('command', '').strip()
    source = data.get('source', 'text')
    
    if not command: return jsonify({"response": "Empty transaction payload.", "execution_time": 0.0})
    
    interaction_session_counter += 1
    print(f"\n📥 Transaction received from [{source.upper()}]: \"{command}\"")
    lower_cmd = command.lower()
    context_string = f"{len(chat_history)}/20 SLOTS"

    # 🛑 MEMORY PURGE LAYER INTERCEPTS
    if pending_memory_clear:
        if "yes" in lower_cmd or "confirm" in lower_cmd or "do it" in lower_cmd:
            chat_history = []
            pending_memory_clear = False
            reply = "Memory banks cleared. Active conversation logs are fully purged, Aryan."
            if source == 'voice': execute_audio_playback(reply)
            return jsonify({"response": reply, "type": "standard", "model": FAST_MODEL, "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": "0/20 SLOTS", "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})
        elif "no" in lower_cmd or "cancel" in lower_cmd or "abort" in lower_cmd:
            pending_memory_clear = False
            reply = "Purge canceled. Memory logs preserved safely, Aryan."
            if source == 'voice': execute_audio_playback(reply)
            return jsonify({"response": reply, "type": "standard", "model": FAST_MODEL, "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})
        else:
            pending_memory_clear = False  
            reply = "Invalid confirmation vector. Purge sequence aborted to protect data integrity."
            if source == 'voice': execute_audio_playback(reply)
            return jsonify({"response": reply, "type": "standard", "model": FAST_MODEL, "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})

    purge_actions = ["clear", "wipe", "reset", "delete", "purge", "forget", "erase"]
    memory_targets = ["memory", "history", "logs", "context", "cache"]
    if any(action in lower_cmd for action in purge_actions) and any(target in lower_cmd for target in memory_targets):
        pending_memory_clear = True
        reply = "Are you absolutely sure you want to purge my active memory logs, Aryan? Please confirm with a 'yes' or 'no'."
        if source == 'voice': execute_audio_playback(reply)
        return jsonify({"response": reply, "type": "standard", "model": FAST_MODEL, "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})

    # 🎛️ PASSIVE STANDBY COMPLIANCE TRIPS
    if any(x in lower_cmd for x in ["turn microphone off", "deactivate voice channels", "microphone off", "turn off voice mode", "voice mode off"]):
        reply = "Understood, Aryan. Entering passive standby mode. Say 'Activate voice mode' or 'Hey Ace' when you need me again."
        if source == 'voice': execute_audio_playback(reply)
        return jsonify({"response": reply, "type": "standard", "model": FAST_MODEL, "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})
        
    if any(x in lower_cmd for x in ["activate voice mode", "turn on microphone", "voice mode"]):
        reply = "Advanced Cognitive Engine arrays online, Aryan. Audio tracking channel locked open."
        execute_audio_playback(reply)
        return jsonify({"response": reply, "type": "standard", "model": FAST_MODEL, "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})

    # 🏛️ CASE A: MULTI-AGENT COUNCIL ROUTING
    if should_trigger_council(command):
        print(f"👥 Assembling Research Council Boardroom Core using {SMART_MODEL}...")
        debate_packet = run_council_debate(command) 
        return jsonify({"response": debate_packet, "type": "council", "model": SMART_MODEL, "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})

    # 🌐 CASE B: AUTONOMOUS HERMES BROWSER HARNESS (Grabs web content, reasons with DeepSeek)
    elif should_trigger_browser(command):
        # 1. Spin up Playwright tool payload
        web_context = execute_browser_harness(command)
        
        # 2. Package the findings and route them to DeepSeek-R1 for intelligent synthesis
        hermes_instructions = (
            f"You are Ace operating with an autonomous Hermes Browser Harness integration. "
            f"Analyze this raw scraped web data context carefully and synthesize a highly accurate, short response for Aryan: '{web_context}'"
        )
        try:
            response = ollama.chat(
                model=SMART_MODEL,
                messages=[
                    {"role": "system", "content": hermes_instructions},
                    {"role": "user", "content": f"Based on that fresh web trace context data, resolve this: {command}"}
                ]
            )
            reply = response['message']['content']
            
            # Clean up DeepSeek's native internal thinking tokens if present
            reply = re.sub(r'<think>[\s\S]*?</think>', '', reply).strip()
            
            if source == 'voice': execute_audio_playback(reply)
            return jsonify({"response": reply, "type": "browser", "model": "hermes-harness", "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})
        except Exception as e:
            return jsonify({"response": f"Hermes processing anomaly: {e}", "type": "browser", "model": "hermes-harness", "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})

    # 💻 CASE C: SURGICAL CODING AGENT ROUTING
    elif should_trigger_coding_agent(command):
        print(f"🛠️ Detecting development requirements. Activating Coding Agent -> {CODING_MODEL}")
        coding_instructions = "You are the Core Software Engineering Agent of the Advanced Cognitive Engine. Provide optimal programming blocks. Keep explanations brief."
        try:
            response = ollama.chat(model=CODING_MODEL, messages=[{"role": "system", "content": coding_instructions}, {"role": "user", "content": command}])
            reply = response['message']['content']
            if source == 'voice': execute_audio_playback("Code architecture compiled successfully. Dropping snippets into viewports.")
            return jsonify({"response": reply, "type": "coding", "model": CODING_MODEL, "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})
        except Exception as e:
            return jsonify({"response": f"Coding pipeline dropped: {e}", "type": "coding", "model": CODING_MODEL, "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})

    # ⚡ CASE D: SNAPPY CONVERSATIONAL ROUTATION
    else:
        print(f"⚡ Pacing layer optimally -> routing conversational query through {FAST_MODEL}")
        messages_payload = [
            {"role": "system", "content": "You are Ace, an elite Advanced Cognitive Engine desktop assistant for Aryan. Speak with a witty cadence like Jarvis. Keep responses strictly limited to 1 or 2 sentences maximum."}
        ]
        messages_payload.extend(chat_history)
        messages_payload.append({"role": "user", "content": command})

        try:
            response = ollama.chat(model=FAST_MODEL, messages=messages_payload)
            reply = response['message']['content']
            
            chat_history.append({"role": "user", "content": command})
            chat_history.append({"role": "assistant", "content": reply})
            if len(chat_history) > 20: chat_history = chat_history[-20:]
            context_string = f"{len(chat_history)}/20 SLOTS"

            if source == 'voice': execute_audio_playback(reply)
            return jsonify({"response": reply, "type": "standard", "model": FAST_MODEL, "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})
        except Exception as e:
            return jsonify({"response": f"Conversational pipeline dropped: {e}", "type": "standard", "model": FAST_MODEL, "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})

if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(host='0.0.0.0', port=5000, debug=False)

        </div>
        <div class="hint-text">WAKE: "ACTIVATE VOICE MODE" // STANDBY: "TURN OFF VOICE MODE"</div>
    </div>

    <script src="/three.min.js"></script>
    <script>
        let scene, camera, renderer, starParticles, orbMesh, orbGlow;
        let recognition;
        
        let isListeningMode = false;       
        let shouldRunSpeechEngine = true;  
        let isServerProcessing = false;    

        let audioContext, audioAnalyser, audioDataArray;
        let liveMicrophoneAmplitude = 0.0;

        function updateSystemTheme(hexColor) {
            document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--accent-glow', hexColor);
            document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--accent-card-border', hexColor);
            if (orbMesh && orbMesh.material) orbMesh.material.color.set(hexColor);
            if (orbGlow && orbGlow.material) orbGlow.material.color.set(hexColor);
        }

        function autoCorrectSpeechAndPunctuate(text) {
            let corrected = text.trim();
            if (!corrected) return "";

            const translationMap = {
                "quan": "Qwen",
                "quan 2.5": "Qwen 2.5",
                "queen 2.5": "Qwen 2.5",
                "quinn": "Qwen",
                "gwen": "Qwen",
                "lama": "Llama",
                "llama 3.2": "Llama 3.2",
                "ace": "Ace"
            };

            for (const [misheard, accurate] of Object.entries(translationMap)) {
                const regex = new RegExp(`\\b${misheard}\\b`, 'gi');
                corrected = corrected.replace(regex, accurate);
            }
            
            corrected = corrected.replace(/llama/gi, "Llama");
            corrected = corrected.replace(/qwen/gi, "Qwen");

            if (!/[.!?]$/.test(corrected)) {
                const lower = corrected.toLowerCase();
                const questionTriggers = ["who", "what", "where", "when", "why", "how", "can", "is", "are", "do", "does", "should", "could", "would"];
                const firstWord = lower.split(" ")[0];
                
                if (questionTriggers.includes(firstWord)) corrected += "?";
                else corrected += ".";
            }
            return corrected;
        }

        function initSpaceScene() {
            const container = document.getElementById('canvas-container');
            
            scene = new THREE.Scene();
            camera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(60, window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight, 0.1, 1000);
            camera.position.z = 5;

            renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({ antialias: true, alpha: false });
            renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
            renderer.setPixelRatio(window.devicePixelRatio);
            container.appendChild(renderer.domElement);

            const starGeometry = new THREE.BufferGeometry();
            const starCount = 1200;
            const starPositions = new Float32Array(starCount * 3);
            for(let i=0; i < starCount * 3; i++) {
                starPositions[i] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 15;
            }
            starGeometry.setAttribute('position', new THREE.BufferAttribute(starPositions, 3));
            const starMaterial = new THREE.PointsMaterial({ color: 0xffffff, size: 0.02, transparent: true, opacity: 0.8 });
            starParticles = new THREE.Points(starGeometry, starMaterial);
            scene.add(starParticles);

            const orbGeometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.6, 64, 64);
            const orbMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color: 0x2DD4A8 });
            orbMesh = new THREE.Mesh(orbGeometry, orbMaterial);
            scene.add(orbMesh);

            const glowGeometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.8, 32, 32);
            const glowMaterial = new THREE.MeshBasicMaterial({ color: 0x2DD4A8, transparent: true, opacity: 0.25, side: THREE.BackSide });
            orbGlow = new THREE.Mesh(glowGeometry, glowMaterial);
            scene.add(orbGlow);

            window.addEventListener('resize', onWindowResize);
            document.addEventListener('keydown', handleGlobalKeydown);

            initUnifiedSpeechEngine();
            initHardwareAudioAnalyzer();
            animateLoop();
        }

        function initHardwareAudioAnalyzer() {
            navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ audio: true })
            .then(stream => {
                const AudioContextClass = window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext;
                audioContext = new AudioContextClass();
                const sourceNode = audioContext.createMediaStreamSource(stream);
                audioAnalyser = audioContext.createAnalyser();
                audioAnalyser.fftSize = 256;
                const bufferLength = audioAnalyser.frequencyBinCount;
                audioDataArray = new Uint8Array(bufferLength);
                sourceNode.connect(audioAnalyser);
            })
            .catch(err => { console.log("⚠️ Acoustic analyzer link standby."); });
        }

        function animateLoop() {
            requestAnimationFrame(animateLoop);
            const time = Date.now() * 0.001;
            let breathingFactor = Math.sin(time * 1.5) * 0.04;
            
            if (shouldRunSpeechEngine && audioAnalyser && audioDataArray) {
                audioAnalyser.getByteFrequencyData(audioDataArray);
                let totalFrequencySum = 0;
                for (let i = 0; i < audioDataArray.length; i++) { totalFrequencySum += audioDataArray[i]; }
                let calculatedAverage = totalFrequencySum / audioDataArray.length;
                let targetAmplitude = calculatedAverage / 128.0;
                liveMicrophoneAmplitude += (targetAmplitude - liveMicrophoneAmplitude) * 0.2;
            } else {
                liveMicrophoneAmplitude += (0.0 - liveMicrophoneAmplitude) * 0.1;
            }

            let finalScalingFactor = 1.0 + breathingFactor + (liveMicrophoneAmplitude * 1.2);
            if (orbMesh) orbMesh.scale.set(finalScalingFactor, finalScalingFactor, finalScalingFactor);
            if (orbGlow) orbGlow.scale.set(finalScalingFactor * 1.25, finalScalingFactor * 1.25, finalScalingFactor * 1.25);
            if (starParticles) starParticles.rotation.y = time * 0.02;
            renderer.render(scene, camera);
        }

        function onWindowResize() {
            camera.aspect = window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight;
            camera.updateProjectionMatrix();
            renderer.setSize(window.innerWidth, window.innerHeight);
        }

        function initUnifiedSpeechEngine() {
            if (!('webkitSpeechRecognition' in window) && !('SpeechRecognition' in window)) {
                appendResponseCard("Hardware Alert", "Speech recognition structures not supported.");
                return;
            }

            const SpeechRecognition = window.SpeechRecognition || window.webkitSpeechRecognition;
            recognition = new SpeechRecognition();
            recognition.continuous = true;
            recognition.interimResults = false;
            recognition.lang = 'en-US';

            if ('processLocally' in recognition) {
                recognition.processLocally = true;
            } else if ('localService' in recognition) {
                recognition.localService = true; 
            }

            recognition.onresult = (event) => {
                if (!shouldRunSpeechEngine || isServerProcessing) return; 
                
                const lastIndex = event.resultIndex;
                const rawTranscript = event.results[lastIndex][0].transcript.trim();
                const transcript = autoCorrectSpeechAndPunctuate(rawTranscript);
                const transcriptLower = transcript.toLowerCase();
                
                console.log("Core Captured token:", transcript);

                if (transcriptLower.includes("microphone off") || 
                    transcriptLower.includes("text mode only") || 
                    transcriptLower.includes("turn microphone off") || 
                    transcriptLower.includes("turn off voice mode") || 
                    transcriptLower.includes("voice mode off")) {
                    
                    switchToAmbientMode(); 
                    postCommandToBackend("turn off voice mode", 'voice');
                    return;
                }

                if (isListeningMode) {
                    postCommandToBackend(transcript, 'voice');
                } 
                else {
                    const functionalTriggers = ["hi ace", "hey ace", "wake up ace", "ok ace", "activate voice mode", "turn on microphone", "voice mode"];
                    let targetTriggerMatch = null;
                    
                    for (let trigger of functionalTriggers) {
                        if (transcriptLower.includes(trigger)) {
                            targetTriggerMatch = trigger;
                            break;
                        }
                    }

                    if (targetTriggerMatch) {
                        switchToActiveListeningMode();
                        let triggerPosition = transcriptLower.indexOf(targetTriggerMatch) + targetTriggerMatch.length;
                        let isolatedTrailingCommand = transcript.substring(triggerPosition).trim();
                        
                        if (isolatedTrailingCommand.length > 0) {
                            postCommandToBackend(autoCorrectSpeechAndPunctuate(isolatedTrailingCommand), 'voice');
                        } else {
                            appendResponseCard("System Core", "Advanced Cognitive Engine line wide open. Speak freely...");
                        }
                    }
                }
            };

            recognition.onerror = (e) => { console.log("Speech tracking exception ignored."); };
            
            recognition.onend = () => { 
                if (shouldRunSpeechEngine && !isServerProcessing) {
                    try { recognition.start(); } catch(err) {}
                }
            };

            if (shouldRunSpeechEngine) { recognition.start(); }
        }

        function switchToActiveListeningMode() {
            shouldRunSpeechEngine = true;
            isListeningMode = true;
            if (audioContext && audioContext.state === 'suspended') { audioContext.resume(); }
            
            const btn = document.getElementById('master-mic-btn');
            const svgIcon = document.getElementById('mic-icon-svg');
            if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
            updateSystemUIState("listening");
            if (svgIcon) svgIcon.innerHTML = `<rect x="6" y="6" width="12" height="12"/>`;
        }

        function turnMicrophoneCompletelyOff() {
            isListeningMode = false;
            shouldRunSpeechEngine = false;
            if (recognition) recognition.stop();
            
            const btn = document.getElementById('master-mic-btn');
            const svgIcon = document.getElementById('mic-icon-svg');
            if (btn) btn.classList.remove('active');
            updateSystemUIState("muted");
            if (svgIcon) svgIcon.innerHTML = `<path d="M12 14c1.66 0 3-1.34 3-3V5c0-1.66-1.34-3-3-3S9 3.34 9 5v6c0 1.66 1.34 3 3 3zm5.3-3c0 3-2.54 5.1-5.3 5.1S6.7 14 6.7 11H5c0 3.41 2.72 6.23 6 6.72V21h2v-3.28c3.28-.48 6-3.3 6-6.72h-1.7z"/>`;
            appendResponseCard("System Core", "Microphone pipeline terminated. Pure Text Mode Active.");
        }

        function switchToAmbientMode() {
            isListeningMode = false;
            shouldRunSpeechEngine = true;
            const btn = document.getElementById('master-mic-btn');
            const svgIcon = document.getElementById('mic-icon-svg');
            if (btn) btn.classList.remove('active');
            updateSystemUIState("idle");
            if (svgIcon) svgIcon.innerHTML = `<path d="M12 14c1.66 0 3-1.34 3-3V5c0-1.66-1.34-3-3-3S9 3.34 9 5v6c0 1.66 1.34 3 3 3zm5.3-3c0 3-2.54 5.1-5.3 5.1S6.7 14 6.7 11H5c0 3.41 2.72 6.23 6 6.72V21h2v-3.28c3.28-.48 6-3.3 6-6.72h-1.7z"/>`;
        }

        function toggleVoiceCapture() {
            if (!shouldRunSpeechEngine || !isListeningMode) { 
                switchToActiveListeningMode();
                try { recognition.start(); } catch(err) {}
            } else { 
                switchToAmbientMode();
                postCommandToBackend("turn off voice mode", 'voice');
            }
        }

        function handleGlobalKeydown(event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter' && document.activeElement !== document.getElementById('chat-entry')) {
                event.preventDefault();
                toggleVoiceCapture();
            }
        }

        function handleTextSubmit(event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter') {
                const inputElement = document.getElementById('chat-entry');
                let commandText = inputElement.value.trim();
                if (!commandText) return;
                inputElement.value = "";
                
                const lowerCmd = commandText.toLowerCase();
                
                if (lowerCmd.includes("activate voice mode") || lowerCmd.includes("turn on microphone") || lowerCmd.includes("voice mode")) {
                    switchToActiveListeningMode();
                    try { recognition.start(); } catch(err) {}
                    postCommandToBackend(commandText, 'voice');
                } else if (lowerCmd.includes("turn microphone off") || lowerCmd.includes("text mode only") || lowerCmd.includes("microphone off") || lowerCmd.includes("turn off voice mode")) {
                    switchToAmbientMode();
                    postCommandToBackend(commandText, 'voice');
                } else {
                    postCommandToBackend(commandText, isListeningMode ? 'voice' : 'text');
                }
            }
        }

        function postCommandToBackend(payloadText, source) {
            updateSystemUIState("processing");
            appendResponseCard(source === 'voice' ? "Aryan (Voice)" : "Aryan (Keyboard)", payloadText);

            document.getElementById('scout-status').innerText = "THINKING";
            document.getElementById('scout-entry').innerText = "Routing transaction package across local array nodes...";

            if (source === 'voice') {
                isServerProcessing = true;
                if (recognition) {
                    try { recognition.stop(); } catch(e) {}
                }
            }

            fetch('/api/command', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ command: payloadText, source: source })
            })
            .then(res => res.json())
            .then(data => {
                document.getElementById('inbox-counter').innerText = `${data.interaction_count} processed entries`;
                document.getElementById('flux-status').innerText = data.context_loaded;

                if (data.type === 'council' || (data.response && typeof data.response === 'object')) {
                    const debate = data.type === 'council' ? data.response : data.response;
                    
                    async function runVisualBoardroomChain() {
                        document.getElementById('scout-status').innerText = data.model.toUpperCase();
                        document.getElementById('scout-entry').innerText = "Boardroom debate analysis in active execution.";

                        updateSystemTheme('#FF453A');
                        appendResponseCard("🎭 The Contrarian", debate.contrarian, data.execution_time);
                        if (source === 'voice') {
                            await fetch('/api/speak', {
                                method: 'POST',
                                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                                body: JSON.stringify({ text: "Analyzing the risk layout from the contrarian. " + debate.contrarian })
                            });
                        } else { await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 1200)); }

                        updateSystemTheme('#BF5AF2');
                        appendResponseCard("🚀 The Synergist", debate.synergist, data.execution_time);
                        if (source === 'voice') {
                            await fetch('/api/speak', {
                                method: 'POST',
                                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                                body: JSON.stringify({ text: "Reviewing the strategy modification from the synergist. " + debate.synergist })
                            });
                        } else { await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 1200)); }

                        updateSystemTheme('#2DD4A8');
                        appendResponseCard("🏛️ The Chairman Summary", debate.chairman, data.execution_time);
                        if (source === 'voice') {
                            await fetch('/api/speak', {
                                method: 'POST',
                                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                                body: JSON.stringify({ text: "The chairman's final evaluation and takeaways. " + debate.chairman })
                            });
                        }

                        finalizeBoardroomTransaction(data.model);
                    }
                    runVisualBoardroomChain();
                } else {
                    if (data.type === 'coding' || data.type === 'browser') {
                        const stack = document.getElementById('response-stack');
                        const card = document.createElement('div');
                        card.className = 'response-card';
                        
                        let cleanText = data.response.replace(/```[a-z]*\n([\s\S]*?)```/g, '<pre>$1</pre>');
                        let tagLabel = data.type === 'coding' ? `Dev Core (${data.model})` : `Hermes Harness (${data.model})`;
                        
                        card.innerHTML = `
                            <div class="speaker-tag">${tagLabel}</div>
                            <div>${cleanText}</div>
                            <div style="font-size: 10px; opacity: 0.4; text-align: right; margin-top: 6px; font-family: monospace; letter-spacing: 0.05em;">LATENCY: ${data.execution_time}s</div>
                        `;
                        stack.appendChild(card);
                        stack.scrollTop = stack.scrollHeight;
                    } else {
                        appendResponseCard("Ace Intelligence", data.response, data.execution_time);
                    }
                    finalizeBoardroomTransaction(data.model);
                }
            })
            .catch(err => {
                appendResponseCard("System Error", "Link dropped.");
                finalizeBoardroomTransaction("OFFLINE");
            });

            function finalizeBoardroomTransaction(activeModelLabel) {
                isServerProcessing = false; 
                updateSystemTheme('#2DD4A8'); 

                document.getElementById('scout-status').innerText = activeModelLabel.toUpperCase();
                document.getElementById('scout-entry').innerText = `Transaction pipeline completed via ${activeModelLabel}.`;

                if (!shouldRunSpeechEngine) updateSystemUIState("muted");
                else updateSystemUIState(isListeningMode ? "listening" : "idle");

                if (source === 'voice' && shouldRunSpeechEngine && recognition) {
                    try { recognition.start(); } catch(e) {}
                }
            }
        }

        function triggerMapModule() { 
            const stack = document.getElementById('response-stack');
            const card = document.createElement('div');
            card.className = 'response-card';
            card.innerHTML = `
                <div class="speaker-tag">System Topology</div>
                <div style="font-family: monospace; font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.4; margin-top: 5px;">
                    [INPUT ROUTING LAYER]<br>
                    &nbsp;&nbsp;│<br>
                    &nbsp;&nbsp;├──► Banter ──► qwen3:4b<br>
                    &nbsp;&nbsp;├──► Scripts ─► qwen2.5-coder:14b<br>
                    &nbsp;&nbsp;├──► Browser ─► playwright_harness<br>
                    &nbsp;&nbsp;└──► Debate ──► deepseek-r1:14b<br><br>
                    [VAD GATEKEEPER]: 1.0s Debounce<br>
                    [AUDIO LINE]: Local Sync Lock
                </div>
            `;
            stack.appendChild(card);
            stack.scrollTop = stack.scrollHeight;
        }
        
        function triggerAlertsModule() { 
            const stack = document.getElementById('response-stack');
            const card = document.createElement('div');
            card.className = 'response-card';
            card.innerHTML = `
                <div class="speaker-tag">Diagnostic Trace</div>
                <div style="font-family: monospace; font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.4; margin-top: 5px;">
                    HOST: localhost:5000<br>
                    PLAYWRIGHT DRIVER: Headless Chromium<br>
                    OLLAMA PORT: 11434 (STABLE)<br>
                    TTS HARDWARE: CONNECTED<br>
                    VRAM PROFILE: DEPLOYED SECURE
                </div>
            `;
            stack.appendChild(card);
            stack.scrollTop = stack.scrollHeight;
        }

        function updateSystemUIState(state) {
            const text = document.getElementById('system-status-text');
            const dot = document.getElementById('global-status-dot');
            if (!dot) return;
            dot.className = "status-dot";
            
            if(state === "listening") { if(text) text.innerText = "LISTENING"; dot.classList.add('listening'); }
            else if(state === "processing") { if(text) text.innerText = "PROCESSING"; dot.classList.add('processing'); }
            else if(state === "muted") { if(text) text.innerText = "MUTED"; dot.classList.add('muted'); }
            else { if(text) text.innerText = "ONLINE"; dot.classList.add('idle'); }
        }

        function appendResponseCard(speaker, message, duration = null) {
            const stack = document.getElementById('response-stack');
            const card = document.createElement('div');
            card.className = 'response-card';
            
            let durationMarkup = duration ? `<div style="font-size: 10px; opacity: 0.4; text-align: right; margin-top: 6px; font-family: monospace; letter-spacing: 0.05em;">LATENCY: ${duration}s</div>` : '';
            card.innerHTML = `<div class="speaker-tag">${speaker}</div><div>${message}</div>${durationMarkup}`;
            
            stack.appendChild(card);
            stack.scrollTop = stack.scrollHeight; 
        }

        function togglePanel() { document.getElementById('activity-panel').classList.toggle('collapsed'); }

        window.onload = initSpaceScene;
    </script>
</body>
</html>

from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
import os
import sys
import threading
import time
import ollama
import re

# Import Playwright framework for automated web routing
from playwright.sync_api import sync_playwright

# Import your locked, functional core speech assets
from audio_provider import speak_text
from council import run_council_debate

app = Flask(__name__)

# 🎛️ THE THREE-TIER MATRIX ARCHITECTURE ANCHORS
FAST_MODEL = "qwen3:4b"               # Snappy, highly accurate casual conversation
SMART_MODEL = "deepseek-r1:14b"       # Advanced deep reasoning for research & web synthesis
CODING_MODEL = "qwen2.5-coder:14b"    # Specialized software engineering agent

chat_history = []
interaction_session_counter = 0       # Tracks telemetry counter metrics
pending_memory_clear = False          # Locks state engine when confirmation is required

def should_trigger_council(text):
    text_lower = text.lower()
    triggers = ["council", "debate", "evaluate", "boardroom"]
    negations = ["don't", "dont", "do not", "never", "without", "skip", "stop"]
    if not any(kw in text_lower for kw in triggers): return False
    for neg in negations:
        if neg in text_lower:
            for kw in triggers:
                if kw in text_lower and text_lower.find(neg) < text_lower.find(kw): return False
    return True

def should_trigger_coding_agent(text):
    text_lower = text.lower()
    coding_keywords = [
        "code", "script", "program", "python", "javascript", "html", "css", 
        "function", "class", "compile", "debug", "refactor"
    ]
    return any(keyword in text_lower for keyword in coding_keywords)

def should_trigger_browser(text):
    text_lower = text.lower()
    browser_keywords = ["search", "browse", "look up", "website", "live info", "current price", "news about"]
    return any(keyword in text_lower for keyword in browser_keywords)

def execute_browser_harness(user_query):
    print(f"🌐 [Browser Harness]: Initializing Chromium instance for query: '{user_query}'")
    search_prompt = f"Extract only the most ideal web search terms or direct URL from this request. Output nothing else but the raw search keywords or URL string: '{user_query}'"
    try:
        response = ollama.chat(model=FAST_MODEL, messages=[{"role": "user", "content": search_prompt}])
        target_search = response['message']['content'].strip().replace('"', '').replace("'", "")
    except:
        target_search = user_query

    if not target_search.startswith("http"):
        target_url = f"https://html.duckduckgo.com/html/?q={target_search.replace(' ', '+')}"
    else:
        target_url = target_search

    scraped_content = ""
    try:
        with sync_playwright() as p:
            browser = p.chromium.launch(headless=True)
            page = browser.new_page()
            print(f"🛰️ [Browser Harness]: Navigating to portal -> {target_url}")
            page.goto(target_url, timeout=10000)
            page.wait_for_load_state("domcontentloaded")
            raw_text = page.inner_text("body")
            clean_lines = [line.strip() for line in raw_text.splitlines() if line.strip()]
            scraped_content = " ".join(clean_lines[:40])
            browser.close()
            print("✅ [Browser Harness]: Context extracted successfully.")
    except Exception as browser_err:
        print(f"❌ [Browser Harness Failure]: Reason: {browser_err}")
        scraped_content = "Error: Unable to connect to the targeted live network node."

    return scraped_content

def execute_audio_playback(text_to_speak):
    try:
        try:
            import pythoncom
            pythoncom.CoInitialize()
        except ImportError:
            pass
        print(f"🔊 [Audio Engine: Vocalizing response via system hardware...]")
        speak_text(text_to_speak)
        print(f"✅ [Audio Engine: Playback transaction complete.]")
    except Exception as tts_error:
        print(f"❌ [Audio Engine Crash]: Reason: {tts_error}")

@app.route('/')
def serve_dashboard_console():
    try:
        with open('index.html', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: return f.read()
    except Exception as e: return f"System Matrix Failure: {e}"

@app.route('/three.min.js')
def serve_local_three_js():
    try:
        with open('three.min.js', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: 
            return f.read(), 200, {'Content-Type': 'application/javascript'}
    except Exception as e: 
        return f"Graphics Engine Asset Failure: {e}", 404

@app.route('/api/speak', methods=['POST'])
def handle_isolated_playback():
    data = request.get_json() or {}
    text = data.get('text', '').strip()
    if text:
        execute_audio_playback(text)
    return jsonify({"status": "vocalization_complete"})

@app.route('/api/command', methods=['POST'])
def orchestrate_command_routing():
    global chat_history, pending_memory_clear, interaction_session_counter
    start_time = time.time()
    
    data = request.get_json() or {}
    command = data.get('command', '').strip()
    source = data.get('source', 'text')
    
    if not command: return jsonify({"response": "Empty transaction payload.", "execution_time": 0.0})
    
    interaction_session_counter += 1
    print(f"\n📥 Transaction received from [{source.upper()}]: \"{command}\"")
    lower_cmd = command.lower()
    context_string = f"{len(chat_history)}/20 SLOTS"

    # 🛑 MEMORY PURGE LAYER INTERCEPTS
    if pending_memory_clear:
        if "yes" in lower_cmd or "confirm" in lower_cmd or "do it" in lower_cmd:
            chat_history = []
            pending_memory_clear = False
            reply = "Memory banks cleared. Active conversation logs are fully purged, Aryan."
            if source == 'voice': execute_audio_playback(reply)
            return jsonify({"response": reply, "type": "standard", "model": FAST_MODEL, "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": "0/20 SLOTS", "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})
        elif "no" in lower_cmd or "cancel" in lower_cmd or "abort" in lower_cmd:
            pending_memory_clear = False
            reply = "Purge canceled. Memory logs preserved safely, Aryan."
            if source == 'voice': execute_audio_playback(reply)
            return jsonify({"response": reply, "type": "standard", "model": FAST_MODEL, "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})
        else:
            pending_memory_clear = False  
            reply = "Invalid confirmation vector. Purge sequence aborted to protect data integrity."
            if source == 'voice': execute_audio_playback(reply)
            return jsonify({"response": reply, "type": "standard", "model": FAST_MODEL, "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})

    purge_actions = ["clear", "wipe", "reset", "delete", "purge", "forget", "erase"]
    memory_targets = ["memory", "history", "logs", "context", "cache"]
    if any(action in lower_cmd for action in purge_actions) and any(target in lower_cmd for target in memory_targets):
        pending_memory_clear = True
        reply = "Are you absolutely sure you want to purge my active memory logs, Aryan? Please confirm with a 'yes' or 'no'."
        if source == 'voice': execute_audio_playback(reply)
        return jsonify({"response": reply, "type": "standard", "model": FAST_MODEL, "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})

    # 🎛️ VOICE CONTROL COMMAND HANDLERS
    if any(x in lower_cmd for x in ["turn microphone off", "deactivate voice channels", "microphone off", "turn off voice mode", "voice mode off"]):
        reply = "Understood, Aryan. Entering passive standby mode. Say 'Activate voice mode' or 'Hey Ace' when you need me again."
        if source == 'voice': execute_audio_playback(reply)
        return jsonify({"response": reply, "type": "shutdown", "model": FAST_MODEL, "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})
        
    if any(x in lower_cmd for x in ["activate voice mode", "turn on microphone", "voice mode"]):
        reply = "Advanced Cognitive Engine arrays online, Aryan. Audio tracking channel locked open."
        execute_audio_playback(reply)
        return jsonify({"response": reply, "type": "wakeup", "model": FAST_MODEL, "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})

    # 🏛️ CASE A: MULTI-AGENT COUNCIL ROUTING
    if should_trigger_council(command):
        print(f"👥 Assembling Research Council Boardroom Core using {SMART_MODEL}...")
        debate_packet = run_council_debate(command) 
        return jsonify({"response": debate_packet, "type": "council", "model": SMART_MODEL, "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})

    # 🌐 CASE B: AUTONOMOUS BROWSER HARNESS
    elif should_trigger_browser(command):
        web_context = execute_browser_harness(command)
        hermes_instructions = (
            f"You are Ace operating with an autonomous Browser Harness integration. "
            f"Analyze this raw scraped data context and synthesize a short response for Aryan: '{web_context}'"
        )
        try:
            response = ollama.chat(
                model=SMART_MODEL,
                messages=[
                    {"role": "system", "content": hermes_instructions},
                    {"role": "user", "content": f"Based on that fresh web trace context data, resolve this: {command}"}
                ]
            )
            reply = response['message']['content']
            reply = re.sub(r'<think>[\s\S]*?</think>', '', reply).strip()
            
            if source == 'voice': execute_audio_playback(reply)
            return jsonify({"response": reply, "type": "browser", "model": "hermes-harness", "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})
        except Exception as e:
            return jsonify({"response": f"Hermes processing anomaly: {e}", "type": "browser", "model": "hermes-harness", "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})

    # 💻 CASE C: SURGICAL CODING AGENT ROUTING
    elif should_trigger_coding_agent(command):
        print(f"🛠️ Detecting development requirements. Activating Coding Agent -> {CODING_MODEL}")
        coding_instructions = "You are the Core Software Engineering Agent of the Advanced Cognitive Engine. Provide optimal programming blocks. Keep explanations brief."
        try:
            response = ollama.chat(model=CODING_MODEL, messages=[{"role": "system", "content": coding_instructions}, {"role": "user", "content": command}])
            reply = response['message']['content']
            if source == 'voice': execute_audio_playback("Code architecture compiled successfully. Dropping snippets into viewports.")
            return jsonify({"response": reply, "type": "coding", "model": CODING_MODEL, "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})
        except Exception as e:
            return jsonify({"response": f"Coding pipeline dropped: {e}", "type": "coding", "model": CODING_MODEL, "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})

    # ⚡ CASE D: SNAPPY CONVERSATIONAL ROUTATION
    else:
        print(f"⚡ Pacing layer optimally -> routing conversational query through {FAST_MODEL}")
        messages_payload = [
            {"role": "system", "content": "You are Ace, an elite Advanced Cognitive Engine desktop assistant for Aryan. Speak with a witty cadence like Jarvis. Keep responses strictly limited to 1 or 2 sentences maximum."}
        ]
        messages_payload.extend(chat_history)
        messages_payload.append({"role": "user", "content": command})

        try:
            response = ollama.chat(model=FAST_MODEL, messages=messages_payload)
            reply = response['message']['content']
            
            chat_history.append({"role": "user", "content": command})
            chat_history.append({"role": "assistant", "content": reply})
            if len(chat_history) > 20: chat_history = chat_history[-20:]
            context_string = f"{len(chat_history)}/20 SLOTS"

            if source == 'voice': execute_audio_playback(reply)
            return jsonify({"response": reply, "type": "standard", "model": FAST_MODEL, "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})
        except Exception as e:
            return jsonify({"response": f"Conversational pipeline dropped: {e}", "type": "standard", "model": FAST_MODEL, "interaction_count": interaction_session_counter, "context_loaded": context_string, "execution_time": round(time.time() - start_time, 2)})

if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(host='0.0.0.0', port=5000, debug=False)
